 <hr>
  <h3 align="center">Kabyle Bible: Luke</h3> 
 <p><a name="an_1:1">1:1</a> Imi aṭas i gebdan tira ɣef wayen yedṛan gar-aneɣ, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:2">1:2</a> akken i ɣ-t-id ɛawden wid yellan d inigan si tazwara, iwalan kullec s wallen-nsen ; uɣalen d iqeddacen n wawal n Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:3">1:3</a> Steqsaɣ ula d nekk akken ilaq ɣef wayen akk yedṛan seg wass amezwaru, ufiɣ d ayen yelhan a k-t-id aruɣ a Tawfilus,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:4">1:4</a> iwakken aț-țissineḍ tideț ɣef wayen i tesliḍ meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:5">1:5</a> Di zzman n Hiṛudus, agellid n tmurt n Yahuda, yella yiwen n lmuqeddem si tejmaɛt n Abya, isem-is Zakarya. Tameṭṭut-is Ilicaba, seg izuṛan n Haṛun.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:6">1:6</a> D iḥeqqiyen i llan i sin, ḥerzen yerna ḍuɛen awal n Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:7">1:7</a> Ur sɛin ara dderya, meqqṛit i sin di leɛmeṛ yerna Ilicaba ț-țiɛiqeṛt.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:8">1:8</a> Mi d-tewweḍ nnuba n leqdic n wedrum n Zakarya di lǧameɛ iqedsen </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:9">1:9</a> akken i tella di lɛadda n lmuqedmin, gren tasɣaṛt, tṣaḥ-ed Zakarya iwakken ad ikcem ɣer wemkan iqedsen ad isseṛɣ lebxuṛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:10">1:10</a> Mi gella isseṛɣay lebxuṛ di lǧameɛ, lɣaci meṛṛa yeqqimen di beṛṛa deɛɛun ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:11">1:11</a> Iḍheṛ-as-d yiwen lmelk n Sidi Ṛebbi, ibedd ɣer tama tayeffust n udekkan-nni anda sseṛɣayen lebxuṛ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:12">1:12</a> Mi t-iwala Zakarya, yedhec ikcem-it lxuf. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:13">1:13</a> Lmelk-nni yenna yas -ed : Ur țțagad ara a Zakarya, ayen i tessutreḍ ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi yețwaqbel. Tameṭṭut-ik Ilicaba ad a k-d-tesɛu aqcic, a s-tsemmiḍ Yeḥya.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:14">1:14</a> Aț-țfeṛḥeḍ yis, a k-yili d sebba n sseɛd ; imdanen meṛṛa ad feṛḥen s tlalit-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:15">1:15</a> Ad yesɛu ccan d ameqqran ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi, a d-iččaṛ d Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen si tɛebbuṭ n yemma-s, ur itess ccṛab, ur itess ayen nniḍen isekkṛen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:16">1:16</a> A d-yerr aṭas n wat Isṛail ɣer webrid n Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:17">1:17</a> Ad ilḥu s leɛnaya n Sidi Ṛebbi, s ṛṛuḥ ț-țezmert n nnbi Ilyas. Ad issemlil imawlan d warraw-nsen, a d-yerr wid ijehlen ɣer webrid n iḥeqqiyen, akken ad iheggi i Sidi Ṛebbi agdud ara t-iḍuɛen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:18">1:18</a> Zakarya yenna i lmelk : Amek ara ɛeqleɣ belli ayen akka i d-tenniḍ ț-țideț ? Nekk d amɣaṛ, ula ț-țameṭṭut-iw meqqṛet di leɛmeṛ !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:19">1:19</a> Lmelk-nni yerra-yas-d : Nekk d Jebrayil, d aqeddac n Sidi Ṛebbi ; usiɣ-ed s ɣuṛ-es iwakken a k-d-awiɣ lexbaṛ-agi n lxiṛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:20">1:20</a> Lameɛna imi ur tumineḍ ara s yimeslayen-iw atan aț-țeggugmeḍ, ur d-ițeffeɣ ara wawal seg yimi-k alamma d asmi ara d-yedṛu wannect-agi. Meɛna ḥṣu belli ayen akka i k-d-nniɣ ad yedṛu deg wass-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:21">1:21</a> Lɣaci-nni yețṛaǧun Zakarya deg ufrag, wehmen acuɣeṛ iɛeṭṭel deg umkan iqedsen n lǧameɛ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:22">1:22</a> Mi d-iffeɣ, yeggugem, ur izmir ara a d-yessufeɣ awal ; lɣaci-nni fehmen belli iweḥḥa-yas-ed kra Sidi Ṛebbi. Yebda ițwehhi-yasen-d s ifassen-is, yeqqim d agugam.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:23">1:23</a> Mi kfan wussan n lxedma-s di lǧameɛ, Zakarya yuɣal ɣer wexxam-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:24">1:24</a> Ɛeddan kra n wussan, tameṭṭut-is Ilicaba terfed tadist ; dɣa tesseḥjeb iman-is xemsa wagguren, teqqaṛ :   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:25">1:25</a> Atan Sidi Ṛebbi yerra-d ddehn-is ɣuṛ-i, ikkes-iyi lɛib zdat yemdanen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:26">1:26</a> Aggur wis sețța, Sidi Ṛebbi iceggeɛ-d lmelk Jebrayil ɣer taddart n Naṣaret, di tmurt n Jlili.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:27">1:27</a> Iceggeɛ-it-id ɣer yiwet n tlemẓit i gexḍeb yiwen wergaz isem-is Yusef, yellan seg izuṛan n Sidna Dawed. Tilemẓit-agi isem-is Meryem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:28">1:28</a> Ikcem lmelk ɣuṛ-es yenna-yas : Sslam fell-am a tin iburek Sidi Ṛebbi ! Sidi Ṛebbi yella yid-em.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:29">1:29</a> Meryem tedhec, tenna : D acu i d lmeɛna n imeslayen agi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:30">1:30</a> Lmelk yenna-yas : Ur țțaggad ara a Meryem ! S ṛṛeḥma-s tameqqrant, Sidi Ṛebbi yextaṛ-ikem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:31">1:31</a> Atan aț-țrefdeḍ tadist, a d-tesɛuḍ aqcic, semmi-yas Ɛisa, (yeɛni : « Amsellek »)  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:32">1:32</a> Ad yesɛu ccan d ameqqran, ad ițțusemmi Mmi-s n Sidi Ṛebbi ɛlayen. Sidi Ṛebbi a t-yerr d agellid akken i t-yella Sidna Dawed, yiwen si lejdud-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:33">1:33</a> Ad iḥkem ɣef tarwa n Yeɛqub i dayem, tageldit-is ur tfennu ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:34">1:34</a> Meryem tenna i lmelk-nni : Amek ara d-idṛu yid-i wayagi nekk ur nezwiǧ ara ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:35">1:35</a> Lmelk yerra-yas : Atan a d-yers fell-am Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen ; tazmert n Sidi Ṛebbi ɛlayen a kem-tɣumm am tili, daymi aqcic-agi imqeddes ara d-ilalen ad ițțsemmi « Mmi-s n Ṛebbi ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:36">1:36</a> Ilicaba i m-ițțilin, ula d nețțat ațan s tadist a d-tesɛu aqcic ɣas akken meqqṛet di leɛmeṛ. Tin akken iwumi semman tiɛiqeṛt, ațan deg waggur wis sețța, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:37">1:37</a> imi ulac wayen iwumi ur izmir Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:38">1:38</a> Meryem tenna : Aql-i ț-țaqeddact n Sidi Ṛebbi, ad idṛu yid-i wayen i d-tenniḍ. Imiren Lmelk-nni yeǧǧa-ț, iṛuḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:39">1:39</a> Deg wussan-nni, Meryem tekker tṛuḥ s lemɣawla ɣer yiwet n taddart yellan deg idurar n tmurt n Yahuda.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:40">1:40</a> Tekcem ɣer wexxam n Zakarya, tsellem ɣef Ilicaba. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:41">1:41</a> Akken i tesla Ilicaba i sslam n Meryem, yefrawes llufan yellan di tɛebbuṭ-is ; imiren teččuṛ d Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:42">1:42</a> tɛeggeḍ tenna : A Meryem, tețțubarkeḍ ger tilawin meṛṛa, ițțubarek daɣen win yellan di tɛebbuṭ-im. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:43">1:43</a> D acu-yi, iwakken a d-terzef ɣuṛ-i yemma-s n Ssid-iw ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:44">1:44</a> Akken kan i sliɣ i sslam-im, llufan yellan di tɛebbuṭ-iw yefrawes s lfeṛḥ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:45">1:45</a> ?-țaseɛdit kemm yumnen s wayen i m-d-yenna Sidi Ṛebbi !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:46">1:46</a> Meryem tenna : Taṛwiḥt-iw teḥmed Sidi Ṛebbi,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:47">1:47</a> ul-iw yeččuṛ d lfeṛḥ imi d nețța i d amsellek-iw,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:48">1:48</a> axaṭer iwala-yi-d nekk taqeddact-is tameɣbunt ur nesɛi azal. Sya d asawen si lǧil ɣer lǧil a yi-qqaṛen : « ț-țaseɛdit »,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:49">1:49</a> imi Sidi Ṛebbi Bab n tezmert, yexdem yis-i ayen issewhamen. Isem-is d imqeddes.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:50">1:50</a>  Ṛṛeḥma-s tețdum si lǧil ɣer lǧil  ɣef wid akk i t-iḍuɛen.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:51">1:51</a> Isken-ed tazmert n yiɣil-is, isseɛṛeq iberdan i wid yețzuxxun ;  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:52">1:52</a>  yessers-ed imeqqranen seg imukan  eɛlayen, yerfed wid yețwaḥeqṛen  ;   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:53">1:53</a>  yesseṛwa-yasen leṛẓaq i wid   yelluẓen, ma d imeṛkantiyen yerra-ten  ifassen d ilmawen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:54">1:54</a>  Isellek tarwa n wat Isṛail   yellan d iqeddacen-is,  ur ițțu ara Ṛṛeḥma-s,   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:55">1:55</a> i gewɛed i Sidna Ibṛahim d warraw-is i dayem akken i t-yenna i lejdud-nneɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:56">1:56</a> Meryem teqqim ɣer Ilicaba azal n tlata wagguren d wamek i tuɣal ɣer taddart-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:57">1:57</a> Yewweḍ-ed lweqt i deg ara d-tarew Ilicaba, tesɛa-d aqcic.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:58">1:58</a> Imawlan-is d lǧiran-is feṛḥen aṭas mi slan s ṛṛehma i d-issers fell-as Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:59">1:59</a> Mi wwḍen tmanya n wussan ɣef weqcic-nni, usan-d a s-sḍehṛen, bɣan a s-semmin s yisem n baba-s : Zakarya. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:60">1:60</a> Dɣa tenṭeq-ed yemma-s tenna-yasen : Xaṭi ! A s-nsemmi Yeḥya !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:61">1:61</a> Nnan-as : Ula d yiwen deg wedrum-nwen ur yesɛi isem-agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:62">1:62</a> Steqsan baba-s s uwehhi amek yebɣa ad isemmi i mmi-s. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:63">1:63</a> Issuter asen-d talwiḥt, yura-yasen-d deg-s : « Yeḥya i d isem-is ». Dɣa wehmen meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:64">1:64</a> Imiren kan iserreḥ yiles-is, yebda iheddeṛ, yețḥemmid Ṛebbi ițcekkiṛ-it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:65">1:65</a> Imezdaɣ n lǧiha-nni meṛṛa wehmen, tɛeǧǧben. Deg idurar n tmurt n Yahuda țmeslayen akk ɣef wayen yedṛan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:66">1:66</a> Wid akk yeslan imeslayen-nni, ḥerzen-ten deg wulawen-nsen, qqaṛen : d acu ara d-iffeɣ weqcic-agi ? Axaṭer s tideț afus n Sidi Ṛebbi yella fell-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:67">1:67</a> Zakarya, baba-s n weqcic-nni, iččuṛ d Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen, icar-ed s imeslayen-agi :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:68">1:68</a> Ad ițțubarek Sidi Ṛebbi, Illu n wat Isṛail imi d-yerra ddehn-is ɣer wegdud-is iwakken a t-isellek.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:69">1:69</a> Yefka-yaɣ-d yiwen wemsellek d ameqqran seg izuṛan n Sidna Dawed aqeddac-is,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:70">1:70</a> am akken i t-id-ixebbeṛ Sidi Ṛebbi si zzman iɛeddan, seg yimi n lenbiya iqedsen :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:71">1:71</a> Ad yili d amsellek ara ɣ-imenɛen seg yiɛdawen-nneɣ, si ger ifassen n wid akk i ɣ-ikeṛhen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:72">1:72</a> Isbeggen ṛṛeḥma-s i lejdud-nneɣ, yemmekta-d lemɛahda-s iqedsen  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:73">1:73</a> i gefka i jeddi-tneɣ Sidna Ibṛahim.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:74">1:74</a> M'ara nețțusellek seg ufus n yeɛdawen-nneɣ, a neɛbed Sidi Ṛebbi mbla lxuf,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:75">1:75</a> s lḥeqq, s ṭṭaɛa d wannuz deg wussan n ddunit-nneɣ meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:76">1:76</a> Ma d kečč a mmi, aț-țețțusemmiḍ d nnbi n Sidi Ṛebbi eɛlayen axaṭer aț-țedduḍ zdat-es iwakken aț-țheggiḍ iberdan-is,   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:77">1:77</a> aț-țesfehmeḍ agdud-is ɣef leslak n Sidi Ṛebbi s leɛfu n ddnubat-nsen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:78">1:78</a> Axaṭer Ṛebbi-nneɣ d aḥnin, s Ṛṛeḥma-ines a d-icṛeq fell-aɣ tafat-is am tin n yiṭij seg yigenwan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:79">1:79</a>  Tafat-is a d-tecṛeq ɣef wid yellan di ṭṭlam n lmut, ad aɣ-yawi deg webrid n lehna.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:80">1:80</a> Aqcic-nni ițțimɣuṛ yețnerni di leɛqel. Iɛac deg unezṛuf armi d ass i deg i d-ibeggen iman-is i wat Isṛail.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:1">2:1</a> Deg ussan-nni, yeffeɣ-ed yiwen n lqanun s ɣuṛ Qayṣeṛ ameqqran ; yefka lameṛ ad țțujerrden imezdaɣ meṛṛa yellan di tmura-ines.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:2">2:2</a> Ajerred-agi amezwaru yedṛa asmi yella Kirinyus d lḥakem n tmurt n Surya. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:3">2:3</a> Imdanen meṛṛa ṛuḥen ad țțujerden mkul yiwen di taddart n lejdud-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:4">2:4</a> Yusef yellan seg izuṛan n Sidna Dawed, yuli ula d nețța si taddart n Naṣaret n tmurt n Jlili ɣer Bitelḥem, taddart n lejdud-is yellan di tmurt n Yahuda.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:5">2:5</a> Iṛuḥ ad ițțujerred nețța ț-țxedibt-is Meryem yellan s tadist.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:6">2:6</a> Mi ten-yuɣ lḥal dinna, yewweḍ-d lweqt i deg ara terbu ( tarew ) Meryem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:7">2:7</a> Tesɛa-d mmi-s amenzu, tețțel-it, tessegen-it di lmedwed, imi ur ufin ara amkan deg wexxam n yemsafren.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:8">2:8</a> Di tmurt-nni, llan imeksawen ițnusun di lexlawi, țɛassan lmal-nsen deg yiḍ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:9">2:9</a> Ataya lmelk n Sidi Ṛebbi iḍheṛ-asen-d, tamanegt n Sidi Ṛebbi tecceɛceɛ tezzi-yasen-d, ikcem-iten lxuf d ameqqran.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:10">2:10</a> Lmelk yenna-yasen : Ur țțagadet ! Aql-i wwiɣ-awen-d lexbaṛ lxiṛ ara isfeṛḥen wugdud meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:11">2:11</a> Ass-agi di taddart n Sidna Dawed, ilul-awen-d yiwen wemsellek, d nețța i d Lmasiḥ n Sidi Ṛebbi !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:12">2:12</a> Atan wamek ara t-tɛeqlem : aț-țafem llufan yețțel, yeṭṭes di lmedwed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:13">2:13</a> Imiren kan, ț-țirebbaɛ n lmalayekkat i d-yernan ɣer lmelk nni, cennunt țḥemmident Sidi Ṛebbi, qqaṛent :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:14">2:14</a> Lḥemd i Sidi Ṛebbi deg imukan eɛlayen, lehna di ddunit ɣef yemdanen eɛzizen fell-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:15">2:15</a> Akken uɣalent lmalayekkat-nni ɣer yigenni, imeksawen nnan wway gar-asen : Kkret a nṛuḥet ɣer Bitelḥem, a nẓer ayen i gedṛan, d wayen akka s wayes i ɣ-d-ixebbeṛ Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:16">2:16</a> Imiren kan ṛuḥen, ufan dinna Meryem d Yusef akk-d llufan-nni yeṭṭes di lmedwed.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:17">2:17</a> Mi walan aqcic-nni, ḥkan-d wayen i sen-d-yenna lmelk fell-as. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:18">2:18</a> Wid akk yeslan s wayen i d-ḥkan imeksawen-nni, dehcen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:19">2:19</a> Meryem teḥrez imeslayen-nni deg wul-is, tețxemmim fell-asen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:20">2:20</a> Mi uɣalen imeksawen-nni, țḥemmiden țcekkiṛen Sidi Ṛebbi ɣef wayen slan d wayen ẓran, imi ufan kullec akken i sen-d-ițțuxebbeṛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:21">2:21</a> Yewweḍ-ed wass wis tmanya i deg ara s-sḍehṛen i weqcic-nni ; semman-as Ɛisa, isem-nni i s-yefka lmelk uqbel ad yili di tɛebbuṭ n yemma-s.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:22">2:22</a> Asmi wwḍen ṛebɛin wussan ɣef tlalit n weqcic-nni, Yusef d Meryem wwin-t ɣer temdint n Lquds iwakken ad ițțuqeddem i Sidi Ṛebbi, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:23">2:23</a> akken yura di ccariɛa n Sidna Musa :  yal aqcic amenzu, ilaq ad ițțuqeddem i Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:24">2:24</a> Yerna ṛuḥen iwakken ad fken d asfel   snat n tmilliwin neɣ sin yetbiren imeẓyanen akken yella di ccariɛa n Sidna Musa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:25">2:25</a> Di temdint n Lquds yella yiwen wergaz isem-is Semɛun. Argaz-agi d aḥeqqi, iḍuɛ Sidi Ṛebbi, yețṛaǧu amsellek n wat Isṛail, Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen yețțili yid-es. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:26">2:26</a> Iweḥḥa-yas-ed belli ur ițmețțat ara alamma yeẓra Lmasiḥ n Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:27">2:27</a> Ṛṛuḥ n Sidi Ṛebbi iwelleh Semɛun ad iṛuḥ ɣer lǧameɛ iqedsen.Atnaya kecmen-d Yusef d Meryem, wwin-d llufan-nni iwakken ad xedmen wayen i d-tenna ccariɛa n Musa fell-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:28">2:28</a> Semɛun yeṭṭef aqcic-nni ger ifassen-is, iḥmed Sidi Ṛebbi yenna :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:29">2:29</a> Tura a Sidi Ṛebbi ɣas ad mmteɣ aql-i di lehna imi amsellek i ɣ-tweɛdeḍ, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:30">2:30</a> yewweḍ-ed yerna walaɣ-t s wallen-iw :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:31">2:31</a> win akken i theggaḍ i leǧnas meṛṛa,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:32">2:32</a> d nețța ara yessalin ccan n wat Isṛail agdud-ik,  ara yilin ț-țafat ara d-icceɛceɛen ula ɣef leǧnas nniḍen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:33">2:33</a> Baba-s d yemma-s n weqcic-nni tɛeǧǧben ɣef wayen i d-qqaṛen fell-as. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:34">2:34</a> Semɛun iburek-iten, yenna i Meryem, yemma-s n weqcic-nni : Atan weqcic-agi ad yili i kra seg wat Isṛail d sebba n tuccḍa, ma d wiyaḍ a ten-id-yerr ɣer webrid. ?ef ddemma-s ara yili lxilaf ger yemdanen ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:35">2:35</a> s wakka ara d-banen ixemmimen n diri deg wulawen, ma d kemm aț-țejreḥ tasa-m, am akken tețwet s ujenwi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:36">2:36</a> Tella daɣen yiwet n tmeṭṭut isem-is ?anna, meqqṛet di leɛmeṛ, ula d nețțat si lenbiya, d yelli-s n Fanwil n wedrum n Azir. Seg wasmi i tedda ț-țislit, tɛac d wergaz is sebɛa n yiseggasen </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:37">2:37</a> dɣa teǧǧel. Di leɛmeṛ-is ṛebɛa utmanyin n yiseggasen. Am yiḍ am ass ur teṭṭixiṛ si lǧameɛ iqedsen, tɛebbed Sidi Ṛebbi, tețțuẓum, tețẓalla. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:38">2:38</a> Ula d nețțat tewweḍ-ed di teswiɛt-nni, teḥmed Sidi Ṛebbi, theddeṛ ɣef weqcic-nni i wid akk yețṛaǧun leslak n temdint n Lquds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:39">2:39</a> Mi fukken imawlan n Ɛisa ayen akk i d-tenna ccariɛa n Sidi Ṛebbi, uɣalen ɣer taddart-nsen Naṣaret yellan di tmurt n Jlili. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:40">2:40</a> Aqcic-nni yețțimɣuṛ yețnerni di tmusni, lbaṛaka n Sidi Ṛebbi tella fell-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:41">2:41</a> Imawlan n Sidna Ɛisa țṛuḥun mkul aseggas ɣer temdint n Lquds iwakken ad sɛeddin Tafaska  n izimer n leslak. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:42">2:42</a> Asmi yesɛa Ɛisa tnac yiseggasen, yedda akk-d imawlan-is ɣer temdint n Lquds, akken tella di lɛadda n lɛid.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:43">2:43</a> Mi tɛedda Tafaska,  lɣaci țțuɣalen ɣer yexxamen-nsen, ma d Ɛisa yeqqim di temdint Lquds, imawlan-is ur d-wwin ara s lexbaṛ, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:44">2:44</a> ɣilen yedda-d ț-țerbaɛt nniḍen. Lḥan ass kamel dɣa bdan țqelliben fell-as. Steqsan wid akk i sen-yețțilin d wid meṛṛa ssnen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:45">2:45</a> lameɛna ur t-ufin ara. Uɣalen ɣer temdint n Lquds iwakken ad qellben fell-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:46">2:46</a> Ass wis tlata, ufan-t di lǧameɛ iqedsen yeqqim ger lecyux, ismeḥsis asen, isteqsay-iten. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:47">2:47</a> Wid akk i s isellen wehmen di lefhama-s d wayen i d-ițarra i yesteqsiyen-nsen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:48">2:48</a> Mi t-walan imawlan-is, qqimen wehmen, dɣa tenna-yas yemma-s : A mmi, acuɣeṛ i ɣ-txedmeḍ akka ? Nekk d baba-k neṛwa aḥebbeṛ, acḥal i nqelleb fell-ak !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:49">2:49</a> Nețța yenna-yasen : Acuɣeṛ i tețqellibem fell-i ? Eɛni ur teẓrim ara ilaq-iyi ad xedmeɣ lecɣal n baba ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:50">2:50</a> Lameɛna nutni ur fhimen ara ayen i sen-d-yenna. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:51">2:51</a> Ɛisa yedda d imawlan-is ɣer temdint n Naṣaret, yețțaɣ-asen awal. Yemma-s teḥrez annect-agi meṛṛa deg wul-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:52">2:52</a> Ɛisa ițțimɣuṛ, yetɛeqqil ; eɛziz ɣer Ṛebbi, eɛziz ɣer yemdanen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:1">3:1</a> Deg wuseggas wis xemseṭṭac n tgeldit n Qayṣer Tibeṛyus, llan ṛebɛa lḥekkam di tmurt n Falisṭin. Bunṭus Bilaṭus d lḥakem n tmurt n Yahuda, Hiṛudus Antifas yeḥkem ɣef tmurt n Jlili, Filbas gma-s n Hiṛudus, ɣef tmura n Iturya akk-d Tṛaxunit, ma d Lisanyas yeḥkem ɣef tmurt n Abilan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:2">3:2</a> Di lweqt-nni, ?ennan akk-d Qayif llan d lmuqedmin imeqqranen. Awal n Sidi Ṛebbi ițwaxebbeṛ-as-ed i Yeḥya, mmi-s n Zakarya, deg unezṛuf.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:3">3:3</a> Iṛuḥ ițnadi timura i d-izzin i wasif n Urdun, yețberriḥ yeqqaṛ : Beddlet tikli, uɣalet-ed ɣer webrid, aset-ed aț-țețwaɣeḍsem iwakken Sidi Ṛebbi a wen-isemmeḥ ddnubat-nwen !   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:4">3:4</a> Akken i d-ițțuxebeṛ di tektabt n nnbi Iceɛya :  ?-țaɣect n win ițɛeggiḍen deg wunezṛuf : Heggit abrid n Sidi Ṛebbi, ssemsawit iberdan-is !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:5">3:5</a>  Iɣezṛan, idurar ț-țɣaltin ad uɣalen d izuɣaṛ !  Iberdan iɛewjen ad țțuseggmen,  wid ixesṛen ad qeɛden .  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:6">3:6</a>  Imdanen meṛṛa ad ẓren leslak n Sidi Ṛebbi.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:7">3:7</a> Yeḥya yeqqaṛ i lɣaci i d-ițțasen iwakken ad țwaɣeḍsen deg waman : A ccetla n yizerman, anwa i kkun-isfaqen belli tzemrem aț- țrewlem i lɛiqab i d-iteddun ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:8">3:8</a> Deg wayen akk txeddmem, sbeggnet-ed belli ṣfan wulawen nwen ! Ur qqaṛet ara kan deg yiman-nwen : jeddi-tneɣ d Sidna Ibṛahim, axaṭer a wen-iniɣ : seg idɣaɣen-agi, Sidi Ṛebbi yezmer a d-issufeɣ dderya i Ibṛahim.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:9">3:9</a> Ațan ihi tcaquṛt thegga ɣer izuṛan n ttjuṛ, yal ttejṛa ur d-nețțak ara lfakya lɛali, aț-țețwagzem, aț-țețwaḍeggeṛ ɣer tmes.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:10">3:10</a> Lɣaci steqsan-t nnan-as : D acu i ɣ-ilaqen a t-nexdem ihi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:11">3:11</a> Yerra-yasen : Win yesɛan sin iqendyaṛ ad yefk yiwen i win ur nesɛi ara ; win yesɛan ayen ara yečč, ad yefk i win ur nesɛi ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:12">3:12</a> Usan-d ula d imekkasen itețțen ayla n medden iwakken ad țwaɣeḍsen deg wasif, nnan-as : A Sidi, i nukkni yellan d imekkasen n tebzert ( leɣṛama ) d acu ara nexdem ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:13">3:13</a> Yenna-yasen : Ur țnadit ara sennig wayen i d-yenna lqanun.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:14">3:14</a> Iɛeskṛiwen daɣen steqsan-t : I nukkni, d acu ara nexdem ? Yerra-yasen : Ur xeddmet ara lbaṭel, ur țțaṭṭafet ara tajɛelt, setqenɛet kan s lexlaṣ nwen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:15">3:15</a> Yuɣ lḥal lɣaci meṛṛa llan țṛaǧun qqaṛen deg ulawen-nsen : Ahat d nețța i d Lmasiḥ !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:16">3:16</a> Yeḥya yenna-yasen : Nekk sseɣḍaseɣ-kkun deg waman, meɛna a d-yas win yesɛan tazmert akteṛ-iw ; ur uklaleɣ ara ad fsiɣ ula d lexyuḍ n warkasen-is. Nețța a kkun-isseɣḍes s Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen ț-țmes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:17">3:17</a> Yeṭṭef tazzart deg wufus-is, ad yessizdeg tirect deg wennar-is, a d-ijmeɛ irden ɣer yikufan, ma d alim a t-isseṛɣ di tmes ur nxețți. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:18">3:18</a> Yeḥya ițbecciṛ i lɣaci lexbaṛ n lxiṛ, inehhu-ten s waṭas n yimeslayen nniḍen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:19">3:19</a> Yesseḍlem ula d agellid Hiṛudus, yeqqaṛ-as : mačči d lḥeqq fell-ak aț-țaɣeḍ Hiṛudyad tameṭṭut n gma-k ! Ilumm-it daɣen ɣef lecɣal nniḍen n diri i gxeddem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:20">3:20</a> Hiṛudus ikemmel di txeṣṣarin-is, yessekcem Yeḥya ɣer lḥebs !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:21">3:21</a> Mi țwaɣeḍsen lɣaci deg waman, Sidna Ɛisa yețwaɣḍes ula d nețța. Akken i gdeɛɛu ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi, igenni yeldi-d, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:22">3:22</a> Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen yers-ed fell-as s ṣṣifa icuban titbirt. Yiwet n taɣect tekka-d seg yigenni tenna-d : Kečč, d mmi eɛzizen, deg-k i gella lfeṛḥ-iw.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:23">3:23</a> Mi gebda Sidna Ɛisa aselmed, ad yili yesɛa tlatin iseggasen di leɛmeṛ-is. ?er yemdanen yella : d mmi-s n Yusef atnan lejdud-is : Heli, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:24">3:24</a> Matta, Lewwi, Melki, Yennay, Yusef, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:25">3:25</a> Matatya, Ɛamus, Naḥun, ?esli, Naggay, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:26">3:26</a> Maḥat, Matatya, Camɛi, Yusef, Yuda, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:27">3:27</a> Yuḥanan, Rica, Zurubabil, Calatyel, Niri, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:28">3:28</a> Melki, Addi, Qusam, Elmudan, Ɛir, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:29">3:29</a> Yusa, Elyazer, Yurim, Matta, Lewwi, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:30">3:30</a> Semɛun, Yahuda, Yusef, Yuna, Elyaqim, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:31">3:31</a> Melya, Menna, Mattata, Natan, Dawed, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:32">3:32</a> Yassa, Ɛubed, Buɛaz, Salmun, Naḥsun, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:33">3:33</a> Ɛaminadab, Admin, Aram, ?esṛun, Fares, Yahuda, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:34">3:34</a> Yeɛqub, Isḥaq, Ibṛahim, Teraḥ, Naḥur, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:35">3:35</a> Saruǧ, Raɛu, Faleǧ, Ɛaber, Salaḥ, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:36">3:36</a> Kenan, Arfaksad, Cam, Nuḥ, Lamek,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:37">3:37</a> Matusalaḥ, ?anux, Yared, Mahalalyel, Kenam, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:38">3:38</a> Inuc, Cit, Adem illan d mmi-s n Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:1">4:1</a> Mi d- yuɣal Sidna Ɛisa seg wasif n Urdun, Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen yewwi-t ɣer unezṛuf. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:2">4:2</a> Ṛebɛin wussan ur yečči, Cciṭan yețjeṛṛib deg-s. Mi ɛeddan wussan-nni, yuɣal illuẓ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:3">4:3</a> Cciṭan yenna-yas : Ma d Mmi-s n Ṛebbi i telliḍ, ini-yas i wedɣaɣ-agi a d-yuɣal d aɣṛum.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:4">4:4</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Yura di tektabt iqedsen :  amdan ur yețɛic ara s weɣṛum kan meɛna s mkul awal i d-ițțasen s ɣuṛ Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:5">4:5</a> Yuɣal Cciṭan yewwi-t ɣer yiwen wemkan eɛlayen, deg yiwet n teswiɛt yesken-as-ed akk tigeldiwin n ddunit, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:6">4:6</a> yenna-yas : Ad a k-d-fkeɣ lḥekma d ccan n ddewlat-agi meṛṛa, axaṭer țțunefkent iyi-d. Zemreɣ a tent-fkeɣ i win i yi-ihwan ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:7">4:7</a> ma tseǧǧdeḍ zdat-i ad uɣalent akk d ayla-k.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:8">4:8</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Yura :  Anagar Sidi Ṛebbi Illu-inek ara tɛebdeḍ, i nețța kan iwumi ara tseǧǧdeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:9">4:9</a> Cciṭan yewwi-t daɣen ɣer temdint n Lquds, yessers-it ɣef yixef n lǧameɛ iqedsen, yenna-yas : Ma d Mmi-s n Ṛebbi i telliḍ, ḍeggeṛ iman-ik d akessar, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:10">4:10</a> axaṭer yura :  Ad yefk lameṛ i lmalayekkat-is iwakken ad ḥarbent fell-ak,  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:11">4:11</a> yerna a k-awint ger ifassen-nsent, ad ḥadrent iḍaṛṛen-ik ɣef wedɣaɣ.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:12">4:12</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Yura daɣen :  Ur țjeṛṛib ara Sidi Ṛebbi, Illu-inek.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:13">4:13</a> Mi i t-ijeṛṛeb s waṭas n tḥila ur s-yufi ara abrid, Iblis yeṭṭaxeṛ fell-as alamma ț-țikkelt nniḍen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:14">4:14</a> Sidna Ɛisa yuɣal ɣer tmurt n Jlili yeččuṛ ț-țazmert n Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen, slan yis di mkul tama n tmurt-agi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:15">4:15</a> Ikeččem ɣer leǧwameɛ n wat Isṛail yesselmad, imdanen meṛṛa țcekkiṛen-t. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:16">4:16</a> Iṛuḥ ɣer taddart n Naṣaret anda yețțuṛebba ; akken innum, ikcem ɣer lǧameɛ deg wass n westeɛfu. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:17">4:17</a> Mi gekker a d-iɣeṛ, fkan-as-d taktabt n nnbi Iceɛya, yeldi-ț, yufa amkan anda yura :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:18">4:18</a>  Ṛṛuḥ n Sidi Ṛebbi yers-ed fell-i, axaṭer yextaṛ-iyi iwakken ad beccṛeɣ lexbaṛ n lxiṛ i yimeɣban, ad beccṛeɣ i yimeḥbas tilelli, iwakken a d-rreɣ iẓri i yiderɣalen , a d kkseɣ lḥif ɣef wid ițwaḍelmen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:19">4:19</a>  ad beccṛeɣ ɣef wuseggas i deg ara d-issers Sidi Ṛebbi ṛṛeḥma ines .  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:20">4:20</a> Ijmeɛ taktabt-nni, yerra-ț i uqeddac, imiren yeqqim. Wid akk yellan di lǧameɛ ččan-t s wallen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:21">4:21</a> Dɣa yenna-yasen : Ayen i wen-d-ɣṛiɣ akka, atan yedṛa-d gar-awen ass-agi !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:22">4:22</a> Wehmen atas, tɛeǧǧben deg yimeslayen i d-ițeffɣen seg yimi-s, qqaṛen : Amek ? Mačči d mmi-s n Yusef wagi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:23">4:23</a> Dɣa yenna-yasen : ?riɣ belli a yi-d-tinim lemtel-agi : « A ṭṭbib sseḥlu iman-ik,» neɣ « xdem dagi di tmurt-ik ayen i nesla txedmeḍ-t di temdint n Kafernaḥum.»  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:24">4:24</a> Yenna-yasen daɣen : S tideț a wen-iniɣ : ulac nnbi yețwaqeblen di tmurt-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:25">4:25</a> A wen-iniɣ tideț : Di zzman n nnbi Ilyas, tlata yiseggasen d wezgen ur d-tewwit lehwa dɣa yeɣli-d laẓ d ameqqran ɣef tmurt meṛṛa. Deg wussan-nni, aṭas n tuǧǧal i gellan di tmurt n wat Isṛail. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:26">4:26</a> ?as akken, Sidi Ṛebbi ur iceggeɛ ara nnbi Ilyas ɣer yiwet deg-sent, anagar ɣ er yiwet n taǧǧalt yellan di taddart n ?urfat di tmurt n Sidun . </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:27">4:27</a> Llan daɣen aṭas n wid ihelken lbeṛs di tmurt n wat Isṛail di zzman n nnbi Ilyaceɛ , meɛna ula d yiwen deg-sen ur iḥli anagar Neɛman n tmurt n Surya.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:28">4:28</a> Mi slan imeslayen-agi, lɣaci meṛṛa yellan di lǧameɛ yenɣa-ten lɣecc. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:29">4:29</a> Kkren ɣuṛ-es, ssufɣen-t si taddart, ssawḍen-t armi d ixef n wedrar i ɣef tebna taddart-nsen iwakken a t-ssegrirben d akessar ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:30">4:30</a> lameɛna nețța iɛedda gar-asen, iṛuḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:31">4:31</a> Sidna Ɛisa iṣubb ɣer tamdint n Kafernaḥum, illan n at Jlili, anda yesselmad lɣaci deg wass n westeɛfu. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:32">4:32</a> Imdanen wehmen aṭas deg wuselmed-ines axaṭer imeslayen-is sɛan tissas.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:33">4:33</a> Di lǧameɛ, yella yiwen wergaz izdeɣ-it uṛuḥani, iɛeggeḍ s lǧehd n taɣect-is :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:34">4:34</a> D acu i tebɣiḍ ɣuṛ-nneɣ a Ɛisa Anaṣari ? Tusiḍ-ed iwakken ad aɣ tesnegreḍ ? ?riɣ d acu-k , kečč d Imqeddes n Ṛebbi !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:35">4:35</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenṭeq ɣuṛ-es yenna-yas : Ssusem ! Effeɣ seg wergaz-agi ! Aṛuḥani iḍeggeṛ argaz-nni ɣer lqaɛa di tlemmast-nsen, dɣa iffeɣ seg-s mbla ma iḍuṛṛ-it.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:36">4:36</a> Lɣaci ikcem-iten akk lxuf, qqaṛen wway gar-asen : D acu-ten yimeslayen-agi ? Yesɛa tazmert s wayes iḥekkem ula ɣef leǧnun ! Akken kan ara sen-yefk lameṛ ad ffɣen !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:37">4:37</a> Di yal tama n tmurt slan s lexbaṛ n Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:38">4:38</a> Iffeɣ-ed si lǧameɛ, yerra ɣer wexxam n Semɛun. Yuɣ lḥal taḍeggalt n Semɛun tuɣ-iț tawla ț-țameqqrant, ḥellelen Sidna Ɛisa iwakken a ț-yesseḥlu. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:39">4:39</a> Yekna ɣuṛ-es, yumeṛ i tawla aț-țeffeɣ seg-s, dɣa teffeɣ-iț ; imiren kan tekker teqdec-asen-d.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:40">4:40</a> Tameddit mi geɣli yiṭij, kra n win yesɛan amuḍin n mkul aṭan, yewwi-yas-t-id. Mkul win i ɣef yessers afus-is yeḥla ! Yesseḥla-ten meṛṛa ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:41">4:41</a> Llan daɣen leǧnun i d-ițeffɣen seg waṭas n yemdanen, țɛeggiḍen qqaṛen : « Kečč d Mmi-s n Ṛebbi ! » Lameɛna Sidna Ɛisa ițɛeggiḍ fell- asen, ur ten-ițțaga ara a d-hedṛen, axaṭer nutni ẓran d nețța i d Lmasiḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:42">4:42</a> Mi guli wass, iffeɣ si temdint, yerra ɣer yiwen wemkan yexlan. Aṭas n lɣaci ṛuḥen țqelliben fell-as. Mi t-ufan, ḥellelen-t iwakken ad yeqqim ɣuṛ-sen, ur ițṛuḥu ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:43">4:43</a> Lameɛna nețța yenna-yasen : Ilaq-iyi ad ṛuḥeɣ ad beccṛeɣ lexbaṛ n lxiṛ n tgeldit n Ṛebbi i temdinin nniḍen ! ?ef wayagi i d țțuceggɛeɣ !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:44">4:44</a> Imiren iṛuḥ ițbecciṛ di leǧwameɛ n tmurt n Yahuda.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:1">5:1</a> Yiwen wass, Sidna Ɛisa yella ɣef rrif n lebḥeṛ n Jiniṣaret. Lɣaci meṛṛa zzin-as-d, mčuččaɛen-d akken ad slen i wawal n Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:2">5:2</a> Iwala snat n teflukin rrif n lebḥeṛ, iḥewwaten rsen-d iwakken ad ssirden icebbaken nsen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:3">5:3</a> Sidna Ɛisa yuli ɣer yiwet si teflukin-nni, tin yellan n Semɛun, yenna-yas ad ibɛed acemma ɣef rrif. Yeqqim , yebda yesselmad-ed lɣaci syenna. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:4">5:4</a> Mi gfukk aselmed yenna i Semɛun : Sbeɛdet taflukt ɣer wemkan lqayen, tḍeggṛem icebbaken-nwen aț-țṣeggdem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:5">5:5</a> Semɛun yenna-yas : A Sidi, iḍ kamel nukni d aṣeggeḍ ur d-neṭṭif acemma ; lameɛna ɣef wawal-ik a nexdem akken i d-tenniḍ, a nḍeggeṛ icebbaken.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:6">5:6</a> Mi xedmen akken i sen-yenna Sidna Ɛisa, ṭṭfen-d aṭas n iselman ( lḥut ), armi qṛib ad qeṛsen icebbaken nsen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:7">5:7</a> Ssawalen, țwehhin i yemdukkal nsen yellan di teflukt nniḍen a d-asen a ten-ɛiwnen. Mi d-usan, ččuṛen snat-nni n teflukin armi qṛib ad ɣeṛqent.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:8">5:8</a> Semɛun-Buṭrus, mi gwala ayagi, yuɣal ɣef tgecrar zdat Sidna Ɛisa, yenna-yas : Beɛɛed fell-i a Sidi axaṭer d amednub i lliɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:9">5:9</a> Ikcem-it lxuf nețța d wid yellan yid-es, dehcen imi i d-ṭṭfen annect-nni n yiselman. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:10">5:10</a> Ula d Yeɛqub akk-d Yuḥenna, arraw n Zabadi yellan d imdukkal n Semɛun wehmen. Sidna Ɛisa yenṭeq ɣer Semɛun yenna-yas : Ur țțagad ara, sya d asawen mačči d iselman ara d-țṣeggideḍ, meɛna d imdanen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:11">5:11</a> Imiren rran-d tiflukin-nsen ɣer rrif, ǧǧan kullec dinna, ddan d Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:12">5:12</a> Mi gella Sidna Ɛisa deg yiwet n taddart n at Jlili, yusa-d yiwen wergaz ihelken lbeṛs, mi gwala Sidna Ɛisa, yuzzel ɣuṛ-es yeɣli ɣer iḍaṛṛen-is, yenna-yas : A Sidi, ma tebɣiḍ, tzemreḍ a yi-tesseḥluḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:13">5:13</a> Sidna Ɛisa issers afus-is fell-as, yenna-yas : Bɣiɣ ! Ili-k teḥliḍ ! Imiren kan, argaz-nni ikkes-as lbeṛs, yeṣfa weglim-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:14">5:14</a> Sidna Ɛisa iweṣṣa-t ur iqqaṛ i yiwen ayen yedṛan yid-es. Yenna-yas : Ṛuḥ ɣer lmuqeddem a k-iwali, tefkeḍ lweɛda ɣef ṣeffu-inek, akken yura di ccariɛa n Musa. Lweɛda-nni a sen-tili d țbut ɣef ḥellu-inek.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:15">5:15</a> Simmal ițwassen Sidna Ɛisa, simmal țnejmaɛen-d ɣuṛ-es lɣaci iwakken ad slen i wawal-is yerna a ten-isseḥlu si lehlakat-nsen ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:16">5:16</a> meɛna nețța iṭeṛṛif iman-is, ițṛuḥu ɣer yimukan yexlan iwakken ad iẓẓall.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:17">5:17</a> Yiwen wass Sidna Ɛisa yella yesselmad. Llan dinna ifariziyen d lɛulama n ccariɛa, usan-d si tuddar n at Jlili, n at Yahuda akk ț-țemdint n Lquds, qqimen smeḥsisen-as. Tazmert n Sidi Ṛebbi yellan yid-es tesseḥlay imuḍan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:18">5:18</a> Atnaya kra n yemdanen wwin-d yiwen wukrif akken deg wusu-ines. ?qelliben amek ara t-skecmen iwakken a t-ssersen zdat Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:19">5:19</a> Imi aṭas n lɣaci i gellan, ur ufin ara ansi ara t-sɛeddin ; ulin ɣef ssqef, kksen kra n iqermuden, ṣubben-t-id s wusu-ines ɣer tlemmast n lɣaci, zdat Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:20">5:20</a> Mi gwala liman-nsen, yenna i umuḍin-nni : Ay argaz, țwaɛeffan-ak ddnubat ik !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:21">5:21</a> Lɛulama akk-d ifariziyen bdan țxemmimen qqaṛen : Amek yezmer a d-yini imeslayen agi ? Wagi d lekfeṛ ! Anwa i gzemren ad iɛfu ddnubat anagar Sidi Ṛebbi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:22">5:22</a> Sidna Ɛisa yeẓran ayen i țxemmimen, yenna-yasen : Acuɣeṛ tețxemmimem akka deg ulawen-nwen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:23">5:23</a> D acu i gsehlen a s-t-iniɣ ? « ?waɛeffan-ak ddnubat-ik» neɣ « ekker telḥuḍ ? »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:24">5:24</a> Ilaq-awen aț-țeẓrem belli Mmi-s n bunadem yesɛa tazmert ad yeɛfu ddnubat di ddunit-agi ! Yezzi ɣer wukrif-nni, yenna-yas : Kker ddem usu-inek tuɣaleḍ ɣer wexxam-ik !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:25">5:25</a> Imiren kan ukrif-nni yekker zdat-sen, yeddem usu i deg yeḍleq, yuɣal ɣer wexxam-is, ițḥemmid Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:26">5:26</a> Wehmen meṛṛa lɣaci, țḥemmiden Sidi Ṛebbi, ikcem-iten lxuf qqaṛen : Ass-agi neẓra ayen werǧin neẓri !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:27">5:27</a> Mi geffeɣ Sidna Ɛisa, iwala yiwen umekkas isem-is Lewwi yeqqim di texxamt anda țxelliṣen tabzert ( leɣṛama ), iqeṛṛeb ɣuṛ-es yenna-yas : Ddu yid-i.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:28">5:28</a> Lewwi yekker, yeǧǧa kullec yedda yid-es. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:29">5:29</a> Lewwi yeɛṛeḍ Sidna Ɛisa ɣer wexxam-is, ihegga-yas imensi. Aṭas n yimekkasen d yemdanen nniḍen i geqqimen yid-sen ad ččen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:30">5:30</a> Ifariziyen d lɛulama n ukabar-nsen iɣaḍ-iten lḥal, nnan i yinelmaden is : Acuɣeṛ i tețțem, tessem akk-d imekkasen imakaren d imednuben ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:31">5:31</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yasen : Mačči d wid iṣeḥḥan i geḥwaǧen ṭṭbib, i t-iḥwaǧen d imuḍan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:32">5:32</a> Ur d-usiɣ ara ad ssiwleɣ i iḥeqqiyen, usiɣ-ed ɣer yimednuben iwakken a d-uɣalen ɣer webrid.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:33">5:33</a> Nnan-as daɣen : Inelmaden n Yeḥya d wid n ifariziyen țțuẓummen acḥal d abrid yerna țẓallan, ma d inelmaden-ik tețțen tessen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:34">5:34</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna yasen : Eɛni tzemrem a sen-tinim i yinebgawen n yesli ad uẓummen ass n tmeɣṛa ? Ur tezmirem ara !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:35">5:35</a> Ad asen wussan i deg ara sen-ițwakkes yesli, ass-nni ad uẓummen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:36">5:36</a> Yerna-yasen-d lemtel-agi : Yiwen ur d-itekkes tafaweț si llebsa tajdiṭ iwakken a ț-ixiḍ ɣef llebsa taqdimt , neɣ m'ulac llebsa-nni tajdiṭ aț-țcerreg ; tafaweț-nni tajdiṭ ur d-țezgay ara ɣef llebsa-nni taqdimt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:37">5:37</a> Daɣen yiwen ur ismaray ccṛab ajdid ɣer yiyeddiden iqdimen , neɣ m'ulac ccṛab-nni ajdid ad icerreg iyeddiden nni ; ur d-ițɣimi ccṛab ur d-țɣimin iyeddiden. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:38">5:38</a> Ihi ccṛab ajdid, ilaq a t-nesmir ɣer iyeddiden ijdiden.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:39">5:39</a> Akken daɣen win yennumen d ccṛab aqdim ur issutur ara ajdid axaṭer yeqqaṛ « d aqdim i gelhan. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:1">6:1</a> Yiwen wass, Sidna Ɛisa akk-d inelmaden-is zegren igran n yirden deg wass n westeɛfu. Tekksen d tigedrin, țḥukkun-tent ger ifassen nsen, tețțen-tent. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:2">6:2</a> Kra n ifariziyen nnan-asen : Acuɣeṛ i txeddmem ayen ur neḥlil deg wass n westeɛfu ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:3">6:3</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yasen : Ur teɣṛim ara ayen yexdem ugellid Dawed asmi yelluẓ nețța d imdukkal-is, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:4">6:4</a> d wamek i gekcem ɣer wexxam iqedsen anda keččmen anagar lmuqedmin ! Iddem-ed aɣṛum n lweɛda, yečča yerna yefka i wid yellan yid-es ɣas akken aɣṛum-nni i lmuqedmin kan iwumi yeḥlel !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:5">6:5</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerna-yasen-d : Mmi-s n bunadem, d nețța i gḥekkmen ɣef wass n westeɛfu !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:6">6:6</a> Ass n westeɛfu nniḍen, Sidna Ɛisa yekcem ɣer lǧameɛ, yebda yesselmad. Yella dinna yiwen wergaz iwumi yekref ufus ayeffus. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:7">6:7</a> Lɛulama n ccariɛa d ifariziyen țɛassan Sidna Ɛisa, ad ẓren ma ad isseḥlu deg wass n westeɛfu iwakken a s-d-afen sebba s wacu ara ccetkin fell-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:8">6:8</a> Lameɛna Sidna Ɛisa yessnen ixemmimen-nsen, yekker yenna i wergaz-nni iwumi yekref ufus : Ekker tbeddeḍ dagi di tlemmast n lɣaci. Argaz-nni yekker ibedd. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:9">6:9</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna : A kkun-steqsiɣ : d acu yellan d leḥlal deg wass n westeɛfu, a nexdem lxiṛ neɣ a nexdem cceṛ ? A nsellek amdan neɣ a t-neǧǧ ad immet ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:10">6:10</a> Yerfed allen-is ɣer wid akk i s-d-yezzin , dɣa yenna i wergaz nni : Eḍleq afus-ik ! Ukrif-nni yeḍleq afus-is, yeḥla.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:11">6:11</a> Nutni yenɣa-ten lɣecc, bdan țemcawaṛen wway gar-asen amek ara xedmen i Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:12">6:12</a> Deg ussan-nni, Sidna Ɛisa yuli ɣer wedrar akken ad iẓẓall. Yeqqim iḍ kamel nețța ideɛɛu ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:13">6:13</a> Mi yuli wass, yessawel i yinelmaden is, yextaṛ seg-sen tnac iwumi isemma « ṛṛusul» yeɛni « imceggɛen.»  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:14">6:14</a> Yella Semɛun iwumi isemma Buṭrus akk-d gma-s Andriyus, Yeɛqub, Yuḥenna, Filbas, Bartelmay, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:15">6:15</a> Matta, ?uma, Yeɛqub mmi-s n ?alfi, Semɛun iwumi qqaṛen awaṭani, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:16">6:16</a> Yahuda mmi-s n Yeɛqub d Yudas n taddart n Qeṛyut win yuɣalen d axeddaɛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:17">6:17</a> Sidna Ɛisa iṣubb-ed yid-sen seg wedrar, ḥebsen di luḍa anda nnejmaɛen aṭas n yinelmaden-is d waṭas n lɣaci i d-yusan si tmurt n Yahuda, si temdint n Lquds, si temdinin n ?ur akk-d Sidun yellan rrif n lebḥeṛ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:18">6:18</a> Usan-d iwakken ad slen i wawal-is yerna a ten-isseḥlu si lehlakat-nsen ; wid akk zedɣen leǧnun, ḥlan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:19">6:19</a> Lɣaci meṛṛa țqelliben a t-nalen ( a t-massen ) axaṭer tețțeffeɣ-ed seg-s tezmert i ten-isseḥlayen akk.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:20">6:20</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerfed allen-is ɣer inelmaden-is yenna : Amarezg-nwen kunwi yellan d iẓawaliyen, tagelda n Sidi Ṛebbi d ayla-nwen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:21">6:21</a> Amarezg-nwen kunwi yelluẓen tura, a d-yas wass i deg ara teṛwum. Amarezg-nwen kunwi yețrun tura, a d-yas wass i deg ara tilim di lfeṛḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:22">6:22</a> D iseɛdiyen ara tilim m'ara kkun-keṛhen yemdanen, m'ara kkun-qecɛen, m'ara kkun-regmen, ad rren isem-nwen amzun d lɛaṛ ɣef ddemma n Mmi-s n bunadem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:23">6:23</a> Ass-nni ilit di lfeṛḥ, friwset s lfeṛḥ axaṭer d ṛṛezq ameqqran i kkun-ițṛaǧun deg igenni ! Imi akka i xedmen lejdud-nsen i lenbiya.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:24">6:24</a> Ma d kunwi ay imeṛkantiyen, a tawaɣit-nwen axaṭer rrbeḥ-nwen tesɛam-t tura. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:25">6:25</a> A tawaɣit-nwen kunwi yeṛwan tura, aț-țuɣalem aț-țellaẓem. A tawaɣit-nwen kunwi yețțaḍṣan tura axaṭer aț-țilim di leḥzen d yimeṭṭawen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:26">6:26</a> A tawaɣit nwen asm'ara kkun-cekkṛen yemdanen, axaṭer akka i xedmen lejdud-nsen i lenbiya n lekdeb.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:27">6:27</a> Ma d nekk a wen-iniɣ i kunwi i d-ițḥessisen : ḥemmlet iɛdawen-nwen, xedmet lxiṛ i wid i kkun-ikeṛhen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:28">6:28</a> Barket wid i kkun-ineɛlen, dɛut s lxiṛ i wid i kkun-iḍelmen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:29">6:29</a> Ma yewwet-ik yiwen ɣer lḥenk, sendi-yas lḥenk nniḍen. Ma yekkes-ak yiwen abeṛnus-ik, anef-as ad yernu ula d aqenduṛ-ik.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:30">6:30</a> Efk-as ayen yuḥwaj i win i k-id-yessutren ; win i k-ikksen kra, ur țṛaǧu ara a k-t-id-yerr. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:31">6:31</a> Xedmet i wiyaḍ ayen i tebɣam a wen-t xedmen i kunwi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:32">6:32</a> Ma yella tḥemmlem kan wid i kkun-iḥemmlen, d acu n lxiṛ i txedmem ? Ula d imcumen ḥemmlen wid i ten-iḥemmlen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:33">6:33</a> Ma yella txeddmem lxiṛ i wid kan i wen ixeddmen lxiṛ, d acu n lxiṛ i txedmem ? Ula d imcumen xeddmen akka.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:34">6:34</a> Ma yella tṛeṭṭlem i wid kan i teẓram a wen-d-rren, d acu i trebḥem ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi ? Imcumen daɣen ṛeṭṭlen i imddukal-nsen iwakken ad afen aṛeṭṭal ula d nutni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:35">6:35</a> Lameɛna kunwi : ḥemmlet iɛdawen-nwen, xedmet lxiṛ, ṛeḍlet mbla ṭṭmeɛ, akka ara tesɛum lfayda tameqqrant, ara tilim d arraw n Sidi Ṛebbi ɛlayen. Axaṭer Ṛebbi d aḥnin ula ɣef yemcumen akk-d wid inekkṛen lxiṛ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:36">6:36</a> Iḥninet, sɛut ṛṛeḥma akken i ț-isɛa Baba-twen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:37">6:37</a> Ur țḥasabet ara wiyaḍ iwakken Sidi Ṛebbi ur kkun-ițḥasab ara. Ur ḥekkmet ara ɣef wiyaḍ iwakken Sidi Ṛebbi ur iḥekkem ara fell-awen. Semmḥet i wiyaḍ iwakken a wen isameḥ Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:38">6:38</a> Seddqet, a wen d-yuɣal s ɣuṛ Ṛebbi. Ma tseddqem mbla lkil, a wen-d yuɣal s ɣuṛ Ṛebbi mbla lkil ; axaṭer a wen-d-ițwaktal s lkil s wacu tektalem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:39">6:39</a> Yewwi-yasen-d lemtel nniḍen, yenna-yasen : Aderɣal ur izmir ara ad iṭṭef afus i uderɣal nniḍen, neɣ m'ulac ad grirben i sin ɣer yeɣzeṛ ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:40">6:40</a> anelmad werǧin yugar ccix-is, lameɛna anelmad ara yawḍen am ccix-is di tmusni, ad yili am nețța.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:41">6:41</a> Acuɣeṛ tețwaliḍ axeclaw yellan di tiṭ n gma-k ur tețwaliḍ ara tigejdit yellan di tiṭ-ik ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:42">6:42</a> Amek ara tiniḍ i gma-k : eǧǧ-iyi ad kkseɣ axeclaw yellan di tiṭ-ik kečč ur neẓri tigejdit yellan di tiṭ-ik ? A bu sin wudmawen, ekkes uqbel tigejdit yellan di tiṭ-ik, imiren aț-țwaliḍ amek ara tekkseḍ axeclaw yellan di tiṭ n gma-k.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:43">6:43</a> Ulac ttejṛa lɛali i d-ițțaken lfakya n diri. Ulac daɣen ttejṛa n diri i d-ițțaken lfakya lɛali. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:44">6:44</a> Ihi mkul ttejṛa, tețwaɛqal s lfakya-ines. Ur d-ntekkes ara lexṛif seg isennanen, ur d-ntekkes ara daɣen tiẓurin seg inijel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:45">6:45</a> Argaz yelhan issufuɣ-ed ayen yelhan seg wugerruj yellan deg wul-is, ma d amcum d ayen n diri yellan deg ul-is i d-issufuɣ. Axaṭer d ayen yellan deg wul n wemdan i d-ițeffɣen seg imi-s.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:46">6:46</a> Acuɣer i yi-d-tessawalem « A Sidi, a Sidi », ur txeddmem ara ayen i wen-d-qqaṛeɣ ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:47">6:47</a> A wen-d-iniɣ ar wuɣuṛ ițemcabi wemdan i d-ițțasen ɣuṛ-i, isellen i wawal-iw yerna yeṭṭafaṛ-it :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:48">6:48</a> ițemcabi ɣer yiwen n wemdan yebnan axxam. Yeɣza, yeɣza deg wakal iwakken ad issers lsas-is ɣef wezṛu ; iḥmel-ed wasif, infel-ed ɣef wexxam-nni, meɛna ur t-issenhezz ara imi lsas-is yerṣa, yebna ɣef wezṛu akken ilaq.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:49">6:49</a> Ma d win isellen i wawal-iw ur netbiɛ ara ayen i d-nniɣ, ițemcabi ɣer wemdan yebnan axxam ɣef ṛṛmel mbla lsas : iḥmel-ed wasif, infel-ed ɣef wexxam-nni, imiren kan yeɣli , lexsaṛa-s ț-țameqqrant !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:1">7:1</a> Mi gekfa awal zdat widak i s-d-ismeḥsisen, yekcem ɣer temdint n Kafernaḥum. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:2">7:2</a> Yiwen lqebṭan aṛumani yesɛa aqeddac i gḥemmel aṭas ; aqeddac-agi yuḍen, ițmețțat.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:3">7:3</a> Mi gesla s Sidna Ɛisa, iceggeɛ ɣuṛ-es kra seg yimeqqranen n wat Isṛail iwakken a d-yas ad isseḥlu aqeddac-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:4">7:4</a> Mi wwḍen ɣer Sidna Ɛisa, ḥellelen-t nnan-as : A Sidi ! Yuklal a s-txedmeḍ lxiṛ agi, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:5">7:5</a> axaṭer iḥemmel agdud nneɣ ; d nețța i gebnan lǧameɛ-nneɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:6">7:6</a> Sidna Ɛisa yedda yid-sen. Mi qṛib ad yaweḍ ɣer wexxam, lqebṭan-nni iceggeɛ imdukkal-is a s-inin : A Sidi, ur țɛețțib ara iman-ik, ur uklaleɣ ara a d-tkecmeḍ axxam-iw.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:7">7:7</a> Nekk s yiman-iw daɣen walaɣ ur uklaleɣ ara a n-aseɣ ɣuṛ-ek ; ini-d kan yiwen wawal, aqeddac-iw ad iḥlu. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:8">7:8</a> Axaṭer sɛiɣ wid i gṭebbiṛen fell-i, sɛiɣ daɣen lɛeskeṛ seddaw lḥekma-w. Ad iniɣ i yiwen ṛuḥ ad iṛuḥ ; i wayeḍ as-ed, a d-yas ; ad iniɣ i wqeddac-iw xdem ayagi, a t-ixdem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:9">7:9</a> Mi gesla Sidna Ɛisa i yimeslayen-agi, itɛeǧǧeb deg-sen. Yezzi ɣer lɣaci yeddan yid-es, yenna-yasen : A wen-d-iniɣ : di tmurt n wat Isṛail meṛṛa ur ufiɣ ara liman yecban wagi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:10">7:10</a> Widak-nni i d-ițwaceggɛen, mi uɣalen ɣer wexxam ufan aqeddac-nni yeḥla.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:11">7:11</a> Azekka-nni, Sidna Ɛisa iṛuḥ ɣer yiwet n taddart isem-is Naɛim. Ddan yid-es inelmaden-is d waṭas n lɣaci.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:12">7:12</a> Mi gewweḍ ɣer tewwurt n taddart, atnaya lɣaci wwin-d lmegget a t-meḍlen, d mmi-s n yiwet n taǧǧalt, anagar nețța i tesɛa. Aṭas n imezdaɣ n taddart-nni i d-iddan yid-es. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:13">7:13</a> Mi ț-iwala Sidna Ɛisa, tɣaḍ-it, yenna-yas : Ur țru ara !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:14">7:14</a> Iqeṛṛeb ɣer usenduq n lmegget nni, iḍleq afus-is innul-it, dɣa widak i t-irefden ḥebsen. Yenna : Ay aqcic ! Ekker !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:15">7:15</a> Dɣa lmegget-nni ikker-ed, yebda iheddeṛ. Sidna Ɛisa yerra aqcic-nni i yemma-s.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:16">7:16</a> Ikcem-iten akk lxuf, bdan țḥemmiden Ṛebbi qqaṛen : « Sidi Ṛebbi yerra-d ddehn-is ɣer wegdud is, nnbi ameqqran ikker-ed gar-aneɣ. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:17">7:17</a> Slan s wannect-agi di tmurt n Yahuda meṛṛa akk ț-țmura i s-d izzin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:18">7:18</a> Inelmaden n Yeḥya xebbṛen-t ɣef wayen akk yedṛan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:19">7:19</a> Yeḥya iceggeɛ sin seg yinelmaden-is ɣer Sidna Ɛisa iwakken a s-inin ma d nețța i d win akken ara d-yasen, neɣ ilaq ad ṛǧun wayeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:20">7:20</a> Ewwḍen ɣer Sidna Ɛisa nnan-as : Iceggeɛ-aɣ-ed ɣuṛ-ek Yeḥya aɣeṭṭas iwakken a k-nesteqsi ma d kečč i d win akken ara d-yasen neɣ ilaq a neṛǧu wayeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:21">7:21</a> Di teswiɛt-nni ufan Sidna Ɛisa isseḥla aṭas n yemdanen si lehlakat nsen d leɛyubat-nsen, issufeɣ leǧnun seg wid yețwamelken, yerra-d iẓri i waṭas n yiderɣalen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:22">7:22</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna i yinelmaden n Yeḥya : Ṛuḥet erret lexbaṛ i Yeḥya ɣef wayen teẓram d wayen teslam : iderɣalen țwalin, wid ikerfen teddun, wid ihelken lbeṛs ṣeffun, iɛeẓẓugen sellen, lmegtin ḥeggun-d, le xbaṛ n lxiṛ ițwabecceṛ i yigellilen . </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:23">7:23</a> D aseɛdi win iwumi ur țțiliɣ ara d ugur.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:24">7:24</a> Mi ṛuḥen inelmaden-nni i d-iceggeɛ Yeḥya, Sidna Ɛisa yebda iheddeṛ i lɣaci ɣef Yeḥya yenna : D acu i tṛuḥem a d-teẓrem deg unezṛuf ? D aɣanim yețhuzzu waḍu ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:25">7:25</a> D acu i tṛuḥem a d-teẓrem ? D amdan yelsan llebsa ifazen ? Wid yețlusun llebsa ifazen, yețɛicin di rrbeḥ atnan di lebṛuj n yigelliden !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:26">7:26</a> Anwa i tṛuḥem a t-id-teẓrem ihi ? D nnbi ? A wen-d-iniɣ ... yugar nnbi ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:27">7:27</a> Yeḥya d win i ɣef yura di tira iqedsen :  Atan ad zzewreɣ amceggeɛ-inu zdat-ek iwakken a k-iheggi abrid.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:28">7:28</a> Nniɣ-awen, ulac di ddunit amdan yugaren Yeḥya aɣeṭṭas. Lameɛna amecṭuḥ maḍi di tgelda n Sidi Ṛebbi, d ameqqran fell-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:29">7:29</a> Lɣaci meṛṛa mi slan i Yeḥya, setɛeṛfen s lḥeqq n Sidi Ṛebbi, qeblen ad țwaɣeḍsen deg waman, llan gar-asen ula d imekkasen n tebzert ( n leɣṛama ).  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:30">7:30</a> Ma d ifariziyen d lɛulama n ccariɛa, ur qbilen ara ayen i sen yebɣa Sidi Ṛebbi, ugin a ten yesseɣḍes Yeḥya.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:31">7:31</a> ?er wacu ara metleɣ imdanen n lǧil-agi ? ?er wuɣuṛ i țemcabin ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:32">7:32</a> ?emcabin ɣer warrac yeqqimen di tejmaɛt, țemsawalen wway gar-asen qqaṛen : Newwet-awen-d ajewwaq ur tecḍiḥem ara, nerna newwi-yawen-d acewwiq n leḥzen ur trum ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:33">7:33</a> Yeḥya aɣeṭṭas yusa-d ur itețț aɣṛum ur itess ccṛab, teqqaṛem ițwamlek.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:34">7:34</a> Mmi-s n bunadem yusa-d itețț itess, teqqaṛem : ițxemmim kan ad yečč ad isew, d amdakkul n yimekkasen akk-d yemcumen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:35">7:35</a> Lameɛna lḥeqq n Sidi Ṛebbi ɛeqlen-t warraw-is, nutni qeblen-t.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:36">7:36</a> Yiwen ufarizi yusa-d ad iɛṛrḍ Sidna Ɛisa ad yečč ɣuṛ-es. Idda yid-es, ikcem ɣer wexxam-is, yeqqim ad yečč. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:37">7:37</a> Di taddart-nni tella yiwet n tmeṭṭut yellan d yir tameṭṭut ; mi tesla s Sidna Ɛisa yella deg wexxam n wufarizi-nni, tekcem tewwi yid-es tabuqalt n leɛṭer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:38">7:38</a> Tekka-d deffir Sidna Ɛisa, teɣli ɣer idaṛṛen-is tețru. Tessebzeg (tesselxes) iḍaṛṛen n Sidna Ɛisa s yimeṭṭawen-is, tesfeḍ-iten s ucebbub-is, tessudun-iten yerna tdehhin-iten s leɛṭeṛ-nni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:39">7:39</a> Afarizi-nni mi gwala annect-nni, ixemmem deg iman-is yenna : Lemmer argaz-agi d nnbi i gella, yili yeɛqel belli tameṭṭut-agi i t-ițnalen d yir tameṭṭut i tella.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:40">7:40</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna i ufarizi-nni : A Semɛun ! Bɣiɣ a k-d-iniɣ yiwen wawal ! Afarizi yerra-yas-d : Ini-d a Sidi !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:41">7:41</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Illa yiwen umeṛkanti issekray idrimen. Ițțalas i sin yergazen, yiwen yețțalas-as xemsmeyyat alef, wayeḍ xemsin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:42">7:42</a> Imi ur sɛin ara i sin s wacu ara xelṣen, isemmeḥ-asen. Anwa deg-sen ara t-iḥemmlen akteṛ ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:43">7:43</a> Semɛun afarizi yerra-yas : Ahat d win iwumi i gsumeḥ ṭṭlaba tameqqrant. Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Tesɛiḍ lḥeqq !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:44">7:44</a> Dɣa iwehha ɣer tmeṭṭut-nni, yenna i Semɛun : Twalaḍ tameṭṭut-agi ? Kecmeɣ-d ɣer wexxam-ik, ur iyi-d-tefkiḍ ara aman ad ssirdeɣ iḍaṛṛen-iw, nețțat tessared-iten s yimeṭṭawen-is terna tesfeḍ-iten s ucebbub-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:45">7:45</a> Kečč ur d-tselmeḍ ara fell-i, nețțat segmi i d-tekcem tessudun deg iḍaṛṛen-iw. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:46">7:46</a> Kečč ur tedhineḍ ara aqeṛṛuy-iw ula s zzit, ma d nețțat tesmar-ed leɛṭeṛ ɣef yiḍaṛṛen-iw.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:47">7:47</a> A k-iniɣ : ddnubat-is meṛṛa țwaɛfan as daymi i d-tbeggen leḥmala tameqqrant. Ma d win iwumi yețwaɛfa ciṭuḥ, leḥmala-ines ț-țamecṭuḥt.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:48">7:48</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna i tmeṭṭut-nni : Atan țwaɛeffan-am ddnubat-im !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:49">7:49</a> Inebgawen nniḍen bdan qqaṛen deg yiman-nsen : « d acu-t wergaz-agi i gessawḍen iman-is ad yeɛfu ula d ddnubat ? »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:50">7:50</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna i tmeṭṭut-nni : Imi tumneḍ yis-i tețțusellkeḍ, ṛuḥ di lehna.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:1">8:1</a> Sidna Ɛisa iteddu yețbecciṛ lexbaṛ n lxiṛ n tgeldit n Ṛebbi si temdint ɣer tayeḍ, si taddart ɣer tayeḍ. Tnac-nni yinelmaden-is ddan yid-es, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:2">8:2</a> ddant daɣen kra n tilawin i gesseḥla si lehlakat-nsent, tid iwumi yessufeɣ leǧnun. Tella gar-asent Meryem iwumi qqaṛen tamagdalit ițwasellken si sebɛa leǧnun, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:3">8:3</a> akk-d Yunna tameṭṭut n Cuza lewkil n ugellid Hiṛudus, Suzana akk ț-țilawin nniḍen i ten-ițɛawanen s wayen sɛant.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:4">8:4</a> Lɣaci usan-d seg waṭas n tudrin. Mi d-nnejmaɛen ɣuṛ-es, Sidna Ɛisa yewwi-yasen-d lemtel-agi :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:5">8:5</a> Yiwen ufellaḥ iffeɣ ad izreɛ irden. Mi gzerreɛ, kra n iɛeqqayen ɣlin ɣer webrid , țwaṛekḍen yerna ččan-ten yefṛax n igenni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:6">8:6</a> Amur nniḍen n zzerriɛa yeɣli ger yedɣaɣen , mi d-temɣi teqquṛ imi xuṣṣen waman.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:7">8:7</a> Amur nniḍen yeɣli daɣen ger isennanen , mi d-temɣi zzerriɛa mɣin-d yid-es isennanen, ɣummen-ț. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:8">8:8</a> Amur nniḍen daɣen yeɣli deg wakal lɛali ; mi d-mɣin, mkul aɛeqqa yefka-d meyya. Mi d-yenna ayagi, iɛeggeḍ yenna : Win yesɛan imeẓẓuɣen isel-ed !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:9">8:9</a> Inelmaden-is ssutren-as d acu i d lmeɛna n lemtel-agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:10">8:10</a> Yerra-yasen : Kunwi yețțunefk-awen-d aț țissinem lbaḍna n tgeldit n Ṛebbi, ma d wiyaḍ ițțunefk-asen-d a ț-issinen s lemtul kan iwakken  ɣas ad ẓren s wallen-nsen ur țwalin ara, ɣas ma slan ur fehhmen ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:11">8:11</a> Atah lmeɛna n lemtel-agi : zzerriɛa d awal n Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:12">8:12</a> Llan kra n yemdanen țemcabin ɣer webrid-nni anda teɣli zzerriɛa, m'ara slen i wawal, Cciṭan a d-yas a t-iqleɛ seg ulawen-nsen iwakken ur țțamnen ur țwasellaken.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:13">8:13</a> Wiyaḍ țemcabin ɣer wakal yeččuṛen d idɣaɣen. M'ara slen i wawal a t-qeblen s lfeṛḥ lameɛna ur t-țaǧǧan ara ad iger izuṛan ; imiren kan ad amnen, m'ara d-yas lweqt n ujeṛṛeb țțuɣalen ɣer deffir.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:14">8:14</a> Ayen yeɣlin ger isennanen, d wid isellen i wawal meɛna m'ara d-imɣi ur igemmu ara deg-sen axaṭer țțaǧan anezgum d rrbeḥ akk-d zzhu n ddunit ad iɣumm awal-nni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:15">8:15</a> Ma d ayen yețwazerɛen deg wakal lɛali, d wid isellen i wawal s wul yeṣfan d neyya ḥerzen-t yerna țțaǧan-d lxiṛ s ṣṣbeṛ-nsen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:16">8:16</a> Yiwen ur iceɛɛel taftilt iwakken a ț-iɣum s lḥila neɣ a ț-issedreg; lameɛna a ț-issers ɣef lmeṣbeḥ iwakken kra n win ara d-ikecmen ad iwali tafat. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:17">8:17</a> Kra n wayen yeffren a d-iban, kra n wayen yellan di ṭṭlam a t-id-tesban tafat.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:18">8:18</a> Ɛasset iman-nwen ihi ɣef wayen i tsellem, axaṭer win i gḥerzen ayen yesɛa a s-nernu, ma d win ur nḥerrez ara a s-ițwakkes ula d ayen i gɣil yesɛa-t.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:19">8:19</a> Yemma-s d watmaten n Sidna Ɛisa usan-d a t-ẓren, meɛna ur zmiren ara ad qeṛṛben ɣuṛ-es imi aṭas n lɣaci i gellan dinna. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:20">8:20</a> Ssawḍen-as lexbaṛ nnan-as : A Sidi, yemma-k d watmaten-ik atnan di beṛṛa, bɣan a k-ẓren.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:21">8:21</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yasen : Yemma d watmaten-iw d widak ismeḥsisen i wawal n Ṛebbi yerna ttabaɛen-t.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:22">8:22</a> Yiwen wass, Sidna Ɛisa yuli ɣer yiwet n teflukt nețța d yinelmaden-is. Yenna-yasen : Eyyaw a nzegret ɣer tama nniḍen n lebḥeṛ n Jlili. Dɣa ṛuḥen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:23">8:23</a> Mi teddun ɣef waman, Sidna Ɛisa yeṭṭes. Yekker-ed waḍu iǧehden di lebḥeṛ, taflukt tebda tețțačaṛ d aman, ikcem-iten lxuf ameqqran. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:24">8:24</a> Inelmaden qeṛṛben ɣuṛ-es, sekkren-t-id nnan-as : A Sidi, a Sidi, atan a neɣṛeq. Yekker-ed, dɣa yumeṛ i waḍu d lemwaji ad ḥebsen, imiren kan ters-ed talwit.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:25">8:25</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen : Anida-t liman-nwen ? Tɛeǧǧben, țergigin, qqaṛen wway gar-asen : Anwa-t wagi ? Izmer ad yefk lameṛ i waḍu d lebḥeṛ yerna țțaɣen as awal !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:26">8:26</a> Wwḍen ɣer tama nniḍen n lebḥeṛ, ɣer tmurt n ijiṛaziyen iqublen tamurt n Jlili.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:27">8:27</a> Mi d-yers Sidna Ɛisa, ataya yusa-d ɣuṛ-es yiwen wergaz n taddart nni, melken-t waṭas n leǧnun ; acḥal ur yelsi llebsa, ur yezdiɣ axxam, yețɛici di tmeqbeṛt ger iẓekwan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:28">8:28</a> Mi gwala Sidna Ɛisa, yeɣli ɣer iḍaṛṛen-is iɛeggeḍ yenna : D acu i tebɣiḍ ɣuṛ-i a Ɛisa Mmi-s n Ṛebbi ɛlayen ? Di leɛnaya-k ur iyi-țɛețțib ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:29">8:29</a> Yenna-yas-d akka axaṭer Sidna Ɛisa yefka lameṛ i uṛuḥani i t-izedɣen ad iffeɣ seg-s. Acḥal d abrid i s-cudden ifassen d iḍaṛṛen s ssnasel, nețța isseɣṛas-itent yerna aṛuḥani-nni yezzuɣuṛ-it ɣer yimukan yexlan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:30">8:30</a> Sidna Ɛisa isteqsa-t yenna-yas : Isem-ik ? yerra-yas : Tarbaɛt. Yenna-yas-d akka axaṭer aṭas n leǧnun i t-izedɣen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:31">8:31</a> ?ḥellilen Sidna Ɛisa ur ten-ițceggiɛ ara ɣer yimukan n ṭṭlam. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:32">8:32</a> Tella dinna yiwet n tqeḍɛit tameqqrant n yilfan kessen deg yiwet n tiɣilt. Leǧnun-nni țḥellilen Sidna Ɛisa a ten-yeǧǧ ad kecmen deg yilfan-nni ; Sidna Ɛisa iserreḥ-asen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:33">8:33</a> Imiren ffɣen seg wergaz-nni, kecmen deg yilfan, grarben seg ixef n tiɣilt ɣer lebḥeṛ, ɣeṛqen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:34">8:34</a> Imeksawen-nsen mi walan ayen yedṛan uzzlen ɣer taddart d lexlawi ad ssiwḍen lexbaṛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:35">8:35</a> Usan-d lɣaci ɣer Sidna Ɛisa, ufan-d argaz-nni i seg d-ffɣen leǧnun yeqqim ɣer iḍaṛṛen-is, yuɣal-ed ɣer leɛqel-is, yelsa llebsa. Wehmen akk, tekcem-iten tugdi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:36">8:36</a> Wid iḥedṛen i wayen yedṛan, ḥkan amek yețwasellek umeǧnun-nni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:37">8:37</a> Imezdaɣ n tmurt uggaden, dɣa ssutren i Sidna Ɛisa ad ibɛed fell-asen. Sidna Ɛisa yuli ɣer teflukt iwakken ad iṛuḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:38">8:38</a> Argaz-nni i seg d-ffɣen leǧnun, issuter a t-yeǧǧ ad yeddu yid-es, meɛna Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:39">8:39</a> Uɣal ɣer wexxam-ik, teḥkuḍ ayen akk i k-ixdem Ṛebbi. Argaz-nni iṛuḥ, ikcem ɣer taddart, yeḥka meṛṛa wayen i s-ixdem Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:40">8:40</a> Mi d-yuɣal Sidna Ɛisa, lɣaci meṛṛa i t-ițṛaǧun mmugren-t-id.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:41">8:41</a> Yewweḍ-ed yiwen wergaz isem-is Jayrus, d ameqqran n lǧameɛ, yeɣli ɣer iḍaṛṛen n Sidna Ɛisa, yețḥellil deg-s iwakken ad iddu ɣer wexxam is </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:42">8:42</a> axaṭer yesɛa yelli-s tnac yiseggasen di leɛmeṛ-is, tețmețțat yerna anagar nețțat i gesɛa. Akken ițeddu Sidna Ɛisa ɣer dinna, ḥeṛsen-t-id lɣaci si mkul lǧiha. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:43">8:43</a> Tella dinna yiwet n tmeṭṭut ihelken, tnac iseggasen nețțat tessaq d idammen. Texṣeṛ ayen akk i tesɛa ɣer ṭṭebba, yiwen ur ț-isseḥla. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:44">8:44</a> Tekka-d deffir Sidna Ɛisa, teḍleq afus-is, tennul iri n ubeṛnus-is, imiren kan teḥla ḥebsen idammen-nni. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:45">8:45</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenṭeq yenna : Anwa akka i yi-d-innulen ? Imi ssusmen meṛṛa, Buṭrus yenna yas : A Sidi, lɣaci yezzi-yak-d yerna iḥṛes-ik-id si mkul tama, kečč teqqaṛeḍ anwa i k-id-innulen !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:46">8:46</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Yella yiwen i yi-d-innulen axaṭer ḥusseɣ i kra n tezmert teffeɣ seg-i.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:47">8:47</a> Tameṭṭut-nni imi twala ulamek ara teffer, tusa-d tețțergigi teɣli ɣer yiḍaṛṛen n Sidna Ɛisa, teḥka-d zdat lɣaci meṛṛa acuɣeṛ i t-tennul d wamek teḥla imiren kan si lehlak-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:48">8:48</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : A yell-i, imi tumneḍ yis-i teḥliḍ ! Ṛuḥ di talwit.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:49">8:49</a> Mazal-it iheddeṛ, ataya yiwen wergaz yusa-d seg wexxam n Jayṛus, yewwi-yas-d lexbaṛ-agi : Yelli-k temmut ! Ur țɛețțib ara Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:50">8:50</a> Sidna Ɛisa mi s-yesla i wergaz-nni, yenna i Jayṛus : Ur țțagad ara ! Amen kan, yelli-k aț-țeslek.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:51">8:51</a> Mi gewweḍ ɣer wexxam, ur yeǧǧi yiwen ad ikcem yid-es anagar Buṭrus, Yuḥenna, Yeɛqub akk-d baba-s d yemma-s n teqcict-nni. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:52">8:52</a> Wid yellan dinna țrun akk, țɣerriden ( țmeǧǧiden ) fell-as. Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen : Beṛka-kkun imeṭṭawen ! taqcict ur temmut ara ! D iḍes i teṭṭes.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:53">8:53</a> Nutni ugin a s-d-ḥessen imi ẓran taqcict temmut.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:54">8:54</a> Sidna Ɛisa yeṭṭef-iț-id seg wufus yenna-yas s taɣect ɛlayen : A taqcict, ekker !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:55">8:55</a> Imiren kan yuɣal-iț-id ṛṛuḥ, tekker-ed. Sidna Ɛisa yumeṛ a s-fken ayen ara tečč. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:56">8:56</a> Imawlan-is wehmen. Sidna Ɛisa iweṣṣa-ten ur țɛawaden i yiwen ayen yedṛan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:1">9:1</a> Sidna Ɛisa isnejmaɛ-ed tnac yinelmaden-is, yefka-yasen tazmert d lḥekma s wacu ara ssufɣen leǧnun, ara sseḥlun imuḍan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:2">9:2</a> Iceggeɛ-iten ad beccṛen tageldit n Ṛebbi, yerna ad sseḥlun imuḍan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:3">9:3</a> Yenna-yasen : Ur țțawit acemma yid-wen d aɛwin, ur țțawit aɛekkaz neɣ agrab (aqwrab), ur țțawit aɣṛum neɣ idrimen, ur țțawit ara daɣen sin yiqendyaṛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:4">9:4</a> Kra n win ara yestṛeḥben yis wen, qqimet deg wexxam-is alamma tṛuḥem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:5">9:5</a> Ma d anda ur stṛeḥben ara yis-wen, m'ara teffɣem si taddart-nni, zwit ula d aɣebbaṛ-is seg yiḍaṛṛen nwen, iwakken aț-țcehdem fell-asen belli d nutni i kkun-yugin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:6">9:6</a> Ṛuḥen, țeddun si taddart ɣer tayeḍ, țbecciṛen lexbaṛ n lxiṛ, sseḥlayen imuḍan di mkul amkan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:7">9:7</a> Hiṛudus lḥakem n tmurt n Jlili, yeɛweq mi gesla s wayen yedṛan meṛṛa, axaṭer kra n yemdanen qqaṛen : « d Yeḥya i d-iḥyan si ger lmegtin ! » </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:8">9:8</a> Wiyaḍ qqaṛen : « d Sidna Ilyas i d-yuɣalen ! » Neɣ : « ahat d yiwen si lenbiya n zik i d-iḥyan ! »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:9">9:9</a> Lameɛna Hiṛudus yeqqaṛ : « Yeḥya kkseɣ-as aqeṛṛuy ! Anwa-t ihi wagi i ɣef selleɣ annect-agi ? » Dɣa ițqellib ad iẓer Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:10">9:10</a> Mi d-uɣalen ṛṛusul n Sidna Ɛisa, bdan ḥekkun-as ayen akk i xedmen. Yewwi-ten yid-es ɣer yiwen wemkan, ɣer tama n taddart n Bitsayda akken ad qqimen weḥḥed-sen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:11">9:11</a> Mi slan anda yella lɣaci tebɛen-t. Nețța yesteṛḥeb yis-sen, yebda iheddeṛ-asen ɣef tgeldit n Ṛebbi, yesseḥla daɣen wid ihelken. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:12">9:12</a> Akken qṛib ad yeɣli yiṭij, tnac-nni n ṛṛusul usan-d ɣer Sidna Ɛisa nnan-as : Serreḥ i lɣaci ad ṛuḥen ɣer temdinin ț-țudrin iqeṛben iwakken ad afen ayen ara ččen d wanda ara ṭsen, axaṭer aql-aɣ deg wemkan yexlan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:13">9:13</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen : Fket-asen kunwi s yiman-nwen ayen ara ččen. Erran-as : ?uṛ-nneɣ anagar xemsa teḥbulin n weɣṛum d sin yiselman. Neɣ tebɣiḍ a nṛuḥ nukni a d-naɣ ayen ara ččen lɣaci-agi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:14">9:14</a> Llan dinna azal n xemsa alaf n yergazen. Sidna Ɛisa yenna i yinelmaden-is : Feṛqet lɣaci ț-țirebbaɛ n xemsin xemsin, tesɣimem-ten.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:15">9:15</a> Ṛuḥen sɣimen-ten akken i sen-d yenna. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:16">9:16</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerfed allen-is ɣer yigenni, yeḥmed Ṛebbi icekkeṛ-it, yeddem-ed xemsa-nni teḥbulin n weɣṛum d sin-nni iselman yebḍa-ten, yefka-ten i inelmaden-is a ten- feṛqen i lɣaci. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:17">9:17</a> ?čan akk armi ṛwan, yerna ččuṛen tnac yiḍellaɛen s wayen i d-yugran.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:18">9:18</a> Yiwen wass Sidna Ɛisa yeqqim weḥd-es yețẓalla. Inelmaden-is qeṛṛben ɣuṛ-es dɣa isteqsa-ten yenna-yasen : D acu-yi ɣer lɣaci ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:19">9:19</a> Rran-as : Kra qqaṛen d Yeḥya aɣeṭṭas ; wiyaḍ d Sidna Ilyas i d-yuɣalen ; ma d kra nniḍen qqaṛen d yiwen si lenbiya n zik i d-iḥyan si ger lmegtin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:20">9:20</a> Yenna-yasen : I kunwi, d acu-yi ɣuṛ-wen ? Yenṭeq Buṭrus yenna-yas : D kečč i d Lmasiḥ n Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:21">9:21</a> Sidna Ɛisa iweṣṣa-ten ur qqaṛen i yiwen belli d nețța i d Lmasiḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:22">9:22</a> Yenna-yasen daɣen : Ilaq Mmi-s n bunadem ad yeɛteb aṭas. A t-nekkṛen lecyux d lmuqedmin imeqqranen akk-d lɛulama n ccariɛa yerna a t-nɣen, lameɛna ass wis tlata a d-iḥyu si ger lmegtin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:23">9:23</a> Yenna daɣen i lɣaci : Win yebɣan ad iddu yid-i ur ilaq ara ad ixemmem ɣef tudert-is ; ilaq ad iqbel ad yenɛețțab yal ass ɣef ddemma n yisem-iw yerna ad yetbeɛ abrid-iw. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:24">9:24</a> Axaṭer win yebɣan ad isellek tudert-is a s-tṛuḥ. Ma d win iwumi ara tṛuḥ ɣef ddemma-w ad yuɣal a ț-yaf. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:25">9:25</a> D acu i d lfayda n wemdan ara irebḥen ddunit meṛṛa ma yesṛuḥ tudert-is neɣ issenger iman-is ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:26">9:26</a> Atan win issetḥan yis-i neɣ s yimeslayen iw, ad issetḥi yis Mmi-s n bunadem m'ara d-yas di tmanegt-is ț-țmanegt n Baba Ṛebbi akk-d lmalayekkat iqedsen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:27">9:27</a> A wen-d-iniɣ tideț, llan gar-awen wid ur nețmețțat ara alamma walan Tageldit n Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:28">9:28</a> Ɛeddan azal n tmanya wussan segmi i d-yenna imeslayen-agi. Sidna Ɛisa yewwi yid-es Buṭrus, Yuḥenna d Yeɛqub, yuli ɣer wedrar ad iẓẓall. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:29">9:29</a> Mi gella ideɛɛu yenbeddal wudem-is, llebsa-s tuɣal ț-țamellalt tețfeǧǧiǧ am yiṭij.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:30">9:30</a> Taswiɛt kan bedden-d ɣuṛ-es sin yergazen heddṛen yid-es : d Sidna Musa akk-d Sidna Ilyas. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:31">9:31</a> Banen-ed di tafat tameqqrant, țmeslayen yid-es ɣef lmut-is ara yedṛun di temdint n Lquds.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:32">9:32</a> Buṭrus d yimdukkal-is yewwi ten yiḍes. Mi d-endekwalen, walan tamanegt n Sidna Ɛisa akk-d wid yellan yid-es.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:33">9:33</a> Mi kkren ad ṛuḥen sin-nni yergazen, yenṭeq Buṭrus ɣer Sidna Ɛisa yenna : A Sidi, acḥal yelha m'akka nella dagi ! Ma tebɣiḍ a nesbedd tlata yiqiḍunen, yiwen i kečč, yiwen i Sidna Musa wayeḍ i Sidna Ilyas. Yenna-d akka, axaṭer ur yeẓri d acu i d-iqqaṛ ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:34">9:34</a> Mazal-it iheddeṛ mi ten-id-tɣumm yiwet n tagut. Buṭrus d imdukkal-is ikcem-iten lxuf d ameqqran. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:35">9:35</a> Iffeɣ-ed yiwen n ṣṣut si tagut-nni yenna-d : Wagi d Mmi, d nețța i xtaṛeɣ, smeḥsiset-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:36">9:36</a> Mi geḥbes ṣṣut-nni, walan anagar Sidna Ɛisa. Deg ussan-nni, inelmaden ur ḥkin i yiwen ayen ẓran.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:37">9:37</a> Azekka-nni mi d-ṣubben seg wedrar, aṭas n lɣaci i d-immugren Sidna Ɛisa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:38">9:38</a> Atah yiwen wergaz iɛeggeḍ-ed si ger lɣaci yenna : A Sidi, di leɛnaya-k muqel-ed ɣer mmi, ala nețța i sɛiɣ ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:39">9:39</a> Ikcem-it uṛuḥani, tiswiɛin m'ara t-ițhuccu, yețɛeggiḍ alamma ffɣent-ed tkufta seg imi-s, ur as-ițserriḥ ara alamma yerẓa-t akk. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:40">9:40</a> ?elleleɣ inelmaden-ik a t-ssufɣen seg-s, lameɛna ur zmiren ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:41">9:41</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenṭeq yenna : A lǧil ijehlen iɛewjen, ar melmi ara yiliɣ yid-wen, ara wen-sebṛeɣ ? Awi-d mmi-k ɣer dagi !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:42">9:42</a> Akken i d-iqeṛṛeb weqcic-nni, aṛuḥani isseglallez-it di lqaɛa armi i d-țeffɣent tkufta seg yimi-s. Sidna Ɛisa yefka lameṛ i uṛuḥani-nni iwakken a t-iffeɣ. Aqcic-nni yeḥla, Sidna Ɛisa yerra-t i baba-s.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:43">9:43</a> Lɣaci meṛṛa wehmen di tezmert n Sidi Ṛebbi. Imi tɛeǧǧben akk s wayen i gxeddem, Sidna Ɛisa yenṭeq ɣer yinelmaden-is yenna :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:44">9:44</a> ?esset-ed mliḥ i wayen ara wen-d-iniɣ tura : « Mmi-s n bunadem ad ițțusellem ger ifassen n yemdanen. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:45">9:45</a> Inelmaden-is ur fhimen ara imeslayen-agi, lmeɛna-ines tețwaffer fell-asen iwakken ur t-fehmen ara yerna kukran a t-steqsin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:46">9:46</a> Inelmaden țmeslayen wway gar-asen, țmesteqsayen anwa i d ameqqran deg-sen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:47">9:47</a> Sidna Ɛisa yeẓran ayen țxemmimen deg ulawen-nsen, ikker yeddem-ed yiwen weqcic isbedd-it zdat-es, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:48">9:48</a> yenna-yasen : Win iqeblen aqcic am wagi ɣef ddemma n yisem-iw d nekk i geqbel, win i yi-qeblen, yeqbel win i yi-d iceggɛen. Win yessimẓiyen iman-is gar-awen d nețța i d ameqqran.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:49">9:49</a> Yuḥenna yenna i Sidna Ɛisa : A Sidi, neẓra yiwen wergaz yessuffuɣ leǧnun s yisem-ik, nebɣa a s-neqḍeɛ imi ur k-itbiɛ ara am nukni. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:50">9:50</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Ur s-țțagit ara ! Win ur wen-d neffiɣ ara d aɛdaw, yid-wen i gella !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:51">9:51</a> Mi qṛib a d-awḍen wussan i deg ara yețwarfed ɣer igenwan, Sidna Ɛisa yeqsed ad iṛuḥ ɣer temdint n Lquds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:52">9:52</a> Yessezwer imceggɛen zdat-es iwakken a s-heggin ayen ilaqen. Kecmen ɣer yiwet n taddart n yisamariyen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:53">9:53</a> lameɛna ugin ad stṛeḥben yis imi slan ɣer temdint n Lquds i gteddu.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:54">9:54</a> Yeɛqub d Yuḥenna mi ẓran ayagi, nnan : A Sidi, tebɣiḍ a nefk lameṛ i tmes n yigenni a d-teɣli fell-asen a ten tessenger ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:55">9:55</a> Sidna Ɛisa yezzi ɣuṛ-sen, iɛeggeḍ fell-asen yenna : Acuɣeṛ i tețxemmimem akka ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:56">9:56</a> Mmi-s n bunadem ur d-yusi ara ad issenger imdanen lameɛna yusa-d a ten-isellek. Dɣa ṛuḥen ɣer taddart nniḍen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:57">9:57</a> Mi teddun deg webrid, yiwen wergaz yenna i Sidna Ɛisa : A Sidi, anda teddiḍ ad dduɣ !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:58">9:58</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Uccanen ɣuṛ-sen lɣiṛan, ifṛax n yigenni sɛan leɛcuc, ma d Mmi-s n bunadem ur yesɛi ara anda ara yessers aqeṛṛuy-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:59">9:59</a> Dɣa yenna i yiwen nniḍen : Eyya-d aț-țedduḍ yid-i. Yerra-yas : A Sidi, serreḥ-iyi uqbel ad ṛuḥeɣ ad meḍleɣ baba. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:60">9:60</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Eǧǧ wid yemmuten ad meḍlen lmegtin-nsen, ma d kečč eyya-d aț-țbecṛeḍ tageldit n Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:61">9:61</a> Wayeḍ yenṭeq yenna-yas : Ad dduɣ yid-ek a Sidi, lameɛna eǧǧ-iyi ad ṛuḥeɣ ad sellmeɣ ɣef wat wexxam-iw.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:62">9:62</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Kra n win yeṭṭfen lmaɛun, yețmuqul ɣer deffir, ur yenfiɛ ara i tgelda n Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:1">10:1</a> Syenna, Sidna Ɛisa yextaṛ-ed tnin usebɛin yinelmaden nniḍen, iceggeɛ-iten sin sin ad ṛuḥen ɣer mkul taddart d mkul amkan anda ilaq ad iṛuḥ ula d nețța. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:2">10:2</a> Yenna-yasen : Tamegra meqqṛet meɛna drus yixeddamen i gellan. Dɛut ihi ɣer Bab n tmegra iwakken a d-iceggeɛ ixeddamen ɣer yigran-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:3">10:3</a> Atan a kkun-ceggɛeɣ am izamaren ger wuccanen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:4">10:4</a> Ur țțawit yid-wen idrimen, ur țțawit aɛwin neɣ tayuga nniḍen n yerkasen. Deg webrid-nwen ur sṛuḥuyet ara lweqt di sslam. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:5">10:5</a> Kra n wexxam ara tkecmem init : sslam n Ṛebbi fell-awen ay at wexxam !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:6">10:6</a> Ma yella dinna walebɛaḍ d imhenni, sslam-nwen ad yers fell-as, neɣ m'ulac lehna-nwen aț-țeqqim ɣuṛ-wen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:7">10:7</a> Qqimet deg wexxam-nni, ččet swet ayen ara wen-d-fken, axaṭer axeddam yuklal lexlaṣ-is. Ur țṛuḥut ara seg wexxam ɣer wayeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:8">10:8</a> Mkul taddart ara tkecmem, ma stṛeḥben yis-wen ččet ayen ara wen-d-ssersen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:9">10:9</a> Sseḥlut imuḍan-nsen, init-asen : tageldit n Ṛebbi tewweḍ-ed ɣuṛ-wen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:10">10:10</a> Lameɛna mkul taddart ara tkecmem m'ur stṛeḥben ara yis-wen, effɣet ɣer yizenqan-nsen init : </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:11">10:11</a> « a nezwi ula d aɣebbaṛ n taddart-nwen i d-ineṭḍen deg yiḍaṛṛen nneɣ, meɛna ḥṣut belli tageldit n Ṛebbi tewweḍ-ed ɣuṛ-wen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:12">10:12</a> Aql-i nniɣ-awen, ass n lḥisab taddart-agi aț-țețțuɛaqeb akteṛ n temdint n ?udum. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:13">10:13</a> A nnger-im a tamdint n Kurazim, a nnger-im a Bitsayda ! A lukan lbeṛhanat yețwaxedmen deg kkunt țwaxedmen di temdinin n ?ur akk-d Sidun, tili imezdaɣ-nsent acḥal aya segmi sburren ticekkaṛin n leḥzen, sexnunnsen iman-nsen deg iɣiɣden iwakken a d-beggnen belli ndemmen, uɣalen-d ɣer webrid.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:14">10:14</a> ?ef wannect-agi, ass n lḥisab a ț-țețțuɛaqbemt akteṛ n temdinin n ?ur d Sidun.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:15">10:15</a> I kemmini a tamdint n Kafernaḥum, tɣileḍ aț-țaliḍ ɣer yigenni ? Xaṭi ! ?er tesraft lqayen n laxeṛt ara tețwaḍeggṛeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:16">10:16</a> Win i wen-ismeḥsisen ismeḥsis-iyi-d i nekk. Win ur kkun-neqbil d nekk ur geqbil ara, win ur iyi-neqbil ara, ur iqbil ara Win i yi-d-iceggɛen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:17">10:17</a> Tnin usebɛin-nni yinelmaden uɣalen-d ččuṛen d lfeṛḥ, nnan-as : A Sidi, ula d leǧnun țțagaden-aɣ s yisem-ik.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:18">10:18</a> Yenna-yasen : Walaɣ Cciṭan yeɣli-d am lebṛaq seg yigenni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:19">10:19</a> Slet-ed i wayen ara wen-iniɣ : ț-țideț fkiɣ-awen tazmert s wayes ara tṛekḍem izerman ț-țɣerdmiwin, aț-țmeḥqem lǧehd n weɛdaw yerna ulac ayen ara wen-izemren ;  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:20">10:20</a> lameɛna ur feṛṛḥet ara imi i tḥekkmem ɣef leǧnun, feṛḥet imi ismawen-nwen țwajerden deg igenwan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:21">10:21</a> Imiren kan, Sidna Ɛisa yeččuṛ-it Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen s lfeṛḥ, yenṭeq yenna : Tanemmirt a Baba, kečč yellan d Bab n yigenwan d lqaɛa, imi ayen akk i teffreḍ ɣef lɛuqal d yimusnawen tbeggneḍ-t-id i yimecṭuḥen. Tanemmirt a Baba Ṛebbi aḥnin axaṭer d wagi i d lebɣi-k.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:22">10:22</a> Baba yerra kullec ger ifassen-iw. Yiwen ur yeẓri d acu-yi anagar Baba Ṛebbi, yiwen ur issin Baba Ṛebbi anagar Mmi-s akk-d win iwumi yebɣa Mmi-s a t-id-isbeggen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:23">10:23</a> Dɣa yezzi ɣer yinelmaden-is yenna-yasen : Amarezg n wid iwalan ayen tețwalim ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:24">10:24</a> Aql-i nniɣ-awen : aṭas n lenbiya d waṭas n yigelliden i gebɣan ad ẓren ayen i tẓerrem ur t-ẓrin, i gebɣan ad slen ayen i tsellem ur t-slin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:25">10:25</a> Ikred yiwen umusnaw n ccariɛa yebɣan ad ijeṛṛeb Sidna Ɛisa, yenna yas : A Sidi, d acu ara xedmeɣ iwakken ad sɛuɣ tudert n dayem ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:26">10:26</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : D acu yuran di ccariɛa n Musa ? D acu i tfehmeḍ deg-s mi ț-teɣriḍ ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:27">10:27</a> Yerra-yas-d :  Aț-țḥemmleḍ Sidi Ṛebbi s wul-ik d ṛṛuḥ-ik, s wayen yellan di tezmert-ik akk-d lɛeqliya-k. Aț-țḥemmleḍ daɣen wiyaḍ am yiman-ik . </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:28">10:28</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Ayen akka i d-tenniḍ ț-țideț, exdem akka aț-țesɛuḍ tudert n dayem !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:29">10:29</a> Lɛalem-nni n ccariɛa yebɣan ad yefk lḥeqq i yiman-is, yenna i Sidna Ɛisa : Anwa-ten wiyaḍ-agi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:30">10:30</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Yiwen wergaz iṣubb-ed si temdint n Lquds ɣer temdint n Yiriku ; sqaṭɛen-as yimakaren ɛerran-t rnan wten-t, ṛuḥen ǧǧan-t ur yemmut ur iddir. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:31">10:31</a> Iɛedda-d syenna yiwen lmuqeddem n ccariɛa ; mi t-iwala iwwet iɛedda si tama nniḍen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:32">10:32</a> Iɛedda-d daɣen seg webrid-nni yiwen wemṛabeḍ n at Lewwi, iwala-t, ikemmel abrid-is iṛuḥ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:33">10:33</a> Ataya yiwen wubeṛṛani n tmurt n Samarya, iwweḍ-ed ɣuṛ-es, mi t-iwala iɣaḍ-it.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:34">10:34</a> Iqeṛṛeb ɣuṛ-es, idhen leǧruḥ-is s zzit d ccṛab, icudd iten ; isserkeb-it ɣef zzayla-s, yewwi-t ɣer yiwen wexxam n yemsafren, ilha-d yid-es. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:35">10:35</a> Azekka-nni yefka sin yiṣurdiyen i bab n wexxam-nni, yenna-yas : « Bedd ɣuṛ-es, ayen ara tṣeṛṛfeḍ n zzyada fell-as, a k-t-id-kemmleɣ asm'ara d-uɣaleɣ. » </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:36">10:36</a> Di tlata-agi, anwa i gḥemmlen am yiman-is argaz-agi yețțuɛerran ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:37">10:37</a> Amusnaw n ccariɛa yerra-yas : D win akken iḥunnen fell-as, i s ixedmen lxiṛ. Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Ṛuḥ ula d kečč exdem akken.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:38">10:38</a> Deg webrid-nsen ɣer temdint n Lquds, Sidna Ɛisa yekcem ɣer yiwet n taddart. Yiwet n tmeṭṭut isem is Marṭa teɛṛeḍ-it ɣer wexxam-nsen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:39">10:39</a> Tesɛa weltma-s isem-is Meryem, teqqim-ed ɣer iḍaṛṛen n Sidna Ɛisa, tesmeḥsis i wawal-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:40">10:40</a> Marṭa tqeddec yečča-ț ccɣel, tusa-d ɣer Sidna Ɛisa tenna-yas : A Sidi, ur ak-tewqiɛ ara lmeɛna imi iyi-teǧǧa weltma ad qedceɣ weḥd-i ? Ini-yas aț-țekker a yi-tɛiwen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:41">10:41</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : A Maṛta, tețḥebbiṛeḍ tețqelliqeḍ iman-im ɣef waṭas n tɣawsiwin ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:42">10:42</a> lameɛna yiwet kan i gṣeḥḥan ! Meryem textaṛ ayen ilaqen yerna yiwen ur as-t-ițekkes.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:1">11:1</a> Yiwen wass, Sidna Ɛisa yețẓalla deg yiwen wemkan. Mi gfukk, yiwen seg yinelmaden-is yenna-yas : A Sidi, selmed-aɣ amek ara neẓẓal akken yesselmed Yeḥya i yinelmaden-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:2">11:2</a> Yenna-yasen : M'ara tẓallem, init : A Baba Ṛebbi, isem-ik ad ițwaqeddes, lḥekma n tgeldit-ik a d-tas.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:3">11:3</a> Yal ass efk-aɣ-d aɣṛum-nneɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:4">11:4</a> Semmeḥ-aɣ ddnubat-nneɣ akken i nețsamaḥ ula d nukkni i wid i ɣ-ixedmen cceṛ, ur aɣ-țaǧǧa ara a neɣli deg wujeṛṛeb.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:5">11:5</a> Yenna-yasen daɣen : Ma yella yiwen deg-wen yesɛa aḥbib, iṛuḥ ɣuṛ-es di țnaṣfa n yiḍ a s-yini : « Ay aḥbib ṛḍel-iyi-d tlata teḥbulin n weɣṛum , </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:6">11:6</a> atan yusa-yi-d yiwen weḥbib i geṭṭef webrid, ur sɛiɣ d acu ara s-d-sserseɣ. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:7">11:7</a> Ma yerra-yas-d si zdaxel n wexxam : « Ur iyi-țɛețțib ara, tawwurt tsekkeṛ, nekk d warraw-iw aql-aɣ neṭṭes, ur zmireɣ ara a d-kkreɣ iwakken a k-d-fkeɣ aɣṛum. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:8">11:8</a> A wen-d-iniɣ : ma yeɛdez ur yebɣi ara a d-yekker ɣuṛ-es ɣas akken d aḥbib-is, a d-ikker a s-d-yefk ayen akk i s-issuter axaṭer yusa-d ɣuṛ es di țnaṣfa n yiḍ yeṛṛez-as aqeṛṛuy-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:9">11:9</a> Ma d nekk nniɣ-awen : ssutret a wen-d-ițunefk, qellbet aț-țafem, sqerbebbet di tewwurt a wen-d-ldin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:10">11:10</a> Axaṭer kra n win yessuturen a s-d ițunefk, win ițqelliben ad yaf, win yesṭebṭuben a s-d-ldin tawwurt.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:11">11:11</a> Anwa deg-wen ara yefken i mmi-s adɣaɣ ma yessuter-as aɣṛum ? Neɣ a s-yefk azrem ma yessuter-as aslem ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:12">11:12</a> Neɣ ma yessuter-as tamellalt a s-yefk tiɣirdemt ?  </p>
