 <p><a name="an_11:13">11:13</a> Ma yella kunwi yellan d imcumen tessnem aț-țefkem ayen yelhan i warraw-nwen, amek Baba-twen yellan deg igenni ur d-ițțak ara Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen i wid i s-t-issuturen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:14">11:14</a> Yiwen wass ikker Sidna Ɛisa yessuffeɣ lǧen yesgugmen yiwen wergaz. Mi t-iffeɣ lǧen, argaz-nni yebda iheddeṛ ; lɣaci meṛṛa wehmen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:15">11:15</a> Lameɛna kra deg-sen nnan : « D Balzabul iḥekmen ɣef leǧnun i s-yefkan tazmert akken a ten issuffeɣ. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:16">11:16</a> Kra nniḍen bɣan a t-jeṛṛben, ssutren-as yiwen n lbeṛhan ara d-yasen seg yigenni. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:17">11:17</a> Sidna Ɛisa yessnen ixemmimen-nsen yenna yasen : Yal tagelda i deg ara țnaɣen imezdaɣ-is wway gar-asen tețțeddu ɣer nnger, ixxamen-is ad ɣlin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:18">11:18</a> Ma yella Cciṭan yețnaɣ d yiman-is amek ara tdum tgelda-s ? Teqqaṛem s Balzabul i ssufuɣeɣ leǧnun ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:19">11:19</a> Ma yella nekk s Balzabul i ten-ssufuɣeɣ, anwa ihi i sen-ițțaken tazmert i yinelmaden-nwen iwakken a ten-ssuffuɣen ? Daymi d nutni ara kkun-iḥasben.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:20">11:20</a> Lameɛna ma yella s ufus n Ṛebbi i ten-ssuffuɣeɣ, ațan ihi tageldit n Ṛebbi tewweḍ-ed ɣuṛ-wen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:21">11:21</a> Argaz iǧehden yesɛan leslaḥ, ițɛassan ɣef wexxam-is, ṛṛezq-is ad yili di laman.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:22">11:22</a> Ma yusa-d ɣuṛ-es yiwen iǧehden akteṛ-is iɣleb-it, a s-ikkes leslaḥ ɣef wacu yețkel, ad yernu ad ifṛeq i wiyaḍ ayen akk yesɛa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:23">11:23</a> Win ur nelli ara yid-i, d axṣim-iw ; win ur njemmeɛ ara yid-i, yețḍeggiɛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:24">11:24</a> M'ara yeffeɣ uṛuḥani seg yiwen wergaz, ad iṛuḥ ɣer yimukan yexlan akken ad iqelleb ɣef ṛṛaḥa. M'ur yufi ara, ad yini : « ad uɣaleɣ ɣer tnezduɣt-iw ansi i d-ffɣeɣ. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:25">11:25</a> M'ara yaweḍ ɣer tnezduɣt-nni, a ț-yaf zeddiget, tqeɛɛed ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:26">11:26</a> imiren ad iṛuḥ a d-yawi sebɛa yiṛuḥaniyen nniḍen iweɛṛen akteṛ-is, ad kecmen ad zedɣen deg-s ; s wakka lḥala n wergaz-nni aț-țenṭeṛ akteṛ n tikkelt tamezwarut.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:27">11:27</a> Mi d-yenna Sidna Ɛisa ayagi, yiwet n tmeṭṭut tenṭeq-ed s ṣṣut ɛlayen si ger n lɣaci tenna-yas : ?-țaseɛdit tmeṭṭut i k-id-yurwen, i k-issuṭṭḍen !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:28">11:28</a> Lameɛna nețța yerra-yas : Iseɛdiyen, d wid ismeḥsisen i wawal n Ṛebbi, yerna ḥerzen-t.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:29">11:29</a> Mi d-innejmaɛ ɣuṛ-es waṭas n lɣaci, Sidna Ɛisa yekker yenna-yasen : Lǧil-agi d lǧil amcum, yessutur lbeṛhan ! Ur as-d-ițunefkay ara lbeṛhan anagar win n nnbi Yunes !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:30">11:30</a> Axaṭer akken yella nnbi Yunes d lbeṛhan i yimezdaɣ n temdint n Ninebi, ara yili Mmi-s n bunadem d lbeṛhan i lǧil-agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:31">11:31</a> Ass n lḥisab tagellit n tmurt n usammer a d-tekker ɣer yemdanen n lǧil-agi a ten-tesseḍlem imi nețțat tusa-d seg yixef n ddunit iwakken aț-țsel i tmusni n ugellid Sliman. Atah yella gar-awen win yugaren agellid Sliman !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:32">11:32</a> Ass n lḥisab a d-kkren daɣen imezdaɣ n temdint n Ninebi ɣer lǧil-agi a ten-sḍelmen, axaṭer nutni uɣalen-d ɣer webrid mi sen-ibecceṛ nnbi Yunes. Kunwi tesɛam dagi gar-awen win yugaren nnbi Yunes !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:33">11:33</a> Yiwen ur iceɛɛel taftilt iwakken a ț-iffer neɣ akken a ț-iɣumm s lḥila, lameɛna a ț-issers ɣef lmeṣbeḥ iwakken kra n win ara d-ikecmen ad iwali tafat.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:34">11:34</a> Tiṭ ț-țaftilt n wemdan. Ma yella tiṭ-ik tṣeḥḥa aț-țiliḍ di tafat, meɛna ma tedderɣel aț-țiliḍ di ṭṭlam.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:35">11:35</a> ?ader ihi aț-țuɣal tafat yellan deg-k d ṭṭlam. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:36">11:36</a> Ma telliḍ di tafat s lekmal-ik, ur yețțili ara deg-k ṭṭlam, aț-țiliḍ di tafat am teftilt m'ara d-cceɛceɛ fell-ak.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:37">11:37</a> Mi gfukk Sidna Ɛisa ameslay, iɛreḍ-it yiwen wufarizi ɣeṛ imensi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:38">11:38</a> Afarizi-nni yewhem mi gwala Sidna Ɛisa ur issared ara uqbel ad yečč, akken tella di lɛadda-nsen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:39">11:39</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Kunwi s yifariziyen tessiridem taqbuct d uḍebṣi s wufella kan ma zdaxel n wulawen teččuṛem d ṭṭmeɛ akk-d ddɣel.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:40">11:40</a> A wid iɣeflen ! Eɛni win i d ixelqen ayen yellan s wufella, mačči d nețța i d-ixelqen ayen n daxel ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:41">11:41</a> Fket lweɛda s wulawen-nwen, imiren kullec ad awen-yeṣfu.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:42">11:42</a> A nnger-nwen ay ifariziyen ! Kunwi yețɛecciṛen nneɛneɛ d uwermi d wayen i d-ițemɣayen di tebḥirt, ma d lḥeqq d leḥmala n Sidi Ṛebbi tețțarram-ten ɣer deffir ; d annect-agi i gezwaren mbla ma tețțum ayen nniḍen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:43">11:43</a> A nnger-nwen ay ifariziyen ! Tḥemmlem imukan imezwura di leǧwameɛ, tḥemmlem ad țsellimen fell-awen yemdanen deg iberdan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:44">11:44</a> A nnger-nwen, kunwi yecban iẓekwan i gɣumm wakal, ur d-nețban ara, ɛeffsen-ten yemdanen ur d-wwin s lexbaṛ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:45">11:45</a> Yenṭeq yiwen lɛalem n ccariɛa, yenna-yas : A Sidi, atan tregmeḍ-aɣ ula d nukkni s wayen i d-tenniḍ akka !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:46">11:46</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : A nnger-nwen ula d kunwi a lɛulama n ccariɛa ! Tețɛebbim i wiyaḍ tiɛekkmin ẓẓayen, ma d kunwi ur tent-tețnalem ara ula s yiwen uḍaḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:47">11:47</a> A tawaɣit-nwen ! Lejdud-nwen nɣan lenbiya, kunwi tbennum-asen iẓekwan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:48">11:48</a> S wakka i d-tesbegnem belli tqeblem ayen i xedmen yerna tețkemmilem di tikli-nsen ; axaṭer nutni nɣan-ten, kunwi tbennum-asen iẓekwan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:49">11:49</a> ?ef wayagi Sidi Ṛebbi yeẓran kullec yenna : a sen-ceggɛeɣ lenbiya d ṛṛusul, kra a ten-nɣen kra a ten qehṛen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:50">11:50</a> Daymi lǧil-agi ad ițțuḥaseb ɣef tazzla n yidammen n lenbiya seg wasmi i d-texleq ddunit ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:51">11:51</a> seg yidammen n Habil mmi-s n Adem armi d idammen n Zakarya i nɣan ger udekkan n iseflawen d lǧameɛ iqedsen. Lǧil-agi ad ițțuḥaseb ɣef ayagi meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:52">11:52</a> A tawaɣit-nwen a lɛulama n ccariɛa ! Teṭṭfem tasaruț n tmusni, ur tekcimem kunwi, ur teǧǧim ad kecmen wid yebɣan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:53">11:53</a> Mi geffeɣ Sidna Ɛisa, lɛulama n ccariɛa d ifariziyen ḥeṛsen-t iwakken a d-immeslay ɣef waṭas n tɣawsiwin nniḍen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:54">11:54</a> țqelliben amek ara t-id-sseɣlin deg wawal.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:1">12:1</a> Di teswiɛt-nni kan, lɣaci yennejmaɛ-ed s luluf armi țemyeɛfasen. Sidna Ɛisa yenna i yinelmaden-is : ?adret iman-nwen ɣef temtunt ( iɣes ) n yifariziyen, axaṭer d at sin wudmawen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:2">12:2</a> Kra n wayen iɣummen a d-iban, kra n wayen yeffren ad yemẓer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:3">12:3</a> Ayen i thedṛem di ṭṭlam a t-slen di tafat, ayen i tennam ɣer umeẓẓuɣ di texxamt ad ițțuberreḥ deg yizenqan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:4">12:4</a> A wen-d-iniɣ i kunwi yellan d iḥbiben-iw : ur țțagadet ara wid ineqqen lǧețța, sennig lmut ur zmiren ad xedmen acemma nniḍen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:5">12:5</a> A wen-d-iniɣ anwa i glaq aț- țaaggadem : aggadet win izemren a kkun-ikkes si ddunit yerna a kkun-iḍeggeṛ ɣer ǧahennama. Atan nniɣ-awen-t-id, d nețța i glaq aț- țaggadem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:6">12:6</a> D acu i swan xemsa iẓiwcen ? Anaɣ sin iṣurdiyen kan ! Lameɛna Sidi Ṛebbi ur itețțu ula d yiwen deg-sen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:7">12:7</a> Ula d anẓaden n iqeṛṛay-nwen țwaḥesben yiwen yiwen. Ur țțagadet ara ihi, teswam akteṛ n iẓiwcen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:8">12:8</a> A wen-d-iniɣ : kra n win ara d-icehden zdat yemdanen belli yumen yis-i, Mmi-s n bunadem ur t-inekkeṛ ara zdat lmalayekkat, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:9">12:9</a> ma d win ara yi-nekṛen zdat yemdanen, ula d nekk a t-nekkṛeɣ zdat lmalayekkat n Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:10">12:10</a> Kra n win ara yewten di Mmi-s n bunadem a s-ițusemmeḥ, ma d win ara iregmen Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen ulac fell-as ssmaḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:11">12:11</a> M'ara kkun-awin ad ḥekmen fell-awen di leǧwameɛ zdat lecyux d lḥekkam, ur țxemmimet ara amek ara tsellkem iman-nwen neɣ ɣef wayen ara d-tinim, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:12">12:12</a> axaṭer d Ṛṛuḥ iqedsen ara wen-d-ifken di teswiɛt-nni ayen ilaqen a t-id-tinim.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:13">12:13</a> Yiwen wergaz inṭeq-ed si ger n lɣaci yenna i Sidna Ɛisa : A Sidi, ini-yas i gma ad ibḍu yid-i lweṛt i d-iǧǧa baba-tneɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:14">12:14</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Ay argaz, anwa i yi-sbedden iwakken ad bḍuɣ gar-awen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:15">12:15</a> Dɣa yenna i lɣaci : ?adret iman-nwen ɣef ṭṭmeɛ imi tudert n wemdan ur d-tekki ara seg wayen yesɛa ɣas akken di rrbeḥ ameqqran i gella.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:16">12:16</a> Imiren yewwi-yasen-d lemtel agi : Yiwen umeṛkanti, yesɛa tamurt tefka-d aṭas n lɣella. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:17">12:17</a> Ixemmem deg iman-is, yenna : « amek ara xedmeɣ imi ur sɛiɣ ara amkan anda ara jemɛeɣ leṛẓaq-iw ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:18">12:18</a> Ad huddeɣ ikuffan-iw, ad bnuɣ wiyaḍ d imeqqranen iwakken ad jemɛeɣ irden-iw d leṛẓaq-iw meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:19">12:19</a> Imiren ad iniɣ i yiman-iw : « atan tesxezneḍ leṛẓaq i waṭas n iseggasen ; steɛfu tura, ečč, sew tezhuḍ. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:20">12:20</a> Lameɛna Sidi Ṛebbi yenna yas-d : « a win iɣeflen ! Iḍ-agi ad a k-ddmeɣ ṛṛuḥ-ik ! Ayen meṛṛa i tjemɛeḍ, iwumi ara d-yeqqim ? »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:21">12:21</a> Akka i tdeṛṛu d win ijemɛen leṛẓaq i yiman-is, wala ad ixdem ɣef laxeṛt-is, ad yili d ameṛkanti ɣer Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:22">12:22</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna daɣen i yinelmaden-is : ?ef wayagi i wen-d-qqaṛeɣ ur țḥebbiṛet ara ɣef tudert-nwen, ɣef wayen ara teččem d wayen ara telsem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:23">12:23</a> Axaṭer tudert-nwen tugar lqut, lǧețța-nwen tugar llebsa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:24">12:24</a> Walit tigerfiwin , ur zerrɛent ur meggrent , ur sɛint akufi ur sɛint acbayli meɛna Sidi Ṛebbi ițɛeyyic itent. Acḥal teswam akteṛ n yefṛax n igenni ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:25">12:25</a> Anwa deg-wen i gzemren s uḥebbeṛ ad yessiɣzef leɛmeṛ-is ula s yiwen n wass ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:26">12:26</a> Imi ur tezmirem ara i tɣawsiwin timecṭuḥin, acuɣeṛ i tețḥebbiṛem ɣef wayen nniḍen ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:27">12:27</a> Walit amek gemmun ijeǧǧigen n lexla ! Ur țellmen ur ẓeṭṭen ! Atan qqaṛeɣ-awen : ula d agellid Sliman s yiman-is di ccan-is, ur yelsi am yiwen seg yijeǧǧigen-agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:28">12:28</a> Ma yella Sidi Ṛebbi yeslusu akka leḥcic yellan ass-agi di lexla, azekka ad iṛeɣ di tmes, amek ur kkun-islusu ara kunwi, ay imdanen ixuṣṣen di liman !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:29">12:29</a> Ur țḥebbiṛet ara ihi ! Ur țqellibet ara ɣef wayen ara teččem d wayen ara teswem, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:30">12:30</a> axaṭer d imdanen ur nețțamen ara s Ṛebbi i gețqelliben ɣef wayagi meṛṛa. Baba-twen yellan deg yigenwan yeẓra ayen teḥwaǧem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:31">12:31</a> Qellbet axiṛ ɣef tgeldit n Ṛebbi, ayen nniḍen meṛṛa d nețța ara wen-t-id ifken.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:32">12:32</a> Ur țțagad ara a taqeḍɛit illan tamecṭuḥt, axaṭer iɛǧeb-as i Baba Ṛebbi a wen-d-yefk tageldit-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:33">12:33</a> Zzenzet ayen tesɛam, tsedqem-t. Heggit i yiman-nwen deg yigenwan agerruj ur nkeffu, ur nrekku, dinna ulac imakaren ara t-yakren, ulac ibeɛɛac ara t-iččen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:34">12:34</a> Axaṭer anda yella ugerruj-ik, dinna ara yili wul-ik.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:35">12:35</a> Heggit iman-nwen, ɛiwzet, beggset ɣef yiman-nwen tceɛlem tiftilin-nwen !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:36">12:36</a> Ilit am wid yețṛaǧun amɛellem nsen ara d-yuɣalen si tmeɣṛa ; akken kan ara d-yesqeṛbeb a s-ldin tawwurt.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:37">12:37</a> Amarezg n yiqeddacen-agi ara d-yaf wemɛellem-nsen ɛawzen. A wen-d iniɣ tideț, ad ibeddel llebsa, a ten isɣim ɣer ṭṭabla iwakken a sen-yefk ad ččen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:38">12:38</a> Ma yewweḍ-ed di țnaṣfa n yiḍ neɣ akteṛ, amarezg-nsen ma yufa-ten-id mazal țṛaǧun-t !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:39">12:39</a> Fehmet ayagi : lemmer yeẓra bab n wexxam lweqt i deg ara d-yas umakar, tili a t-iɛass ur t-ițțaǧa ara ad ikcem axxam-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:40">12:40</a> Heggit iman-nwen ula d kunwi imi di lweqt i ɣef ur tebnim (tedmim) ara a d-yas Mmi-s n bunadem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:41">12:41</a> Buṭrus inṭeq yenna-yas : A Sidi, i nukkni iwumi d-tenniḍ lemtel-agi neɣ i lɣaci meṛṛa ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:42">12:42</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Anwa i d lewkil iḥeṛcen i ɣef yella lețkal, ara iwekkel bab n wexxam ɣef wayla-s, iwakken ad ifṛeq i yiqeddacen amur-nsen n yirden di lweqt ilaqen ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:43">12:43</a> Amarezg n wuqeddac agi ara d-yaf bab-is ibedd ɣer cceɣl-is ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:44">12:44</a> A wen-d-iniɣ tideț, a t iwekkel ɣef wayen akk yesɛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:45">12:45</a> Lameɛna aqeddac-nni ma yeqqaṛ deg wul-is : « amɛellem-iw iɛeṭṭel ur d yuɣal ara» ! Yebda iḥeqqeṛ iqeddacen ț-țqeddacin, yekkat-iten, iteț itess alamma yeskkeṛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:46">12:46</a> A d-yas umɛellem-is deg wass i ɣef ur yebni ara, di lweqt ur yessin ara, a t-iɛaqeb s lmut akken țțuɛaqben wid iɛuṣan Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:47">12:47</a> Aqeddac yessnen lebɣi n bab-is yerna ur t-ixdim ara, ad yečč tiɣṛit tameqqrant, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:48">12:48</a> ma d win ur nessin ara lebɣi n bab-is, ixdem ayen yuklalen tiɣṛit, ad yečč tiɣṛit tamecṭuḥt. Win iwumi nefka aṭas a s-nessuter aṭas, ma d win i ɣef nețkel aṭas a neṛǧu deg-s akteṛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:49">12:49</a> Usiɣ-ed a d-awiɣ yiwet n tmes ɣer ddunit ! Acḥal ɣeṣbeɣ melmi ara tecɛel ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:50">12:50</a> Yella yiwen n weɣḍas i yi-țṛaǧun... D leɛtab ameqqran yerna ɣeṣbeɣ melmi ara d-yas wass-nni !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:51">12:51</a> Tɣilem d lehna i d-wwiɣ ɣer ddunit ? Xaṭi, d beṭṭu i d-wwiɣ !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:52">12:52</a> Sya ɣer zdat ma llan xemsa deg yiwen wexxam, ad bḍun ; tlata a d-kkren ɣer sin, sin a d-kkren ɣer tlata.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:53">12:53</a> Ababat a d-innaɣ d mmi-s, mmi-s a d-yekker ɣer baba-s ; tayemmaț aț-țennaɣ d yelli-s, yelli-s akk-d yemma-s ; tamɣaṛt aț-țennaɣ ț-țeslit-is, tislit akk-d temɣaṛt-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:54">12:54</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna daɣen i lɣaci : M'ara twalim asigna yekka-d si lɣeṛb, teqqaṛem atan a d-tewwet lehwa ; d ayen i gdeṛṛun.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:55">12:55</a> M'ara d-iṣuḍ waḍu seg usammer teqqaṛem ad iḥmu lḥal ; d ayen i d-ideṛṛun daɣen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:56">12:56</a> Ay at sin wudmawen ! Imi tessnem aț-țɛeqlem lḥal n yigenni d lqaɛa, amek ur tezmirem ara aț-țɛeqlem zzman-agi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:57">12:57</a> Acuɣeṛ ur tețmeyyizem ara s yiman-nwen ɣef wayen yellan d lḥeqq ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:58">12:58</a> M'ara k-yessiweḍ wexṣim-ik ɣer ccṛeɛ, eɛṛeḍ a ț-tefruḍ yid-es uqbel aț-țawḍem ɣer dinna, neɣ m'ulac a k-yawi ɣer lḥakem, lḥakem a k-yefk i uɛessas, aɛessas a k-iḍeggeṛ ɣer lḥebs.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:59">12:59</a> A k-d-iniɣ : ur d-tețțeffɣeḍ ara syenna alamma txellṣeḍ aṣurdi aneggaru n ṭlaba-inek.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:1">13:1</a> Di lweqt-nni, kra n yemdanen usan-d a s-ḥkun i Sidna Ɛisa ɣef kra n yergazen n tmurt n Jlili i genɣa Bilaṭus, d wamek issexleḍ dammen-nsen d idammen n iseflawen nsen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:2">13:2</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen : Tɣilem belli imezdaɣ-agi n Jlili ițțuɛetben akka d imednuben akteṛ n wiyaḍ ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:3">13:3</a> Xaṭi, meɛna a wen-d-iniɣ : m'ur tbeddlem ara tikli aț-țemtem ula d kunwi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:4">13:4</a> Neɣ am tmenṭac-nni yergazen yemmuten mi d-yeɣli fell-asen ṣṣuṛ n Silwi, tɣilem d imednuben akteṛ n imezdaɣ nniḍen n temdint n Lquds ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:5">13:5</a> Xaṭi, meɛna nniɣ-awen : m'ur tbeddlem ara tikli aț-țemtem ula d kunwi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:6">13:6</a> Yewwi-yasen-d lemtel-agi : Yiwen wergaz yesɛa taneqleț teẓẓa deg yiger n tẓurin. Yusa-d iwakken a d-ikkes tibexsisin lameɛna ur yufi ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:7">13:7</a> Yenna i uxeddam n yiger-nni : tlata n yiseggasen aya nekk țțaseɣ ed iwakken a d-kkseɣ lexṛif si tneqleț agi meɛna ur d-țțafeɣ ara, gzem-iț ihi ! Acuɣeṛ ara teṭṭef akal mbla nnfeɛ ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:8">13:8</a> Axeddam-nni yerra-yas : a Sidi, eǧǧ-iț aț-țernu aseggas-a ; aț-țneqceɣ, a s-rreɣ leɣbaṛ, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:9">13:9</a> sya d asawen ma tefka-d lfakya eǧǧ-iț, m'ulac qeleɛ -iț.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:10">13:10</a> Sidna Ɛisa yesselmad deg yiwen n lǧameɛ deg wass n westeɛfu. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:11">13:11</a> Tella dinna yiwet n tmeṭṭut ihelken tmenṭac yiseggasen aya ; d yiwen uṛuḥani i ț-ikerfen ur tezmir ara aț-țesbedd lqedd-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:12">13:12</a> Mi ț-iwala Sidna Ɛisa, iluɛa-ț yenna-yas : A tameṭṭut, teḥliḍ seg wekraf-im.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:13">13:13</a> Issers ifassen-is fell-as , imiren kan tesbedd lqedd-is, teḥmed Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:14">13:14</a> Ccix-nni n lǧameɛ iɣaḍ-it lḥal imi i ț-isseḥla Sidna Ɛisa deg wass n westeɛfu, yenna i lɣaci : Llan sețța wussan i deg ilaq a nexdem ; aset-ed ihi deg ussan-nni iwakken a kkun-isseḥlu mačči deg wass n westeɛfu !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:15">13:15</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Ay at sin wudmawen ! Anwa deg-wen ur d-nețserriḥ i wezger-ines neɣ i weɣyul-is iwakken a t-yawi a d-isew ɣas deg wass n westeɛfu ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:16">13:16</a> I tmeṭṭut-agi yellan si dderya n Ibṛahim, i gekref Cciṭan tmenṭac n yiseggasen aya, eɛni ur ilaq ara a s-nekkes akraf ɣas akka d ass n westeɛfu ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:17">13:17</a> Mi d-yenna imeslayen-agi, ixṣimen-is meṛṛa nneḥcamen ma d lɣaci feṛḥen s leɛǧayeb i gxeddem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:18">13:18</a> Yenna daɣen : ?er wacu i tețțemcabi tgeldit n Ṛebbi ? ?er wacu ara ț-metleɣ ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:19">13:19</a> Tețțemcabi ɣer uɛeqqa amecṭuḥ n zerriɛa n uxerḍel i geẓẓa yiwen wergaz di tebḥirt-is. Mi d-imɣi yuɣal d ttejṛa, ifṛax n igenni bnan leɛcuc deg ifurkawen-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:20">13:20</a> Yenna daɣen : ?er wacu i zemreɣ ad metleɣ tageldit n Ṛebbi ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:21">13:21</a> Tețțemcabi ɣer ciṭṭuḥ yiɣes n temtunt i d-teddem tmeṭṭut, tger-it di tlata lkilat n uwren dɣa teǧǧa-t armi yuli meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:22">13:22</a> Deg webrid-is ɣer temdint n Lquds, Sidna Ɛisa ițɛedday ɣef temdinin ț-țudrin, isselmad.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:23">13:23</a> Isteqsa-t yiwen yenna-yas : A Sidi, drus n yemdanen ara yețțuselken ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:24">13:24</a> Yenna-yasen : Qellbet amek ara tkecmem si tewwurt iḍeyqen ; a wen-d-iniɣ : aṭas ara yebɣun ad kecmen lameɛna ur țțizmiren ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:25">13:25</a> M'ara d-yekker bab n wexxam ad isekkeṛ tawwurt, wid i d-yufa lḥal di beṛṛa a d-bdun asqeṛbeb ad qqaṛen : « A Sidi ! A Sidi ! Ldi-yaɣ tawwurt» ! Nețța a wen-d-yerr : ur kkun-ssineɣ ur ẓriɣ ansi i d-tekkam !?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:26">13:26</a> Kunwi ad as-tinim : « anaɣ nečča neswa yid-ek, teslemdeḍ deg yizenqan nneɣ ! » </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:27">13:27</a> Nețța a wen-d-yerr : Nniɣ-awen ur kkun-ssineɣ ara, beɛdet akkin fell-i a kunwi ixeddmen cceṛ !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:28">13:28</a> Dinna ara yilin yimeṭṭawen d nndama tameqqrant m'ara twalim Ibṛahim, Isḥaq, Yeɛqub akk-d lenbiya di tgelda n yigenwan, ma d kunwi aț-țeqqimem di beṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:29">13:29</a> A d-asen si cceṛq d lɣeṛb, seg umalu d usammer, ad ṭṭfen imukan di tmeɣṛa n tgelda n igenwan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:30">13:30</a> Imiren ad ilin ineggura ara yuɣalen d imezwura, am akken daɣen ara yilin imezwura ara yuɣalen d ineggura.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:31">13:31</a> Di teswiɛt-nni, kra n ifariziyen usan-d ɣer Sidna Ɛisa nnan-as : Ṛuḥ tixxeṛ syagi, atan Hiṛudus ițqellib a k-ineɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:32">13:32</a> Yenna-yasen : Ṛuḥet init-as i wuccen-agi : ass-a d uzekka ad ssufɣeɣ leǧnun, ad sseḥluɣ imuḍan , ass wis tlata ad fakeɣ cceɣl-iw.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:33">13:33</a> Lameɛna ilaq ad kemmleɣ tikli-inu ass-a, azekka d sellazekka, axaṭer ur s-ilaq ara i nnbi ad immet beṛṛa n temdint n Lquds.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:34">13:34</a> A tamdint n Lquds ! A tamdint n Lquds ineqqen lenbiya, iṛeǧǧmen wid i m-d-ițwaceggɛen s ɣuṛ Ṛebbi ! Acḥal d abrid i ɛerḍeɣ a d-jemɛeɣ arraw-im am tyaziṭ i d-ijemɛen ifṛax-is seddaw wafriwen-is, lameɛna ur tebɣim ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:35">13:35</a> Atan ihi, axxam-nwen ad ixlu yerna nniɣ-awen, ur iyi-tẓerrem ara alamma d asmi ara tinim :  Ad ițțubarek win i d-yusan s yisem n Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:1">14:1</a> Yiwen wass yellan d ass n westeɛfu, Sidna Ɛisa illa yețwaɛreḍ ɣer wexxam n yiwen seg yimeqqranen n yifariziyen iwakken ad yefteṛ. Wid yellan dinna țɛassan-t d acu ara yexdem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:2">14:2</a> Yella dinna yiwen wergaz yesɛan lehlak n ubezzug. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:3">14:3</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenṭeq ɣer lɛulama n ccariɛa d yifariziyen yenna-yasen : D acu twalam ? D leḥlal win ara isseḥlun deg wass n westeɛfu neɣ ala ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:4">14:4</a> Imi yiwen deg-sen ur d-yenṭiq, Sidna Ɛisa iqeṛṛeb ɣer umuḍin-nni, yesseḥla-t, iserreḥ-as ad iṛuḥ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:5">14:5</a> Dɣa yenna i wiyaḍ : Anwa deg-wen ma yeɣli-yas mmi-s neɣ wezger-ines ɣer lbir, ur t-id-ițekkes ara ɣas ma d ass n westeɛfu ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:6">14:6</a> Yiwen ur izmir a s-d-yerr awal.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:7">14:7</a> Mi gwala wid yețwaɛerḍen bdan țextiṛin imukan imezwura, Sidna Ɛisa yewwi-yasen-d lemtel-agi yenna yasen :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:8">14:8</a> M'ara k-id-yeɛreḍ yiwen ɣer tmeɣṛa, ɣurek ur țțaṭṭaf ara amkan amezwaru ! Axaṭer yezmer ad yili yiwen ger inebgawen yesɛan leqdeṛ akteṛ-ik , </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:9">14:9</a> a d-yas win i kkun-iɛerḍen i sin a k-yini : « eǧǧ-as amkan-nni i wagi ! » Imiren aț-țenneḥcameḍ, aț-țṛuḥeḍ aț-țeṭṭfeḍ amkan aneggaru.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:10">14:10</a> Lameɛna m'ara tețwaɛeṛḍeḍ, ṭṭef amkan aneggaru iwakken m'ara d-yas win i k-id-iɛerḍen, a k-yini : « ay aḥbib ɛeddi-d ɣer zdat ! » Imiren aț-țesɛuḍ leqdeṛ zdat inebgawen meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:11">14:11</a> Axaṭer kra n win yessalayen iman-is a t-id-yessers Ṛebbi , ma d win yesrusuyen iman-is a t-yerfed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:12">14:12</a> Yenna daɣen i win i t-id iɛeṛḍen : M'ara tebɣuḍ aț-țseččeḍ, ur d-ɛeṛṛeḍ ara imdukkal-ik neɣ atmaten ik, ur d-ɛeṛṛeḍ ara imawlan-ik neɣ lǧiran-ik imeṛkantiyen ; m'ulac a k ɛerḍen ula d nutni iwakken a k-d-rren lxiṛ-ik.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:13">14:13</a> Lameɛna m'ara txedmeḍ tameɣṛa, ɛṛeḍ-ed igellilen, ineɛyuba, iquḍaren d yiderɣalen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:14">14:14</a> Ili-k di lfeṛḥ imi ur zmiren ara a k-d-rren lxiṛ-ik, axaṭer lxiṛ-ik a k-id-yuɣal asm'ara d-ḥyun wid yellan d iḥeqqiyen ɣer Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:15">14:15</a> Mi gesla i imeslayen-agi, yiwen seg inebgawen inṭeq-ed yenna i Sidna Ɛisa : Amasseɛd n win ara yeččen tiremt di tgelda n yigenwan!  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:16">14:16</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Yiwen wergaz ixdem imensi, iɛreḍ-ed aṭas lɣaci. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:17">14:17</a> Lweqt n imensi, iceggeɛ aqeddac-is iwakken ad yini i inebgawen : aset-ed ! Kullec iwjed ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:18">14:18</a> Akken ma llan ufan-d sebba. Amezwaru yenna-yas : « aql-i uɣeɣ iger, ilaq ad ṛuḥeɣ a t-id-ẓreɣ , di leɛnaya-k semmeḥ-iyi ». </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:19">14:19</a> Wayeḍ yenna-yas : « aql-i uɣeɣ-d xemsa n tyugiwin n yezgaren bɣiɣ ad ṛuḥeɣ a tent-ɛerḍeɣ, di leɛnaya-k semmeḥ iyi ». </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:20">14:20</a> Wayeḍ daɣen yenna-yas : « tura kan i zewǧeɣ, ulamek ara d aseɣ ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:21">14:21</a> Mi d-yuɣal uqeddac ɣer umɛellem-is, yeḥka-yas ayen akk i s-d-nnan. Bab n wexxam yerfa, yenna i uqeddac-is : « azzel, ṛuḥ ɣer yiberdan d yizenqan n temdint, tɛeṛḍeḍ-ed iẓawaliyen, ineɛyuba, iderɣalen d iquḍaren ». </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:22">14:22</a> Mi d-yuɣal uqeddac-nni yenna-yas : a Sidi, ayen i yi-d-tenniḍ xedmeɣ-t yerna mazal llan imukan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:23">14:23</a> Amɛellem yenna i uqeddac is : « effeɣ ɣer iberdan n tudrin d lexlawi ; wid akk ara tafeḍ, ḥṛeṣ-iten a d asen iwakken ad iččaṛ wexxam-iw. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:24">14:24</a> Atan nniɣ-awen : ula d yiwen seg wid-nni yețwaɛerḍen d imezwura ur iɛerreḍ imensi-inu.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:25">14:25</a> Aṭas n lɣaci i geddan d Sidna Ɛisa. Yezzi ɣuṛ-sen yenna-yasen :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:26">14:26</a> Kra n win ara d-yasen ɣuṛ-i, ma iḥemmel baba-s d yemma-s neɣ tameṭṭut-is d warraw-is neɣ ayetma-s d yessetma-s neɣ iḥemmel iman-is akteṛ-iw, ur izmir ara ad yili d anelmad-iw.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:27">14:27</a> Kra n win ur neqbil ara ad yeɛteb ɣef ddemma n yisem-iw yerna ur iyi-d-itbiɛ ara, ur izmir ara ad yili d anelmad-iw.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:28">14:28</a> Anwa deg-wen ma yebɣa ad ibnu lbeṛǧ, ur yețɣimi ara ad ixdem uqbel leḥsab-is, iwakken ad iẓer ma yezmer a t-ifak ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:29">14:29</a> Axaṭer ma yebda lsas yeǧǧa-t akken, kra n wid ara t-iẓren ad stehzin fell-as ad inin : </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:30">14:30</a> argaz-agi yebda lsas ur izmir ad ikemmel lebni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:31">14:31</a> Neɣ anwa agellid ara yekkren ad innaɣ d ugellid nniḍen, ur ixeddem ara uqbel leḥsab iwakken ad iẓer ma yezmer ad iqabel s ɛecṛa alaf iɛsekṛiwen win i d-iteddun ɣuṛ-es s ɛecrin alef iɛsekriwen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:32">14:32</a> Ma iwala ur s-izmir ara, ad iceggeɛ ɣuṛ-es uqbel a d-yaweḍ, iwakken ad ifru yid-es tamsalt s lehna.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:33">14:33</a> S wakka, yiwen ur yezmir ad yili d anelmad-iw m'ur yeqbil ara ad yeǧǧ ayen akk yesɛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:34">14:34</a> Lmelḥ d ayen yelhan, lameɛna ma tṛuḥ-as lbenna-s amek ara s-ț-id-nerr ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:35">14:35</a> Ur yelhi i wakal, ur yelhi i leɣbaṛ, ilaq kan a t-nḍeggeṛ ɣer beṛṛa. Win yesɛan imeẓẓuɣen isellen, isel-ed !..  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:1">15:1</a> Imekkasen n tebzert akk-d yir imdanen țțasen-d ɣer Sidna Ɛisa iwakken a s-slen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:2">15:2</a> Ifariziyen d lɛulama n ccariɛa iɣaḍ-iten lḥal qqaṛen wway garasen : « argaz-agi yesṭerḥib s imednuben yerna yețɣimi yid-sen ɣer lmakla ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:3">15:3</a> Dɣa Sidna Ɛisa yewwi-yasen-d lemtel-agi :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:4">15:4</a> Anwa deg-wen ma yesɛa meyya wulli tṛuḥ-as yiwet deg-sent, ur yețțaǧa ara di lexla țesɛa uțesɛin nniḍen akken ad iṛuḥ a d-inadi ɣef tin i s-iɛeṛqen alamma yufa-ț ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:5">15:5</a> M'ara ț-yaf, a ț-id-ibibb ɣef tuyat-is s lfeṛḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:6">15:6</a> M'ara d-yaweḍ ɣer wexxam, ad issiwel i imdukkal-is d lǧiran-is, a sen-yini : feṛḥet yid-i, atan ufiɣ tixsi-nni i yi-iɛeṛqen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:7">15:7</a> S wakka nniɣ-awen : ad yili lfeṛḥ d ameqqran deg igenni ɣef yiwen umednub i d-yuɣalen ɣer webrid wala ɣef țesɛa uțesɛin nniḍen ur neɛṛiq ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:8">15:8</a> Neɣ anta tameṭṭut ma tesɛa ɛecṛa n twiztin tṛuḥ-as yiwet, ur tceɛɛel ara taftilt, ur tberrez ara axxam akken aț-țqelleb fell-as alamma tufa-ț ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:9">15:9</a> Mi ț-tufa aț-țessiwel i tmeddukal-is ț-țǧiratin-is a sent-tini : ufiɣ tawizeț-nni i yi-ṛuḥen ! Feṛḥemt yid-i !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:10">15:10</a> S wakka a wen-d-iniɣ : yețțili lfeṛḥ d ameqqran ɣer lmalayekkat ɣef yiwen umednub i d-yuɣalen ɣer webrid.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:11">15:11</a> Yenna-yasen daɣen : Yiwen wergaz yesɛa sin warrac. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:12">15:12</a> Ameẓyan deg-sen yenna i baba-s : a baba, efk-iyi-d amur i yi-d-iṣaḥen deg wayla-k. Dɣa baba-s yefka-yas amur-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:13">15:13</a> Mi Ɛeddan kra n wussan, ikker ameẓyan-nni ijmeɛ-ed akk amur-is, izzenz-it, ibeddel tamurt, iṛuḥ ɣer yiwet n tmurt ibeɛden. Dinna yewwi-t zzhu, yesṛuḥ ayen akk yesɛa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:14">15:14</a> Mi i gṣeṛṛef akk idrimen is, yeɣli-d laẓ d ameqqran di tmurt nni, ula d nețța yuɣal yelluẓ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:15">15:15</a> Yufa lxedma ɣer yiwen umezdaɣ n tmurt nni, iceggeɛ-it ad yeks taqeḍɛit n yilfan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:16">15:16</a> Acḥal imenna ad yečč ulamma d axeṛṛub-nni i tețțen yilfan-nni, meɛna yiwen ur as-d-yefki.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:17">15:17</a> Ihi yebda yețxemmim deg iman-is yenna : « acḥal n ixeddamen yellan ɣer baba ṛwan aɣṛum, nekk yenɣa-yi laẓ dagi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:18">15:18</a> Ad kkreɣ kan ad uɣaleɣ ɣer baba, a s-iniɣ : a baba ɛuṣaɣ Ṛebbi erniɣ-k keččini ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:19">15:19</a> ur uklaleɣ ara ad iliɣ d mmi-k, ḥseb-iyi am yiwen seg ixeddamen-ik »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:20">15:20</a> Ikker iṛuḥ ɣer baba-s. Akken qṛib ad yaweḍ ɣer wexxam, baba-s iɛqel-it-id si lebɛid, iɣaḍ-it, yuzzel-ed ɣuṛ-es. Yeṭṭef-it ger iɣallen-is isellem fell-as.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:21">15:21</a> Mmi-s yenna-yas : « a baba, ɛuṣaɣ Ṛebbi rniɣ-k keččini, ur uklaleɣ ara a yi-tḥesbeḍ d mmi-k ». </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:22">15:22</a> Lameɛna baba-s ikker yenna i iqeddacen-is : « ɣiwlet awit-ed abeṛnus-nni n leḥrir selset-as-t, qnet-as taxatemt i uḍaḍ-is ternum-as isebbaḍen i iḍaṛṛen-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:23">15:23</a> Awit-ed agenduz-nni yeṭṭuqten tezlum-t a t-nečč, a nexdem tameɣṛa ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:24">15:24</a> axaṭer mmi-nni i ḥesbeɣ yemmut yuɣal-ed idder, yella yeɛṛeq tura iban-ed ». Dɣa bdan tameɣṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:25">15:25</a> Mmi-s amenzu yella di lexla. Mi d-yuɣal, akken qṛib a d-yaweḍ ɣer wexxam, yesla i ccna d ccḍeḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:26">15:26</a> Yessawel i yiwen seg iqeddacen, isteqsa-t ɣef wayen yedṛan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:27">15:27</a> Aqeddac nni yenna-yas : « d gma-k i d-yuɣalen, baba-k ifṛeḥ aṭas imi i d-yuɣal di lehna, yezla-yas agenduz-nni yeṭṭuqten.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:28">15:28</a> Mi gesla i yimeslayen-nni, yerfa yugi ad ikcem ɣer wexxam. Baba-s yeffeɣ a t-iḥellel iwakken ad ikcem, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:29">15:29</a> lameɛna nețța yenna-yas : « acḥal iseggasen nekk qeddceɣ fell-ak, ula d yiwen webrid ur ɛuṣaɣ awal-ik, leɛmeṛ ur iyi-tefkiḍ ula d yiwen yiɣid a t-zluɣ iwakken ad feṛḥeɣ d imdukkal-iw. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:30">15:30</a> ma d mmi-k-agi i gesṛuḥen ayen akk yesɛa ɣef yir tilawin, i nețța tezliḍ agenduz-nni yeṭṭuqten ! »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:31">15:31</a> Ikker baba-s yenna-yas : A mmi, kečč kull ass tețțiliḍ yid-i, ayen akk sɛiɣ d ayla-k.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:32">15:32</a> Lameɛna ilaq-aɣ a nefṛeḥ axaṭer gma-k i ḥesbeɣ yemmut atan yuɣal-ed idder, yella ijaḥ, tura iban-ed.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:1">16:1</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna daɣen i inelmaden-is : -- Yiwen wergaz d ameṛkanti yesɛa lewkil ; lewkil-agi ccetkan fell-as ɣer umɛellem-is nnan-as : « lewkil-ik ițḍeggiɛ ayla-k ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:2">16:2</a> Amɛellem-is issawel-as yenna yas : « d acu-ten imeslayen-agi i sliɣ fell-ak ? Efk-iyi-d leḥsab ɣef wayen akk i d-teskecmeḍ d wayen i tessufɣeḍ, axaṭer sya d asawen ur tețțiliḍ ara d lewkil-iw ». </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:3">16:3</a> Lewkil-agi ixemmem deg iman-is yenna : d acu ara xedmeɣ imi amɛellem-iw ad iyi ikkes amkan-iw ? Ad xedmeɣ akal... Ur zmireɣ ara ! Ad țreɣ.... ssetḥaɣ ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:4">16:4</a> ?riɣ d acu ara xedmeɣ, iwakken m'ara yi-istixxeṛ umɛellem-iw, ad afeɣ wid ara yi-iɛiwnen !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:5">16:5</a> Yessawel-asen yiwen yiwen i wid akk yesɛan ṭṭlaba ɣer umɛellem-is. Yenna i umezwaru : « Acḥal i k-ițalas umɛellem-iw ? »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:6">16:6</a> Argaz-nni yerra-yas-d : « Meyya yecbuyla n zzit uzemmur. » Yenna-yas : « sellek awi-d leḥsab ik, qqim taruḍ xemsin ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:7">16:7</a> Yenna daɣen i wayeḍ : « i keččini, acḥal i k-ițalas ? » Yenna-yas-d : « meyya tcekkaṛin n yirden. » Yenna-yas : « awi-d leḥsab-ik, qqim taruḍ tmanyin».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:8">16:8</a> Amɛellem n lewkil-nni axeddaɛ icekkeṛ-it ɣef tiḥeṛci-ines axaṭer arraw n ddunit-agi ḥeṛcen di lecɣal wway gar-asen akteṛ n warraw n tafat.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:9">16:9</a> Ma d nekk atan a wen-d iniɣ: sxedmet adrim n ddunit-agi iwakken aț-țesɛum imdukkal, s wakka asm'ara yefnu cci n ddunit, aț-țețțuqeblem di tmezduɣin n dayem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:10">16:10</a> Ma nesɛa laman deg yiwen ɣef tɣawsiwin timecṭuḥin, a nețkel fell-as ula ɣef tmeqqranin ; win yellan d axeddaɛ di tɣawsiwin timecṭuḥin, ad yili d axeddaɛ ula di tmeqqranin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:11">16:11</a> Ma yella tețḍeggiɛem leṛẓaq n ddunit-agi, anwa ara kkun-iwekklen ɣef leṛẓaq n tideț ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:12">16:12</a> Ma yella ulac daɣen laman deg-wen ɣef wayen i wen-iwekkel walebɛaḍ, amek ara wen-d-yefk Sidi Ṛebbi ayen i wen-ihegga i kunwi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:13">16:13</a> Ulac aqeddac ara iqedcen ɣef sin yemɛellmen : ma iḥemmel yiwen ad ikṛeh wayeḍ neɣ ma yeṭṭef deg yiwen ur yețțak ara lqima i wayeḍ. Ur tezmirem ara aț-țqedcem ɣef Ṛebbi ma yella tettabaɛem leṛẓaq n ddunit agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:14">16:14</a> Ifariziyen i gesmeḥsisen i wayen i d-iqqaṛ Sidna Ɛisa, stehzayen fell-as axaṭer nutni ḥemmlen idrimen ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:15">16:15</a> ma d nețța yenna-yasen : Tesbegginem-d iman-nwen d iḥeqqiyen zdat medden, meɛna Sidi Ṛebbi yessen ulawen-nwen ; ayen yesɛan ccan ɣer yemdanen di ddunit-agi, d ayen yețwakeṛhen ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:16">16:16</a> Uqbel lweqt n Yeḥya aɣeṭṭas, kullec iteddu s ccariɛa n Musa d wayen i d-xebbṛen lenbiya. Tura, lexbaṛ n lxiṛ yeɛnan tgelda n Ṛebbi ițțubecceṛ ; mkul yiwen yekkat amek ara ț-ikcem s ddreɛ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:17">16:17</a> Yeshel i igenni d lqaɛa ad fnun, ma d ccariɛa n Sidi Ṛebbi ur ițțanqas seg-s ula d yiwen n usekkil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:18">16:18</a> Kra n win ara yebrun i tmeṭṭut-is iɛawed zzwaǧ, yezna ; kra n win ara yaɣen tameṭṭut yennebran, yezna daɣen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:19">16:19</a> Yiwen wergaz d ameṛkanti, ițlusu anagar llebsa ifazen n leḥrir aṛqaq ; mkul ass ixeddem tameɣṛa, ițɛici di zzhu d lfeṛḥ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:20">16:20</a> Yiwen igellil isem-is Laɛẓar, iččuṛ d ideddiyen, ițɣimi ɣer tewwurt n umeṛkanti-nni, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:21">16:21</a> iṭṭamaɛ deg-s ad yečč ɣas d ayen i gɣellin ɣer lqaɛa ; ula d iqjan țțasen-d ad mecḥen ideddiyen-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:22">16:22</a> Asmi yemmut uẓawali-nni, ddment-eț lmalayekkat wwint-eț ɣer igenni ɣer wanda yella Ibṛahim. Ameṛkanti-nni yemmut ula d nețța, meḍlen-t. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:23">16:23</a> Di laxeṛt yenɛețțab aṭas, yerfed allen-is, iwala mebɛid Ibṛahim akk-d Laɛẓar ɣer tama-s.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:24">16:24</a> Iɛeggeḍ yenna-yas : « A baba Ibṛahim, ḥunn fell-i ceggeɛ-ed Laɛẓar ad iger ulamma d ixef n uḍad-is deg waman ad issismeḍ iles-iw, aql-i nneɛtabeɣ aṭas deg uḥǧaǧu-yagi n tmes. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:25">16:25</a> Ibṛahim yerra-yas : A mmi, mmekti-d belli tewwiḍ amur-ik di ddunit ; ma d Laɛẓar yeṛwa lehmum. Tura nețța yețțuṣebbeṛ yufa dagi lfeṛḥ, kečč iṣaḥ-ik-id lqeṛḥ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:26">16:26</a> Yerna yella gar-aneɣ yiwen yeɣzeṛ annect ila-t, wid yebɣan ad zegren sya ɣuṛ-wen, ur zmiren ara ; kunwi daɣen ur tezmirem ara a d-zegrem ɣuṛ-nneɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:27">16:27</a> Ameṛkanti-nni yenna-yas : Ihi a baba Ibṛahim di leɛnaya-k ceggeɛ Laɛẓar ɣer wexxam n baba ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:28">16:28</a> ad iɛeggen i xemsa-nni wayetma, iwakken ur d-țțasen ara ula d nutni ɣer wemkan-agi n leɛtab.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:29">16:29</a> Ibṛahim yerra-yas : Atmaten-ik ɣuṛ-sen ccariɛa n Musa d lenbiya, a ten-tebɛen !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:30">16:30</a> Ameṛkanti-nni yenna-yas-d : A baba Ibṛahim, ur țḥessisen ara i ccariɛa d lenbiya lameɛna ma yuɣal ɣuṛ-sen yiwen syagi, ad beddlen tikli.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:31">16:31</a> Ibṛahim yerra-yas : M'ur semḥessen ara i ccariɛa n Musa d lenbiya, atan ɣas ma yuɣal yiwen si lmegtin ur as-smeḥsisen ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:1">17:1</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna i inelmaden is imeslayen-agi : -- D lmuḥal ur d-țilint ara sebbat ara yesseɣlin imdanen di ddnub. A nnger n win ara yilin d sebba n uɣelluy ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:2">17:2</a> axiṛ a s-ɛelqen aɣaṛef n tsirt ɣer temgeṛṭ-is, a t-ḍeggṛen ɣer lebḥeṛ wala ad yesseɣli di ddnub yiwen seg imecṭuḥen-agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:3">17:3</a> ?adret ɣef yiman-nwen ! Ma yeḍlem gma-k ssefhem-it, ma yendem deg wayen ixdem semmeḥ as. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:4">17:4</a> ?as ma yeḍlem-ik sebɛa iberdan deg wass, ma yusa-d ɣuṛ-ek sebɛa tikkal a k-d-yini : « aql-i ndemmeɣ deg wayen xedmeɣ », ilaq a s tsemmḥeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:5">17:5</a> Ṛṛusul n Sidna Ɛisa nnan-as : A Sidi ssemɣeṛ liman-nneɣ !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:6">17:6</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yasen : Lemmer tesɛam liman ulamma annect n uɛeqqa n yired, aț-țizmirem aț-ținim i ttejṛa-yagi n țut qleɛ sya tṛuḥeḍ aț-țeẓẓuḍ iman-im di lebḥeṛ, a wen-taɣ awal.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:7">17:7</a> Anwa deg-wen ara yesɛun axeddam ikerrzen neɣ ikessen lmal, ara s-yinin m'ara d-yuɣal si lexla : « lɛeslama-inek, qqim aț-țesteɛfuḍ, tura a k-d-awiɣ aț-țeččeḍ ». </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:8">17:8</a> Mačči akka ara s-yini, meɛna a s-yini : « ɣiwel beddel lqecc-ik tawiḍ-iyi-d ad ččeɣ ad sweɣ, mi ččiɣ ṛwiɣ, imiren aț-țeččeḍ aț-țesweḍ ula d keččini. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:9">17:9</a> Eɛni ad icekkeṛ axeddam-is imi gexdem ayen i s-yumeṛ ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:10">17:10</a> Kunwi daɣen m'ara txedmem ayen i wen-d yețwamṛen, init : d iqeddacen kan i nella, nexdem ayen ilaqen a t-nexdem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:11">17:11</a> Deg webrid-is ɣer temdint n Lquds, Sidna Ɛisa iɛedda ger tmurt n Samarya akk ț-țmurt n Jlili. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:12">17:12</a> Mi gekcem ɣer yiwet n taddart, mmugren t-id ɛecṛa imuḍan ihelken lbeṛs, bedden mebɛid </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:13">17:13</a> ɛeggḍen nnan-as : A Sidna Ɛisa ! A Sidi ḥunn fell-aɣ !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:14">17:14</a> Mi ten-iwala, Sidna Ɛisa yenna yasen : Ṛuḥet a kkun-walin lmuqedmin, a d-cehden belli teḥlam. Deg webrid-nsen mi ṛuḥen, akken walan iman-nsen ḥlan ṣfan, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:15">17:15</a> yiwen deg-sen yuɣal-ed seg webrid-nni yețḥemmid Ṛebbi s kra yellan di taɣect-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:16">17:16</a> Yusa-d yeɣli ɣer iḍaṛṛen n Sidna Ɛisa, iseǧǧed zdat-es, icekkeṛ-it, yerna argaz-agi d aṣamari i gella. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:17">17:17</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna i lɣaci : Eɛni ur ḥlin ara di ɛecṛa yid-sen ? I țesɛa nniḍen anda llan ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:18">17:18</a> Anagar abeṛṛani-agi i d-yuɣalen ad yeḥmed Ṛebbi !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:19">17:19</a> Dɣa yenna i usamari-nni : Kker fell-ak uɣal ɣer wexxam ik, imi tumneḍ yis-i, tețțusellkeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:20">17:20</a> Ifariziyen steqsan Sidna Ɛisa melmi ara d-tas lḥekma n tgeldit n Sidi Ṛebbi. Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yasen : Lḥekma n Sidi Ṛebbi mačči d ayen țwalint wallen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:21">17:21</a> Ur nezmir ara a d-nini : ațan dagi neɣ ațan dihin, axaṭer lḥekma n Sidi Ṛebbi ațan gar-wen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:22">17:22</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna i inelmaden-is : A d-yas lweqt i deg ara tmennim aț-țeẓrem Mmi-s n bunadem ulamma d yiwen wass lameɛna ur kkun-id-ițṣaḥ ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:23">17:23</a> Imiren ma nnan-awen-d : atah dagi neɣ atan dihin ur țṛuḥut ara, ur țțazzalet ara, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:24">17:24</a> axaṭer am lebṛaq m'ara yewwet seg yixef n igenni ɣer wayeḍ, akken ara yili Mmi-s n bunadem ass n tuɣalin-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:25">17:25</a> Tazwara ilaq ad yeɛteb aṭas, yerna lǧil-agi ur t-iqebbel ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:26">17:26</a> D ayen yedṛan di zzman n Nuḥ ara yedṛun deg ussan n tuɣalin n Mmi-s n bunadem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:27">17:27</a> Imdanen llan tețțen, țessen, țemyezwaǧen, zeggjen i dderya-nsen, armi d asmi yekcem Nuḥ ɣer lbabuṛ ; yewwet-ed uḥemmal, neflen-d waman ɣef ddunit, imdanen meṛṛa mmuten.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:28">17:28</a> D ayen yedṛan di zzman n Luṭ ara yedṛun daɣen : imdanen tețțen tessen, țțaɣen znuzun, țeẓẓun, bennun ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:29">17:29</a> asmi d-yeffeɣ Luṭ si temdint n ?udum, teɣli-d seg igenni tmes d ukebri i ten-isnegren akk. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:30">17:30</a> Akken ara d-tedṛu asm'ara d-iban Mmi-s n bunadem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:31">17:31</a> Ass-nni win ara yilin sufella n wexxam ur ilaq ara ad yekcem a d-iddem lqecc-is ; win i d-yufa lḥal di lexla ur ilaq ara ad yuɣal ɣer deffir ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:32">17:32</a> mmektit-ed tameṭṭut n Luṭ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:33">17:33</a> Win ara yebɣun ad isellek tudert-is ad a s-tṛuḥ, win iwumi ara tṛuḥ ɣef ddemma n yisem-iw a ț-isellek.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:34">17:34</a> Qqaṛeɣ-awen : deg iḍ-nni, ger sin ara yilin deg yiwen wusu, yiwen ad ițwarfed wayeḍ a d-yeqqim.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:35">17:35</a> Ger snat n tilawin yeẓẓaden, yiwet aț-țețwarfed tayeḍ a d-teqqim. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:36">17:36</a> Ger sin yergazen ara yilin di lexla, yiwen ad ițwarfed wayeḍ a d-yeqqim. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:37">17:37</a> Inelmaden-is steqsan-t nnan-as : Anda ara yedṛu wayagi a Sidi ? Yenna-yasen : Anda yella umurḍus, dinna ara a d-nejmaɛen igudar.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:1">18:1</a> Sidna Ɛisa yewwi-yasen-d lemtel-agi iwakken ad deɛɛun daymen ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi ur feččlen ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:2">18:2</a> Yenna-yasen : Deg yiwet n temdint yella yiwen lqaḍi, ur ițțagad Ṛebbi ur yețqadaṛ imdanen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:3">18:3</a> Di temdint-nni tella daɣen yiwet n taǧǧalt tețṛuḥu ɣuṛ-es, teqqaṛ-as : « eḥkem s lḥeqq gar-i d wexṣim-iw. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:4">18:4</a> Aṭas i geqqim yegguma a s-yefk lḥeqq, meɛna ixemmem deg yiman-is yenna : « taǧǧalt-agi eɛyiɣ deg-es ! ?as ur țțaggadeɣ Ṛebbi ur ḥsibeɣ yiwen </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:5">18:5</a> a s-fkeɣ lḥeqq akken ur d-tețțuɣal ara a yi-teṛṛeẓ aqeṛṛuy-iw. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:6">18:6</a> Dɣa Sidna Ɛisa yenna : Twalam ayen i d-yenna lqaḍi agi amesbaṭli ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:7">18:7</a> Amek Sidi Ṛebbi ur d-yețțak ara lḥeqq i wid i gextaṛ, i gețɛeggiḍen ɣuṛ-es am yiḍ am ass ? A wen-d-iniɣ : ur yețɛeṭṭil ara iwakken a ten-iɛiwen, a sen-yefk lḥeqq.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:8">18:8</a> Meɛna Mmi-s n bunadem asm'ara d-yas, wissen ma d-yaf liman di ddunit ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:9">18:9</a> Yenna-d daɣen lemtel-agi ɣef kra n yemdanen iḥesben iman-nsen d iḥeqqiyen ɣer Ṛebbi, iḥeqqṛen wiyaḍ :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:10">18:10</a> Sin yergazen ulin ɣer lǧameɛ ad ẓallen ; yiwen (d ccix n lǧameɛ) n ukabar n ifariziyen, wayeḍ d amekkas (ixeddmen ɣer iṛumaniyen istɛemṛen tamurt).  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:11">18:11</a> Afarizi ibedd yețẓalla yeqqaṛ deg iman-is : a k-ḥemdeɣ a k-cekkṛeɣ a Sidi Ṛebbi imi ur lliɣ ara am wid yellan d imcumen, d ixeddaɛen, yețɛicin di zzna ; a k-cekkṛeɣ daɣen imi ur lliɣ ara am umekkas-agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:12">18:12</a> ?țuẓumeɣ sin wussan di dduṛt, țțakeɣ leɛcuṛ seg wayen sɛiɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:13">18:13</a> Amekkas-nni ibedd mebɛid, issetḥa ad yerfed ula d allen-is ɣer igenni, yekkat deg idmaren-is yeqqaṛ : « a Sidi Ṛebbi, ḥunn fell-i nekk yellan d amednub ! »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:14">18:14</a> A wen-d-iniɣ : amekkas-nni yuɣal ɣer wexxam-is di lehna, yețwaqbel ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi, ma d afarizi-nni ur yețwaqbel ara. Kra n win yessimɣuṛen iman-is a t-id-isres Sidi Ṛebbi ; ma d win yessimẓiyen iman-is a t-issaɛli.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:15">18:15</a> Lɣaci țțawin-as-ed ula d llufanat iwakken ad issers afus-is fell-asen a ten-ibarek. Inelmaden-is mi walan ayagi, țnaɣen-ten. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:16">18:16</a> Sidna Ɛisa issawel asen-d yenna : Anfet-asen i warrac imeẓyanen a d-asen ɣuṛ-i ur ten-țțarrat ara, axaṭer tagelda n Ṛebbi tețwahegga i wid yellan am nutni. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:17">18:17</a> A wen-iniɣ tideț : kra n win ur neqbil ara tageldit n Sidi Ṛebbi am weqcic ameẓyan, ur ț-ikeččem ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:18">18:18</a> Yiwen umeṛkanti isteqsa Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Ay argaz n lɛali, d acu i yi ilaqen a t-xedmeɣ iwakken ad sɛuɣ tudert n dayem ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:19">18:19</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Acuɣeṛ i yi-d-tenniḍ « ay argaz lɛali » ? Ulac win yellan d lɛali-t anagar Sidi Ṛebbi ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:20">18:20</a> Tessneḍ ayen i d-tenna ccariɛa n Musa :  ur xeddem ara zzna, ur neqq ara, ur țțaker ara, ur țcehhid ara s ẓẓur, qadeṛ baba-k d yemma-k.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:21">18:21</a> Argaz-nni yenna-yas : Ayagi akk xeddmeɣ-t seg wasmi lliɣ d ameẓyan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:22">18:22</a> Mi gesla Sidna Ɛisa i imeslayen agi, yenna-yas : Ihi txuṣṣ-ik yiwet lḥaǧa kan : ṛuḥ zzenz ayen akk tesɛiḍ, seddeq-it i yigellilen iwakken aț-țesɛuḍ agerruj deg igenni, tuɣaleḍ-ed aț-țedduḍ yid-i.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:23">18:23</a> Argaz-nni mi gesla i yimeslayen-agi yeɣli-d fell-as leḥzen imi d ameṛkanti i gella. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:24">18:24</a> Mi t-iwala yeḥzen, Sidna Ɛisa yenna : Acḥal i sen-yewɛeṛ i wid yesɛan cci ad kecmen ɣer tgelda n Sidi Ṛebbi ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:25">18:25</a> Ishel i welɣem ad iɛeddi di tiṭ n tissegnit wala i umeṛkanti ad yekcem ɣer tgelda n Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:26">18:26</a> Wid i s-yeslan, nnan-as : Anwa i gzemren ad ițțusellek ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:27">18:27</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yasen : Ayen yellan d lmuḥal i wemdan yeshel ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:28">18:28</a> Buṭrus yenna-yas : I nukkni yeǧǧan kullec iwakken a neddu yid-ek ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:29">18:29</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen : A wen-iniɣ tideț : kra n win yeǧǧan axxam-is, tameṭṭut-is, ayetma- s, imawlan-is neɣ arraw-is ɣef ddemma n tgeldit n Ṛebbi, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:30">18:30</a> a s-d-ițunefk di ddunit-agi akteṛ n wayen yeǧǧa yerna ɣer zdat, ad yesɛu tudert n dayem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:31">18:31</a> Sidna Ɛisa ijmeɛ-ed ɣuṛ-es tnac-nni inelmaden-is yenna-yasen : Aql-aɣ a nali ɣer temdint n Lquds, ad idṛu wayen akk i d-uran lenbiya ɣef wayen yeɛnan Mmi-s n bunadem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:32">18:32</a> Ad ițțusellem ger ifassen n lkeffaṛ, ad ḍsen fell-as, ad kksen fell-as sser, a t-ssusfen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:33">18:33</a> A t-wwten s ujelkkaḍ ( s ucelliṭ ), a t-enɣen ; ass wis tlata a d-iḥyu si ger lmegtin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:34">18:34</a> Inelmaden-is ur fhimen acemma deg wayen i sen-d-yenna, lmeɛna n imeslayen-agi tețwaffer fell-asen. Ur ẓrin ara d acu i gebɣa a t-id-yini.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:35">18:35</a> Akken qṛib ad yaweḍ Sidna Ɛisa ɣer temdint n Yiriku, yiwen uderɣal yeqqim rrif n webrid yessutur tin n Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:36">18:36</a> Mi gesla i lɣaci țɛeddayen, yesteqsa d acu i gedṛan ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:37">18:37</a> nnan-as belli d Ɛisa Anaṣari i d-iɛeddan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:38">18:38</a> Dɣa iɛeggeḍ yenna : A Ɛisa, a mmi-s n Sidna Dawed, ḥunn fell-i !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:39">18:39</a> Wid yezwaren țdemmiren-t ɣer deffir qqaṛen-as : Ssusem a k-ihdu Ṛebbi ! Meɛna nețța yețɛeggiḍ akteṛ : A mmi-s n Sidna Dawed, ḥunn fell-i !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:40">18:40</a> Sidna Ɛisa yeḥbes, yefka lameṛ a s-t-id-awin. Mi d-yewweḍ ɣuṛ-es, yenna-yas :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:41">18:41</a> D acu tebɣiḍ a k-t-xedmeɣ ? Yerra-yas-d : A Sidi, bɣiɣ a yi-d-yuɣal yeẓri !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:42">18:42</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Wali ! Imi tumneḍ yis-i atan tețțusellkeḍ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:43">18:43</a> Imiren kan yuɣal-it-id yeẓri yețwali, yedda d Sidna Ɛisa, iḥemmed Ṛebbi. Mi walan ayagi, lɣaci meṛṛa ḥemden Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:1">19:1</a> Sidna Ɛisa iɛedda si temdint n Yiriku. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:2">19:2</a> Yella dinna yiwen umeṛkanti isem-is Zaci, d ameqqran n imekkasen n ddewla. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:3">19:3</a> Yebɣa ad iẓer anwa i d Sidna Ɛisa lameɛna ur yezmir ara a t-iwali imi aṭas lɣaci i gellan, yerna nețța d awezlan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:4">19:4</a> Yuzzel ɣer zdat, yuli ɣef ttejṛa iwakken a t-iwali m'ara d-iɛeddi syenna. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:5">19:5</a> Mi gewweḍ Sidna Ɛisa ɣer wemkan-nni, yerfed allen-is yenna i Zaci : A Zaci, ɣiwel ers-ed syenna, ɣuṛ-ek ara nseɣ ass-agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:6">19:6</a> Zaci yers-ed s lemɣawla ad yesteṛḥeb s Sidna Ɛisa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:7">19:7</a> Lɣaci mi walan ayagi smermugen wway gar asen qqaṛen : « ɣer yiwen umekkas (axeddaɛ) am wagi ara yens ! »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:8">19:8</a> Zaci iqeṛṛeb-ed ɣer Sidna Ɛisa, yenna-yas : A Sidi, atan ad fkeɣ i igellilen azgen n wayen sɛiɣ, yerna ma ḍelmeɣ yiwen a s-rreɣ ṛebɛa imuren.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:9">19:9</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : Ass-agi leslak ikcem-ed axxam agi, imi argaz-agi ula d nețța d mmi-s n Ibṛahim.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:10">19:10</a> Axaṭer Mmi-s n bunadem yusa-d ad inadi ɣef wid iḍaɛen, a ten-isellek. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:11">19:11</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerna-d yiwen n lemtel i wid i s ismeḥsisen, axaṭer qṛib ad awḍen ɣer temdint n Lquds, lɣaci ɣilen imiren kan ara d-tas tgeldit n Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:12">19:12</a> Yenna yasen : Yiwen wergaz imawlan-is muceɛen, ițeddu ad iṛuḥ ɣer yiwet n tmurt ibeɛden iwakken a t-sbedden d agellid ɣef tmurt-is , imiren a d-yuɣal.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:13">19:13</a> Qbel ad iṛuḥ, yessawel i ɛecṛa seg iqeddacen-is ; yefka tawizeț i mkul yiwen deg-sen, yenna-yasen : « xedmet yis-sent tjaṛa alamma uɣaleɣ-ed ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:14">19:14</a> Arraw n tmurt-is i t-ikeṛhen, ceggɛen deffir-es kra n yemdanen ara yinin : « ur nebɣi ara ad yili wergaz agi d agellid fell-aneɣ. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:15">19:15</a> Mi t-sbedden d agellid, yuɣal ed ɣer tmurt-is ; yessawel i iqeddacen nni iwumi yefka tiwiztin iwakken ad isteqsi mkul yiwen deg-sen d acu i d-yerbeḥ yis-sent. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:16">19:16</a> Amezwaru yusa-d, yenna : A Sidi, s twizeț-nni i yi-d-tefkiḍ rebḥeɣ-ed ɛecṛa nniḍen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:17">19:17</a> Agellid yenna-yas : D ayen yelhan ay aqeddac lɛali, imi deg-ek laman ɣef lḥaǧa tamecṭuḥt, a k-fkeɣ aț-țḥekmeḍ ɣef ɛecṛa n tudrin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:18">19:18</a> Aqeddac wis sin yusa-d yenna : A Sidi, rebḥeɣ-ed xemsa n twiztin s twizeț i yi-d-tefkiḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:19">19:19</a> Agellid yenna-yas : Ula d kečč a k-sbeddeɣ d lḥakem ɣef xemsa tudrin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:20">19:20</a> Yusa-d uqeddac wis tlata yenna : A Sidi, ațah twizeț-inek ! Freɣ-ț deg yiwen uceṭṭiḍ ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:21">19:21</a> uggadeɣ-k axaṭer tweɛṛeḍ, tețțeddmeḍ ayen ur tesriseḍ, tmeggreḍ ayen ur tezriɛeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:22">19:22</a> Agellid yerra-yas : ?ef yimeslayen-ik ara k-ḥasbeɣ ay aqeddac amcum ! Teẓriḍ weɛṛeɣ, țeddmeɣ ayen ur sriseɣ, meggreɣ ayen ur zriɛeɣ ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:23">19:23</a> acuɣeṛ ihi ur tefkiḍ ara idrimen-iw i wid ara ten-isxedmen, iwakken m'ara d-uɣaleɣ a ten-id jebdeɣ s lfayda ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:24">19:24</a> Dɣa yenna i widak yellan dinna : Kkset-as tawizeț-nni, rnut-as-ț i win yesɛan ɛecṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:25">19:25</a> Nnan-as : A Sidi, yesɛa yakan ɛecṛa !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:26">19:26</a> Yerra-yasen : Nniɣ-awen : win yesɛan a s nernu, ma d win ur nesɛi ara a s nekkes ula d ayen i gɣil yesɛa-t. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:27">19:27</a> Ma d iɛdawen-nni-inu ur neqbil ara ad iliɣ d agellid fell-asen, awit-țen-id ɣer dagi tezlum-ten zdat-i.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:28">19:28</a> Mi gekfa ameslay, Sidna Ɛisa yezwar ɣer zdat lɣaci iwakken ad yali ɣer temdint n Lquds.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:29">19:29</a> Mi qṛib ad yaweḍ ɣer tuddar n Bitfaji akk-d Bitani, ɣer tama n yiwen yiɣil ițțusemman « Iɣil Uzemmur, » Sidna Ɛisa iceggeɛ sin seg inelmaden-is, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:30">19:30</a> yenna-yasen : Ṛuḥet ɣer taddart ihin i ɣ-d iqublen, aț-țafem ajḥiḥ yeqqen, leɛmeṛ ur yerkib fell-as yiwen ; brut-as-ed, tawim-t-id.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:31">19:31</a> Ma yella win i wen-d yennan : « acuɣeṛ i s-d-tebram ? » Init-as : yeḥwaǧ-it Ssid-nneɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:32">19:32</a> Imceggɛen-nni ṛuḥen, ufan kullec akken i sen-d-yenna Sidna Ɛisa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:33">19:33</a> Mi s-d-bran i wejḥiḥ-nni, bab-is yenna-yasen : I wacu i s-d-tebram ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:34">19:34</a> Rran-as : Yeḥwaǧ-it Ssid-nneɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:35">19:35</a> Wwin-d ajḥiḥ-nni, ssersen fell-as ibeṛnyas-nsen, srekben Sidna Ɛisa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:36">19:36</a> Akken i gteddu, lɣaci tessun-as-d ibeṛnyas-nsen deg webrid.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:37">19:37</a> Mi qṛib ad awḍen ɣer temdint n Lquds, di tkessart-nni n yiɣil n uzemmur, inelmaden-is d lɣaci meṛṛa ččuṛen d lfeṛḥ, țḥemmiden Sidi Ṛebbi s ṣṣut eɛlayen ɣef lbeṛhanat akk i walan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:38">19:38</a> Qqaṛen :  Yețțubarek ugellid i d-yusan s yisem n Sidi Ṛebbi ! Lehna deg igenwan, tamanegt i Sidi Ṛebbi deg imukan ɛlayen.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:39">19:39</a> Kra ifariziyen di tlemmast lɣaci nnan i Sidna Ɛisa : A Sidi, ini-yasen i inelmaden-ik ad ssusmen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:40">19:40</a> Yenna-yasen : A wen-iniɣ : ma ssusmen nutni, d idɣaɣen ara d-iɛeggḍen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:41">19:41</a> Mi qṛib ad yaweḍ ɣer temdint n Lquds, akken i ț-iwala, Sidna Ɛisa yețru fell-as, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:42">19:42</a> yenna : A tamdint n Lquds ! Lemmer teẓriḍ ass-agi ayen ara m-d-ifken lehna ! Lameɛna tura ayagi yeffer ɣef wallen-im !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:43">19:43</a> A d-asen wussan anda ara d-zeḍmen fell-am yeɛdawen-im, a d-kecmen a m-d-zzin si mkul tama, a kem-ḥeṛsen ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:44">19:44</a> a kem-snegren kemm d warraw-im, ur țțaǧan deg-m azṛu ɣef wayeḍ ; axaṭer ur teɛqileḍ ara usan i deg i d-yusa leslak n Sidi Ṛebbi ɣuṛ-em.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:45">19:45</a> Sidna Ɛisa yekcem ɣer wefrag n lǧameɛ iqedsen, yebda ițqecciɛ wid yeznuzun, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:46">19:46</a> yeqqaṛ-asen : Yura di tira iqedsen :  Axxam-iw ad yili d axxam n tẓallit, kunwi terram-t d axxam n imakaren.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:47">19:47</a> Sidna Ɛisa yesselmad mkul ass di lǧameɛ iqedsen. Lmuqedmin imeqqranen, lɛulama d imeqqranen n wegdud țnadin a t-nɣen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:48">19:48</a> lameɛna ur s-ufin ara abrid axaṭer lɣaci meṛṛa smeḥsisen-as, yerna tɛeǧǧben deg yimeslayen-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:1">20:1</a> Yiwen wass deg ussan-nni, Sidna Ɛisa yella yesselmad lɣaci deg wefrag n lǧameɛ iqedsen yețbecciṛ lexbaṛ n lxiṛ ; leḥqen-d lmuqedmin d lɛulama n ccariɛa akk d imeqqranen n wegdud, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:2">20:2</a> nnan-as : Di leɛnaya-k ! ansi i k-d-tekka lḥekma s wacu i txeddmeḍ annect agi ? Anwa i k-ț-id-yefkan ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:3">20:3</a> Yerra-yasen : A kkun-steqsiɣ ula d nekkini, init-iyi-d : </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:4">20:4</a> anwa i d-icegn, d Ṛebbi neɣ d imdanen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:5">20:5</a> Bdan țemcawaṛen wway gar-asen, qqaṛen : Ma nenna-yas d Ṛebbi, a ɣ-d yini iwacu ihi ur tuminem ara yis ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:6">20:6</a> Ma nenna-yas d imdanen, lɣaci akk a ɣ-ṛejmen axaṭer umnen meṛṛa belli Yeḥya d nnbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:7">20:7</a> Dɣa nnan i Sidna Ɛisa : Atan ur neẓri ara anwa i t-id iceggɛen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:8">20:8</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen : Ula d nekk ur awen-d-qqaṛeɣ ara ansi i yi-d-tekka lḥekma s wacu i xeddmeɣ annect-agi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:9">20:9</a> Dɣa yewwi-d lemtel-agi i lɣaci : Yiwen wergaz yeẓẓa tafeṛṛant ( iger n tẓurin ) issekra-ț i ixemmasen, iṛuḥ ɣer lɣeṛba, iɛeṭṭel dinna. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:10">20:10</a> Mi d-yewweḍ lweqt n tẓurin, iceggeɛ ɣuṛ-sen aqeddac iwakken a s-d-fken amur-is ; lameɛna ixemmasen-nni wwten-t, rrant-id ifassen d ilmawen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:11">20:11</a> Iceggeɛ daɣen aqeddac nniḍen, lameɛna ula d nețța ewten-t, regmen-t, rrant-id ifassen d ilmawen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:12">20:12</a> Iceggeɛ-asen daɣen wis tlata, jerḥen-t rnan qecɛen-t-id syenna.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:13">20:13</a> Amɛellem-nni n tfeṛṛant yenna : « d acu ara xedmeɣ tura ? A sen ceggɛeɣ mmi ameɛzuz , ahat nețța a t-qadṛen ! » </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:14">20:14</a> Lameɛna ixemmasen nni mi t-walan, mcawaṛen wway gar asen nnan : « ataya win ara iweṛten ! Kkret a t-nenneɣ iwakken aț-țuɣal tfeṛṛant d ayla-nneɣ. » </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:15">20:15</a> ?eggṛen-t beṛṛa n tfeṛṛant, nɣan-t. D acu ara sen-yexdem tura bab n tfeṛṛant-agi ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:16">20:16</a> A d-yas ad ineɣ ixemmasen-nni, ad yefk tafeṛṛant i wiyaḍ. Lɣaci mi slan annect-agi, nnan : A ɣ-imneɛ Ṛebbi !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:17">20:17</a> Lameɛna Sidna Ɛisa imuqel-iten yenna : D acu i d lmeɛna n wawal-agi yuran :  adɣaɣ i ḍeggṛen wid ibennun,  yuɣal d win yeṭṭfen lebni .  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:18">20:18</a>  Kra n win ara yeɣlin  ɣef wedɣaɣ-agi ad yeṛṛez ;  ma d win i ɣef ara d-yeɣli,  ad ițwanɣed.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:19">20:19</a> Lɛulama n ccariɛa d imeqqranen n lmuqedmin țqelliben a t-ṭṭfen imiren kan, axaṭer fehmen fell-asen i d-yenna lemtel-agi, lameɛna uggaden lɣaci.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:20">20:20</a> Bdan țɛassan Sidna Ɛisa iwakken ma yeɣli-d deg wawal a t-ṭṭfen. Fkan tajɛelt i kra n yemdanen yerran iman-nsen d wid iḍuɛen Ṛebbi iwakken a t-zenzen ɣer lḥakem n tmurt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:21">20:21</a> Steqsan-t ihi s imeslayen-agi : A Sidi, neẓra ayen i d-teqqaṛeḍ d wayen i tesselmadeḍ d lḥeqq, yerna ur txeddmeḍ ara lxilaf ger yemdanen, tesselmadeḍ abrid n Ṛebbi s tideț. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:22">20:22</a> Ini-yaɣ-d ma d leḥlal a nxelleṣ tabzert i Qayṣer (isteɛmṛen tamurt)?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:23">20:23</a> Sidna Ɛisa ifaqen i tḥila-nsen, yerra-yasen : Seknet-iyi-d aṣurdi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:24">20:24</a> Udem-agi d wayen yuran ɣef wuṣuṛdi-agi wi ten-ilan ? Rran-as : D udem n Qayṣer!  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:25">20:25</a> Dɣa yenna-yasen : Ihi erret i Qayṣer ayen yellan n Qayṣer, terrem i Ṛebbi ayen yellan n Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:26">20:26</a> Wehmen s wayen i sen-d-yerra dɣa ssusmen irkul, axaṭer ur ufin ara amek ara t-id-sseɣlin deg wawal zdat lɣaci.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:27">20:27</a> Kra n isaduqiyen ur nețțamen ara s ḥeggu n lmegtin, qeṛṛben-d ɣer Sidna Ɛisa, steqsan-t nnan-as :   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:28">20:28</a> A Sidi, atah wayen i d-teqqaṛ ccariɛa n Musa :  Ma yemmut yiwen wergaz yeǧǧa-d tameṭṭut-is mbla dderya, ilaq gma-s ad yaɣ tameṭṭut-nni, ad yesɛu yid-es dderya iwakken a d-ixlef isem n gma-s yemmuten.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:29">20:29</a> Ihi llan sebɛa watmaten : amezwaru yezweǧ, yemmut ur d yeǧǧi dderya. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:30">20:30</a> Wis sin yuɣ taǧǧalt-nni, yemmut ula d nețța.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:31">20:31</a> Yuɣ-iț daɣen wis tlata, akken armi d wis sebɛa ; mmuten meṛṛa, yiwen ur d-yeǧǧi yid-es dderya. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:32">20:32</a> ?er taggara temmut tmeṭṭut-nni ula d nețțat. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:33">20:33</a> Ass n ḥeggu n lmegtin, anwa ara ț-yesɛun ț-țameṭṭut-is imi ț-uɣen yiwen yiwen di sebɛa yid-sen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:34">20:34</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yasen : Irgazen akk-d tilawin n ddunit agi țemyezwaǧen wway gar-asen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:35">20:35</a> Lameɛna wid ara yuklalen a d-ḥyun si lmut ɣer tudert n dayem, ur țemyezwaǧen ara, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:36">20:36</a> axaṭer ur țțuɣalen ara ad mmten, ad ilin am lmalayekkat ; Sidi Ṛebbi a ten-yerr d arraw-is imi i d-ḥyan si ger lmegtin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:37">20:37</a> ?ef wayen yeɛnan ḥeggu n lmegtin ula d nnbi Musa ihḍeṛ-ed fell-as mi gessawel i Sidi Ṛebbi zdat udarnu iṛeqqen : a Ṛebbi,  Illu n Ibṛahim, Illu n Isḥaq, Illu n Yeɛqub.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:38">20:38</a> Ṛebbi mačči d Ṛebbi n wid yemmuten meɛna d Ṛebbi n wid yeddren imi ɣuṛ-es ddren irkulli ɣas akken mmuten.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:39">20:39</a> Kra n imusnawen n ccariɛa neṭqen-d nnan-as : A Sidi, d awal n lɛali i d-tenniḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:40">20:40</a> Kukran a s-rnun ula d yiwen usteqsi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:41">20:41</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen : Amek armi qqaṛen Lmasiḥ d mmi-s n Dawed ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:42">20:42</a> Dawed s yiman-is yenna-d di tektabt n ?abur :  Sidi Ṛebbi yenna i Ssid-iw : qqim aț-țḥekmeḍ ɣer tama- w tayeffust  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:43">20:43</a>  alamma rriɣ iɛdawen-ik seddaw iḍaṛṛen-ik.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:44">20:44</a> Ma yella Dawed isemma i Lmasiḥ « Sidi », amek i gezmer ad yili d mmi-s ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:45">20:45</a> Lɣaci meṛṛa llan smeḥsisen, Sidna Ɛisa yenna i inelmaden-is :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:46">20:46</a> ?adret iman-nwen ɣef lɛulama n ccariɛa i gḥemmlen ad țḥewwisen s ijellaben iɣezfanen, ḥemmlen ad țsellimen fell-asen yemdanen di leswaq, ad ṭṭfen imukan imezwura di leǧwameɛ d imukan lɛali di tmeɣṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:47">20:47</a> Tețțen ayla n tuǧǧal, ssiɣzifen taẓallit iwakken a ten-id-walin wiyaḍ. ?ef wannect-agi, Sidi Ṛebbi ihegga-yasen-d lɛiqab d ameqqran.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:1">21:1</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerfed allen-is, iwala imeṛkantiyen srusun lewɛadi deg usenduq n lǧameɛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:2">21:2</a> Ațaya yiwet n taǧǧalt taẓawalit tger sin iṣurdiyen ɣer usenduq-nni, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:3">21:3</a> dɣa yenna : A wen-iniɣ tideț : lweɛda n taǧǧalt-agi taẓawalit tugar akk tiyaḍ ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:4">21:4</a> axaṭer wiyaḍ fkan seg wayen sɛan d zzyada ma d nețțat tefka ciṭṭuḥ-nni s wacu ara tɛic.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:5">21:5</a> Kra n yemdanen țmeslayen ɣef lǧameɛ iqedsen qqaṛen wway gar-asen : Acḥal yecbeḥ lebni n lǧameɛ-agi akk-d țɣawsiwin i s-d-yețțunefken d lweɛda ! Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:6">21:6</a> Deg wayen akka i tețwalim, a d-awḍen wussan anda kullec ad ihudd, ur d-yețɣimi wedɣaɣ ɣef wayeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:7">21:7</a> Steqsan-t nnan-as : A Sidi, melmi ara d-yedṛu wannect-a ? Anta licaṛa ara d isbegnen belli qṛib a d-yedṛu waya ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:8">21:8</a> Yenna-yasen : ?uṛ-wat a kkun-kellxen, axaṭer aṭas ara d-yasen s yisem-iw a d inin : d nekk i d Lmasiḥ ! Neɣ a wen-d-inin : lweqt yewweḍ-ed ! Ur ten-țțamnet ara ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:9">21:9</a> M'ara teslem heddṛen ɣef tegrawliwin d ṭradat ur țțagadet ara, axaṭer ilaq a d-yedṛu uqbel wayagi, lameɛna mačči imiren i ț-țaggara n ddunit.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:10">21:10</a> Yenna-yasen daɣen :  A d-yekker wegdud ɣer wayeḍ, a d-tekker tagelda ɣer tayeḍ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:11">21:11</a> A d-tilint zzelzlat timeqqranin, a d-ɣlin di yal lehlakat i gderrɛen ( i gneṭṭḍen) akk-d laẓ, a d-tilint leɛǧubat yessexlaɛen akk-d licaṛat timeqqranin deg igenni. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:12">21:12</a> Lameɛna uqbel a d-yedṛu wannect-a, kunwi s inelmaden-iw a kkun-ṭṭfen, a kkun qehṛen, ad ḥekmen fell-awen di leǧwameɛ, a kkun-ḍeggṛen ɣer leḥbus, a kkun-sbedden zdat igelliden d lḥekkam ɣef ddemma n yisem-iw.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:13">21:13</a> A d-yedṛu wannect-a yid-wen iwakken aț-țilim d inigan-iw zdat-sen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:14">21:14</a> Ur țḥebbiṛet ara amek ara tsellkem iman-nwen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:15">21:15</a> axaṭer a wen-d-fkeɣ imeslayen d leɛqel s wacu ara tqablem iɛdawen nwen, ur țizmiren ara ad bedden zdat-wen neɣ a kkun-xalfen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:16">21:16</a> Ula d imawlan-nwen akk-d atmaten-nwen d imdukkal-nwen a kkun-zzenzen yerna ad nɣen aṭas seg-wen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:17">21:17</a> A kkun-keṛhen yemdanen meṛṛa ɣef ddemma-w, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:18">21:18</a> lameɛna yiwen wenẓad n uqeṛṛuy-nwen ur yețṛuḥu. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:19">21:19</a> ?ebṛet, axaṭer s ṣṣbeṛ-nwen ara tsellkem tiṛwiḥin-nwen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:20">21:20</a> M'ara teẓrem tamdint n Lquds zzin-as-d lɛeskeṛ n yeɛdawen-is, ḥṣut belli nnger-is yewweḍ-ed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:21">21:21</a> Ass-nni ilaq wid ara yilin di temdint n Lquds ad ffɣen, wid ara yilin di lexla ur keččmen ara ɣer temdint, wid ara yilin di tmurt n Yahuda ad rewlen ɣer idurar. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:22">21:22</a> Axaṭer ussan-nni d ussan n twaɣit deg wacu ara yedṛu meṛṛa wayen yuran.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:23">21:23</a> A nnger n tilawin ara yilin s tadist neɣ tid ara yessuṭuḍen deg ussan-nni axaṭer a d-teɣli cedda ț-țameqqrant ɣef tmurt, a d-yeɣli wurrif n Sidi Ṛebbi ɣef wegdud, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:24">21:24</a> imezdaɣ-is ad mmten s ujenwi, a ten-awin d imeḥbas ɣer tmura nniḍen. Tamdint n Lquds a ț-ṛekḍen leǧnas ur nețțamen ara s Sidi Ṛebbi, alamma yețwakemmel lweqt i sen-d-yefka Sidi Ṛebbi, imiren ad yezzi ɣef leǧnas-nni, a ten-iɛaqeb.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:25">21:25</a> A d-tbanent licaṛat deg iṭij, deg waggur d yitran. Di ddunit, imdanen meṛṛa a ten-iffeɣ leɛqel, ur ẓerren ara d acu ara xedmen m'ara slen i ṣṣut n lemwaji d lebḥuṛ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:26">21:26</a> Ad ilin wid ara yemten si lxuf m'ara walin lmuṣibat ara d-yeɣlin ɣef ddunit ; igenwan d kra yellan deg-sen ad rgagin.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:27">21:27</a> Imiren imdanen ad walin  Mmi-s n bunadem iteddu-d ɣef wusigna s tezmert d lɛaḍima tameqqrant.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:28">21:28</a> M'ara yebdu wannect-agi iḍeṛṛu, sbeddet lqedd-nwen trefdem iqeṛṛay-nwen axaṭer leslak-nwen yewweḍ-ed.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:29">21:29</a> Yewwi-yasen-d lemtel-agi : Walit taneqleț neɣ ttjuṛ nniḍen ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:30">21:30</a> M'ara bdunt fessunt, teẓram qṛib a d-yaweḍ unebdu. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:31">21:31</a> Kunwi daɣen m'ara twalim yewweḍ-ed wannect-agi ḥṣut belli tageldit n Ṛebbi teqṛeb-ed.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:32">21:32</a> A wen-iniɣ tideț: lǧil-agi ur yețmețțat ara alamma yedṛa wannect-agi meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:33">21:33</a> Igenni d lqaɛa ad fnun ma d awal-iw ur ifennu ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:34">21:34</a> Ɛasset ɣef yiman-nwen, ḥadret a kkun-iɣuṛṛ zzhu n ddunit ; ɛasset iman-nwen ɣef tissit n ccṛab d iɣeblan, neɣ m'ulac a d-yeɣli fell awen wass-nni ur tebnim fell-as. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:35">21:35</a> Ass-nni a d-yeɣli am ucebbak ɣef yemdanen n ddunit meṛṛa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:36">21:36</a> Ɛiwzet ihi, deɛɛut dayem ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi a wen-d-yefk tazmert ara kkun-imenɛen seg wayen i d-iteddun, s wayes ara tbeddem zdat Mmi-s n bunadem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:37">21:37</a> Deg wass, Sidna Ɛisa yesselmad di lǧameɛ iqedsen ma deg iḍ, yețṛuḥu ad yens deg yiwen yiɣil ițțusemman : «Iɣil n uzemmur ». </p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:38">21:38</a> ?ṣbeḥ zik, lɣaci meṛṛa țṛuḥun ɣuṛ-es ɣer lǧameɛ iqedsen iwakken ad slen i wawal-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:1">22:1</a> Lɛid i deg xedmen aɣṛum mbla iɣes n temtunt ițțusemman « Tafaska n izimer n leslak » tqeṛb-ed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:2">22:2</a> Lmuqedmin imeqqranen d lɛulama n ccariɛa țqelliben amek ara nɣen Sidna Ɛisa lameɛna uggaden lɣaci.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:3">22:3</a> Yudas n Qeṛyut yiwen si tnac-nni n inelmadenis, ikcem-it Cciṭan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:4">22:4</a> Iṛuḥ ad yemcawaṛ d lmuqedmin imeqqranen akk-d lḥekkam iɛessasen n lǧameɛ iqedsen, iwakken a sen izzenz Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:5">22:5</a> Nutni feṛḥen yerna ɛuhden-t a s-fken idrimen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:6">22:6</a> Yudas yefra awal yid-sen syenna yebda yețqellib amek ara sen-t-yezzenz s tuffra ɣef lɣaci.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:7">22:7</a> Yewweḍ-ed wass n Tfaska n weɣṛum mbla iɣes n tamtunt i deg ilaq ad zlun izimer n leslak. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:8">22:8</a> Sidna Ɛisa iceggeɛ Buṭrus d Yuḥenna, yenna-yasen : Ṛuḥet a ɣ-theggim imensi n Tfaska.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:9">22:9</a> Nnan-as : Anda tebɣiḍ a t-nheggi a Sidi ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:10">22:10</a> Yerra-yasen : M'ara tkecmem ɣer temdint, a d-temmagrem yiwen wergaz yerfed tacmuxt n waman ; tebɛet-eț ɣer wexxam anda ara yekcem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:11">22:11</a> Init i bab n wexxam-nni : yeqqaṛ-ak-d Ssid nneɣ, anda ara nečč imensi n Tfaska  nekk d inelmaden-iw ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:12">22:12</a> A wen-d-isken yiwet n tɣuṛfeț tameqqrant iwejden, dinna ara theggim imensi n Tfaska.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:13">22:13</a> Mi ṛuḥen, ufan kullec akken i sen-t-id-yenna, dɣa heggan imensi n Tfaska.   </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:14">22:14</a> Mi d-yewweḍ lweqt n imensi, Sidna Ɛisa yeqqim ad yečč nețța d Ṛṛusul-is, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:15">22:15</a> yenna-yasen : Acḥal i mennaɣ ad ččeɣ imensi n Tfaska-agi  yid-wen uqbel ad nneɛtabeɣ ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:16">22:16</a> A wen-d-iniɣ : atan ur țțuɣaleɣ ara maḍi a t-ččeɣ alamma tețwakemmel lmeɛna-ines di tgelda n Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:17">22:17</a> Yeddem-d tabuqalt n waman n tẓurin, yeḥmed Sidi Ṛebbi yenna : Axet tabuqalt-agi, feṛqet-eț wway gar-awen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:18">22:18</a> a wen-d-iniɣ : sya d asawen ur țțuɣaleɣ ara ad sweɣ seg waman-agi n tẓurin alamma tewweḍ ed tgeldit n Sidi Ṛebbi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:19">22:19</a> Yeddem-ed daɣen aɣṛum, iḥmed Sidi Ṛebbi, yebḍa-t yefka-yasen-t, yenna : Aɣṛum-agi d lǧețța-w ara fkeɣ fell-awen, feṛqet-eț gar-awen. Sya d asawen xeddmet akkagi akken ad iyi-d-tețmektayem.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:20">22:20</a> Mi gfukk imensi, yeddem-ed tabuqalt n waman n tẓurin, yefka yasen-ț yenna : Tabuqalt-agi, d leɛqed ajdid s idammen-iw ara yazzlen fell-awen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:21">22:21</a> Ma d win ara yi-zzenzen atan yeqqim-ed yid-i ɣer lmakla. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:22">22:22</a> Mmi-s n bunadem ad immet akken yura fell-as di tira iqedsen, lameɛna a nnger n wemdan agi ara t-izzenzen ! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:23">22:23</a> Ṛṛusul bdan țmesteqsayen wway gar-asen anwa-t wagi ara t-ixedɛen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:24">22:24</a> Inelmaden bdan țemjadalen wway gar-asen iwakken ad ẓren anwa deg-sen ara ițwaḥesben d ameqqran. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:25">22:25</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna yasen : Imeqqranen n ddunit ḥekmen s ddreɛ ɣef yigduden-nsen yerna țțusemman d at lxiṛ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:26">22:26</a> Kunwi xḍut i wannect-agi. Ameqqran deg-wen ad yili am umeẓyan, win iḥekmen ad yili am win iqeddcen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:27">22:27</a> Anwa i d ameqqran , d amɛelem yeqqimen ad yečč neɣ d win i s iqeddcen ? Yak d win yeqqimen ad yečč ! Ma d nekk, aql-i gar-awen am win iqeddcen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:28">22:28</a> Kunwi aql-ikkun tṣebṛem yid-i di lmeḥnat-iw. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:29">22:29</a> Akken i yi-d-ihegga Baba tagelda, ula d nekk a wen-ț-id heggiɣ i kunwi </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:30">22:30</a> iwakken aț-țeččem aț-țeswem yid-i di tgelda-inu. Aț-țeqqimem ɣef yikursiyen n lḥekma, aț-țḥekmem ɣef tnac leɛṛac n wat Isṛail.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:31">22:31</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna : A Semɛun sel-iyi-d ! Cciṭan yessuter a kkun-isserwet am yirden, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:32">22:32</a> lameɛna dɛiɣ ɣer Sidi Ṛebbi fell-ak akken ur tfeččleḍ ara di liman. Ma d kečč m'ara d-tuɣaleḍ ɣuṛ-i, sseǧhed atmaten-ik.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:33">22:33</a> Buṭrus yenna-yas : Aql-i heggaɣ iman-iw ad kecmeɣ yid-ek ɣer lḥebs, ad dduɣ yid-ek ula ɣer lmut.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:34">22:34</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : A k-d-iniɣ a Buṭrus , ass-a uqbel ad iskkuɛ uyaziḍ ad iyi-tnekṛeḍ tlata iberdan, aț-ținiḍ ur iyi-tessineḍ ara !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:35">22:35</a> Yenna-yasen daɣen : M'akken i kkun-ceggɛeɣ mbla idrimen, mbla agrab, mbla arkasen, yella kra i kkun-ixuṣṣen ? Rran-as : Ur aɣ-ixuṣṣ wacemma !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:36">22:36</a> Yenna-yasen : Ihi tura win yesɛan idrimen neɣ agrab yawi-ten, win ur nesɛi ara ajenwi ad izzenz abeṛnus-is iwakken a d-yaɣ yiwen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:37">22:37</a> Axaṭer qqaṛeɣ awen : Ilaq ad yedṛu yid-i wayen yuran. «  Ițțuneḥsab seg yembaṣiyen, » yerna ayen yuran fell-i, atan yewweḍ ed.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:38">22:38</a> Inelmaden-is nnan-as : A Sidi , atnan sin ijenwiyen ! Yenna-yasen : D ayen tura, beṛka !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:39">22:39</a> Akken yuɣ tannumi, Sidna Ɛisa yeffeɣ, iṛuḥ ɣer yiɣil n uzemmur ; inelmaden-is tebɛen-t. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:40">22:40</a> Mi gewweḍ ɣer wemkan-nni, yenna-yasen : Dɛut ɣer Ṛebbi akken ur tɣellim ara deg ujeṛṛeb.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:41">22:41</a> Dɣa yessebɛed iman-is fell-asen azal n kra n lmitrat, yeqqim ɣef tgecrar ideɛɛu i Ṛebbi yeqqaṛ :  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:42">22:42</a> A Baba, ma tebɣiḍ ssebɛed fell-i leɛtab-agi i yi-țṛaǧun ; lameɛna d lebɣi-k ara yedṛun mačči d lebɣi inu.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:43">22:43</a> Yiwen n lmelk n Sidi Ṛebbi iḍheṛ-as-d a t-yesseǧhed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:44">22:44</a> Iḍaq wul-is, ikețțeṛ di tẓallit armi tuɣal tidi-ines d idammen yețqiṭṭiren ɣer lqaɛa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:45">22:45</a> Mi gekfa, yuɣal-ed ɣer inelmaden-is, yufa-ten-id yewwi-ten yiḍes axaṭer yeɣli-d fell-asen leḥzen ameqqran ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:46">22:46</a> dɣa yenna-yasen : Acuɣeṛ i tegnem ? Kkret, dɛut ɣer Ṛebbi akken ur tɣellim ara deg ujeṛṛeb.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:47">22:47</a> Mazal-it iheddeṛ, atnaya wwḍen d lɣaci. Yudas, yiwen si tnac-nni inelmaden-is yezwar-ed zdat-sen, iqeṛṛeb ɣer Sidna Ɛisa ad isellem fell-as. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:48">22:48</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna yas : A Yudas, s sslam ara txedɛeḍ Mmi-s n bunadem !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:49">22:49</a> Wid yellan d Sidna Ɛisa, mi walan ayen ara yedṛun nnan-as : A Sidi, a newwet s ijenwiyen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:50">22:50</a> Yiwen deg-sen yewwet aqeddac n lmuqeddem ameqqran, igzem-as ameẓẓuɣ ayeffus. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:51">22:51</a> Sidna Ɛisa yenna yasen : ?ebset ! Dayen tura ! Yessers afus-is ɣef wemkan n umeẓẓuɣ n uqeddac-nni, yerra-yas-t akken yella. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:52">22:52</a> Dɣa yezzi ɣer wid i d-yusan a t-ḥebsen, ɣer lmuqedmin imeqqranen d lɛuqal akk-d lḥekkam n iɛessasen n lǧameɛ iqedsen yenna yasen : Tusam-d ɣuṛ-i s ijenwiyen d iɛekzan am akken d amakar i lliɣ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:53">22:53</a> Mkul ass țțiliɣ yid-wen di lǧameɛ iqedsen yiwen ur d-yerfid afus-is ɣuṛ-i. Lameɛna taswiɛt-agi ț-țaswiɛt nwen, ț-țaswiɛt n tezmert n ṭṭlam.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:54">22:54</a> Mi ṭṭfen Sidna Ɛisa, wwin-t ɣer wexxam n lmuqeddem ameqqran. Buṭrus itbeɛ-iten s lebɛid. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:55">22:55</a> Ceɛlen times di tlemmast n wefrag, qqimen. Buṭrus yella yid-sen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:56">22:56</a> Yiwet n tqeddact twala-t-id yeqqim yeẓẓiẓin, tmuqel-it tenna : Argaz-agi daɣen yella yid-es. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:57">22:57</a> Lameɛna Buṭrus yenkeṛ, yenna : Ur t-ssineɣ ara a tameṭṭut !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:58">22:58</a> Cwiṭ akka, iwala-t-id yiwen nniḍen, yenna : Kečč daɣen d yiwen seg-sen. Buṭrus yerra-yas, yenna : Ur lliɣ ara seg-sen ay argaz !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:59">22:59</a> Iɛedda wazal n ssaɛa, yenṭeq-ed yiwen nniḍen yenna : Mbla ccekk argaz-agi yella yid-es axaṭer d ajlili.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:60">22:60</a> Buṭrus yerra-yas : Ur ẓriɣ ara d acu i d-teqqaṛeḍ ay argaz ! Werɛad yekfi ameslay... yeskkuɛ uyaziḍ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:61">22:61</a> Sidna Ɛisa yezzi ɣuṛ-es, immuqel-it. Dɣa Buṭrus yemmekta-d wayen i s-d-yenna Sidna Ɛisa : « Ass-agi, uqbel ad iskkuɛ uyaziḍ ad iyi-tnekṛeḍ tlata iberdan.» </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:62">22:62</a> Yeffeɣ ɣer beṛṛa iṭṭerḍeq s imeṭṭawen axaṭer yendem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:63">22:63</a> Irgazen-nni i gɛussen Sidna Ɛisa, stehzayen fell-as kkaten-t.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:64">22:64</a> ?ɣummun-as udem-is, rnan qqaṛen-as « eɛqel ihi anwa i k-id yewten ». </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:65">22:65</a> Rnan regmen-t s mkul rregmat yellan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:66">22:66</a> Mi guli wass, tajmaɛt n lɛuqal n wegdud, lmuqedmin imeqqranen d lɛulama n ccariɛa nnejmaɛen. Wwin-d Sidna Ɛisa ɣer usqamu n ccṛeɛ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:67">22:67</a> Steqsan-t nnan-as : Ma d kečč i d Lmasiḥ, ini yaɣ t-id. Yerra-yasen : Atan ma nniɣ-awen-t-id ur iyi tețțamnem ara, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:68">22:68</a> ma steqsaɣ-kkun-id ur iyi-d-țarram ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:69">22:69</a> Lameɛna a wen-d-iniɣ, sya ɣer zdat,  Mmi-s n bunadem ad yeḥkem ɣer tama tayeffust n Sidi Ṛebbi Bab n tezmert.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:70">22:70</a> Kkren-d akken ma llan nnan : Ihi kečč d Mmi-s n Ṛebbi ? Nețța yerra-yasen : Tennam-t-id, d nekk !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:71">22:71</a> Imiren ɛeggḍen nnan : Dayen ur neḥwaǧ ara inigan, yenna-t-id s yimi-s, nesla-yas s imeẓẓuɣen-nneɣ.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:1">23:1</a> Tajmaɛt meṛṛa tekker, wwin Sidna Ɛisa ɣer lḥakem Bilaṭus. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:2">23:2</a> Bdan țcetkin fell-as, qqaṛen : -- Nufa argaz-agi yeskker ccwal ger lɣaci-nneɣ, yeqqaṛ-asen : « ur țxelliṣet ara leɣṛama i Qayṣer », yeqqaṛ daɣen : « d nețța i d Lmasiḥ, i d agellid ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:3">23:3</a> Bilaṭus isteqsa-t s imeslayen-agi : D kečč i d agellid n wat Isṛail ? Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : Tenniḍ-t-id.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:4">23:4</a> Bilaṭus yenna i lmuqedmin imeqqranen d lɣaci : Ur s-d-ssukkseɣ acemma i wergaz-agi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:5">23:5</a> Nutni țkemmilen qqaṛen : Yeskker ccwal ger lɣaci s wayen yesselmad ; yebda-d si tmurt n Jlili, yuɣal ɣer tmurt n Yahuda meṛṛa, tura yewweḍ-ed ɣer dagi. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:6">23:6</a> Bilaṭus, mi gesla bedren-d tamurt n Jlili, yesteqsa ɣef Sidna Ɛisa ma d ajlili i gella. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:7">23:7</a> Mi geẓra belli Sidna Ɛisa ajlili, n tmurt i ɣef yeḥkem Hiṛudus, iceggeɛ-as-t i Hiṛudus yellan ula d nețța di temdint n Lquds ussan-nni.  </p>
