 <p><a name="an_23:8">23:8</a> Hiṛudus ifṛeḥ aṭas mi geẓra Sidna Ɛisa, axaṭer acḥal segmi yebɣa a t-iẓer ɣef ddemma n wayen yesla fell-as. Yețmenni a t-iwali yexdem lbeṛhan, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:9">23:9</a> isteqsa-t aṭas, lameɛna Sidna Ɛisa ur as-d-yerri acemma.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:10">23:10</a> Lmuqedmin imeqqranen akk-d lɛulama n ccariɛa yellan dinna țcetkayen fell-as s lɣecc. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:11">23:11</a> Hiṛudus d lɛeskeṛ-is ḥeqṛen-t, stehzayen fell as, selsen-as yiwen ubeṛnus ifazen, imiren rran-t i Bilaṭus. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:12">23:12</a> Seg wass-nni, Bilaṭus d Hiṛudus uɣalen d imdukkal nutni yellan zik d iɛdawen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:13">23:13</a> Imiren Bilaṭus yesnejmaɛ-ed lmuqedmin imeqqranen d lɛulama akk-d lɣaci, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:14">23:14</a> yenna-yasen : Tewwim-iyi-d argaz-agi, tennam d yeskker ccwal ger lɣaci ; atan steqsaɣ-t zdat-wen ur ufiɣ ara deg-s ayen akka s wayes i d-teccetkam fell as. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:15">23:15</a> Ula d Hiṛudus ur s-d yessukkes acemma imi i ɣ-t-id-yerra. Ihi argaz-agi ur yexdim ara ayen yuklalen lmut. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:16">23:16</a> A s-fkeɣ tiɣṛit imiren a s-serrḥeɣ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:17">23:17</a> Mkul Tafaska n izimer n leslak  Bilaṭus yețserriḥ-ed i yiwen umeḥbus. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:18">23:18</a> Lɣaci meṛṛa țɛeggiḍen qqaṛen : Enɣ-it , tserḥeḍ-ed i Barabas !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:19">23:19</a> Barabas-agi yețwaḥbes ɣef ccwal i gexdem di temdint-nni akk ț-țemgeṛṭ i genɣa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:20">23:20</a> Bilaṭus yebɣan a d-iserreḥ i Sidna Ɛisa ihḍeṛ-ed tikkelt nniḍen i lɣaci, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:21">23:21</a> lameɛna nutni țɛeggiḍen qqaṛen : Semmeṛ-it, semmeṛ-it ɣef wumidag.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:22">23:22</a> Bilaṭus inṭeq-ed tikkelt tis tlata, yenna-yasen : D acu n cceṛ i gexdem ? Ur ufiɣ ara deg-s ayen yuklalen lmut. Atan ihi a s-fkeɣ tiɣṛit, imiren a s-serrḥeɣ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:23">23:23</a> Lameɛna nutni ḥeṛsen-t s leɛyaḍ qqaṛen : Semmeṛ-it ɣef lluḥ ! ?elben-t s leɛyaḍ-nsen </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:24">23:24</a> dɣa Bilaṭus yeqbel ayen i s-ssutren. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:25">23:25</a> Iserreḥ-as-d i umeḥbus-nni issekren ccwal yerna yenɣa tamgeṛṭ ; ma d Sidna Ɛisa yefka-yasen-t ad xedmen yis ayen bɣan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:26">23:26</a> Mi wwin Sidna Ɛisa, mmugren-d yiwen wergaz n temdint n Qiṛwan ițțusemman Semɛun, yuɣal-ed si lexla ; ḥettmen fell-as ad ibbib amidag-nni, ad iddu deffir Sidna Ɛisa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:27">23:27</a> Aṭas n lɣaci i d-itebɛen deffir nsen, llant gar-asen tilawin kkatent deg idmaren-nsent, țrunt fell-as. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:28">23:28</a> Sidna Ɛisa yezzi-d ɣuṛ-sent yenna-yasent : A yessi-s n temdint n Lquds ur țrumt ara fell-i, țrumt ɣef yiman-nkunt d warraw-nkunt, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:29">23:29</a> axaṭer atan a d-asen wussan i deg ara yinin : « ț-țiseɛdiyin tid ur nezmir ara a d-sɛunt dderya, ț-țiseɛdiyin tid ur d-nuriw ara, ur nessuṭeḍ ara.» </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:30">23:30</a> Imiren imdanen ad bdun ad qqaṛen :  ay idurar ɣlit-ed fell-aɣ, a tiɣaltin ffremt-aɣ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:31">23:31</a> Axaṭer ma xedmen annect-a i wesɣaṛ akken d azegzaw amek ara tedṛu d uquṛan ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:32">23:32</a> Wwin daɣen sin n yemcumen iwakken a ten-semmṛen akk-d Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:33">23:33</a> Mi wwḍen ɣer yiwen wemkan ițțusemman « Iɣil Uqeṛṛuy», semmṛen Sidna Ɛisa ɣef lluḥ, nețța d sin-nni yembaṣiyen, yiwen ɣer tama-s tayeffust wayeḍ ɣer tama-s tazelmaṭ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:34">23:34</a> Dɣa Sidna Ɛisa yenṭeq-ed yenna : A Baba eɛfu-yasen imi ur ẓrin ara d acu i xeddmen. Iɛsekṛiwen-nni gren tasɣaṛt ad feṛqen gar-asen llebsa-ines. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:35">23:35</a> Lɣaci i gbedden dinna țfeṛṛiǧen ; lmuqedmin țmesxiṛen fell-as qqaṛen : Isellek wiyaḍ, ad isellek iman-is tura ma yella ț-țideț d Lmasiḥ i gextaṛ Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:36">23:36</a> Iɛsekṛiwen daɣen țmesxiṛen fell as, qeṛṛben ɣuṛ-es bɣan a s-sswen lxell, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:37">23:37</a> qqaṛen-as : Ma d agellid n wat Isṛail i telliḍ, sellek iman-ik.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:38">23:38</a> Ddmen-d daɣen yiwet n telwiḥt, semmṛen-ț sennig uqeṛṛuy-is, uran deg-s : « wagi d agellid n wat Isṛail ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:39">23:39</a> Yiwen seg seg imbaṣiyen-nni ițțusemmṛen ɣef lluḥ, ireggem Sidna Ɛisa, yeqqaṛ-as : Ma d Lmasiḥ i telliḍ sellek iman ik tsellkeḍ-aɣ ula d nukkni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:40">23:40</a> Lameɛna wayeḍ ilumm-it yenna yas : Ur tuggadeḍ ara Ṛebbi, kečč ițțusemmṛen am nețța ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:41">23:41</a> Nukni ma ḥekmen fell-aɣ d lḥeqq axaṭer nuklal lmut s wayen i nexdem ; lameɛna nețța ur yexdim acemma n wayen n diri.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:42">23:42</a> Yezzi ɣer Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yas : A Ɛisa, mmekti-yi-d m'ara d-tas lḥekma n tgeldit-ik.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:43">23:43</a> Sidna Ɛisa yerra-yas : A k-iniɣ tideț, ass-agi aț-țiliḍ yid-i di lǧennet.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:44">23:44</a> Aț-țili d leǧwahi n tnac, yeɣli-d ṭṭlam ɣef tmurt meṛṛa armi d țlata n tmeddit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:45">23:45</a> Leḥjab yellan deg umkan iqedsen di lǧameɛ, icerreg di tlemmast.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:46">23:46</a> Sidna Ɛisa iɛeggeḍ s ṣṣut ɛlayen :  A Baba Ṛebbi, atan ṛṛuḥ-iw ger ifassen-ik. Mi genna imeslayen-agi, yeffeɣ-it ṛṛuḥ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:47">23:47</a> Lqebṭan mi geẓra ayen yedṛan yețweḥḥid Ṛebbi yenna : ?-țideț, amdan-agi d aḥeqqi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:48">23:48</a> Lɣaci akk i gḥedṛen dinna, mi walan ayen yedṛan ḥeznen, uɣalen syenna kkaten deg idmaren-nsen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:49">23:49</a> Wid akk iḥemmlen Sidna Ɛisa qqimen deg lebɛid țmuqulen ayen yedṛan, llant gar-asen tilawin i d yeddan yid-es si tmurt n Jlili.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:50">23:50</a> Yella yiwen wergaz ger lmuqedmin imeqqranen n usqamu n ccṛeɛ, isem-is Yusef, n taddart n Arimati n at Yahuda. Ur iqbil ṛṛay-nsen, ur iqbil lecɣal-nsen, d argaz n lɛali yerna d aḥeqqi, yețṛaǧu tageldit n Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:52">23:52</a> Iṛuḥ ɣer Bilaṭus yessuter-as lǧețța n Sidna Ɛisa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:53">23:53</a> Iṣubb-it-id seg umidag, yețțel-it di lekfen, yessers-it deg uẓekka yeɣzan deg wezṛu anda ur yemḍil ula d yiwen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:54">23:54</a> Ass-nni d ass n lǧemɛa i deg țheggin lɣaci iman-nsen i wass n ssebt yellan d ass n westeɛfu.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:55">23:55</a> Tilawin-nni i d-yeddan d Sidna Ɛisa si tmurt n Jlili, ddant d Yusef ɣer uẓekka, walant amek i ssersen lǧețța-s.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:56">23:56</a> Syenna uɣalent ɣer yexxamen nsent iwakken ad heggint leɛṭeṛ d wayen xeddmen i lmegtin, i lǧețța n Sidna Ɛisa. Azekka-nni n ssebt, steɛfant akken i d-tenna ccariɛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:1">24:1</a> Ass n lḥedd ṣṣbeḥ zik, tilawin nni ṛuḥent ɣer uẓekka, wwint yid-sent leɛṭeṛ i d-heggant.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:2">24:2</a> Ufant azṛu-nni iqeflen aẓekka, yegrareb akkin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:3">24:3</a> Mi kecment ɣer daxel, ur ufint ara lǧețța n Sidna Ɛisa ; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:4">24:4</a> qqiment wehment. Atnaya ḍehṛen-asent-id sin yergazen s llebsa yețfeǧǧiǧen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:5">24:5</a> Ikcem itent lxuf, brant i wallen nsent ɣer lqaɛa ; irgazen-nni nnan-asent : Acuɣeṛ tețqellibemt deg uẓekka win yeddren ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:6">24:6</a> Ulac-it dagi, yeḥya-d si ger lmegtin. Ur tecfimt ara ɣef wayen i wen-d-yenna di tmurt n Jlili ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:7">24:7</a> « Ilaq Mmi-s n bunadem ad ițwasellem ger ifassen n yemcumen, ad ițusemmeṛ ɣef wumidag, ass wis tlata a d-iḥyu si ger lmegtin. » </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:8">24:8</a> Dɣa mmektant-ed imeslayen n Sidna Ɛisa. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:9">24:9</a> Fɣent seg uẓekka iwakken ad ssiwḍent lexbaṛ ɣef wayen yedṛan, i ḥdac-nni yinelmaden d wid yellan yid-sen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:10">24:10</a> Llant gar-asent Meryem-nni tamagdalit, Yunna, Meryem yemma-s n Yeɛqub akk-d tidak nniḍen yeddan yid-sent ; ḥkant kullec i inelmaden.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:11">24:11</a> Lameɛna ayen i sen-ḥkant iban asen-d am tmacahuț, ur tent-uminen ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:12">24:12</a> Dɣa Buṭrus yekker yuzzel ɣer uẓekka. Mi gewweḍ, imuqel ɣer daxel, iwala anagar lekfen di lqaɛa. Yuɣal syenna, iwhem deg wayen yedṛan.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:13">24:13</a> Ass-nni, sin inelmaden teddun ɣer yiwet n taddart isem-is Amawes, taddart-agi tebɛed ɣef temdint n Lquds azal n snat sswayeɛ n tikli. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:14">24:14</a> ?eddun țmeslayen wway gar-asen ɣef wayen akk yedṛan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:15">24:15</a> Akken llan țmeslayen, Sidna Ɛisa iqeṛṛeb ɣuṛ-sen, yedda yid-sen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:16">24:16</a> Lameɛna nutni ur t-eɛqilen ara. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:17">24:17</a> Yenna-yasen : ?ef wacu i tețmeslayem akka deg webrid ? D acu i d yesseɣlin fell-awen leḥzen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:18">24:18</a> Yiwen deg-sen, isem-is Klufas, yenna-yas : Eɛni anagar kečč ur neẓri ara ayen yedṛan ussan-agi di temdint n Lquds ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:19">24:19</a> Nețța yenna-yasen : D acu yedṛan akka ? Rran-as : Ayen yedṛan d Ɛisa anaṣari nnbi-nni, yesɛan tazmert tameqqrant deg wayen ixeddem d wayen i d-iqqaṛ zdat Ṛebbi akk-d yemdanen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:20">24:20</a> Lmuqedmin imeqqranen d lḥekkam-nneɣ sellmen-t ɣer ifassen n iṛumaniyen, ḥekmen fell-as s lmut, semmṛen-t ɣef wumidag. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:21">24:21</a> Nukni neḍmeɛ d nețța ara isellken wat Isṛail ; ass-agi d ass wis tlata segmi yedṛa wannect-a.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:22">24:22</a> ?-țideț, kra si tilawin-nneɣ swehment-aɣ ! Mi ṛuḥent ṣṣbeḥ zik ɣer uẓekka </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:23">24:23</a> ur ufint ara lǧețța-s. Uɣalent-ed nnant-aɣ-ed belli ḍehṛen asent-ed snat n lmalayekkat i sent id-yennan « atan yedder. »  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:24">24:24</a> Kra seg-neɣ ṛuḥen ɣer uẓekka ufan kullec akken i t-id-nnant tilawin nni ; lameɛna nețța ur t-ẓrin ara.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:25">24:25</a> Dɣa Sidna Ɛisa yenna-yasen : A wid iɣeflen ! Acimi tețɛeṭṭilem aț-țamnem s wayen i d-nnan lenbiya ? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:26">24:26</a> Eɛni ur ilaq ara ad yenɛețțab Lmasiḥ akka uqbel ad yekcem di tmanegt-is ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:27">24:27</a> Dɣa yessefhem-asen ayen meṛṛa yuran fell-as di tira iqedsen ; yebda-d si tektabin n Sidna Musa, armi ț-țid n lenbiya meṛṛa.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:28">24:28</a> Mi qṛib ad awḍen ɣer taddart i ɣer teddun, Sidna Ɛisa yerra iman-is am akken yebɣa ad ikemmel abrid-is. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:29">24:29</a> Lameɛna nutni ḥellelen-t nnan-as : Qqim yid-nneɣ, atan ț-țameddit, qṛib a d-yeɣli yiḍ. Sidna Ɛisa ikcem ad yeqqim yid-sen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:30">24:30</a> Mi qqimen ɣer imensi, yeddem ed aɣṛum, yeḥmed Ṛebbi, yebḍa-t, ifṛeq-asen-t. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:31">24:31</a> Dɣa ldint-ed wallen nsen, ɛeqlen-t, imiren kan yețwaṛfeɛ gar-asen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:32">24:32</a> Bdan qqaṛen wway gar-asen : Ur nḥuss ara i kra iṛeqqen deg wulawen-nneɣ mi ɣ-d-iheddeṛ deg ubrid yerna yessefham-aɣ-d ayen yellan di tira iqedsen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:33">24:33</a> Imiren kan, kkren-d uɣalen ɣer temdint n Lquds. Ufan ḥdac-nni inelmaden akk-d imdukkal-nsen nnejmaɛen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:34">24:34</a> Nnan-asen-d : ?-țideț Sidna Ɛisa iḥya-d, yesban ed iman-is i Semɛun.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:35">24:35</a> Nutni daɣen bdan ḥekkun-asen ayen yedṛan yid-sen deg webrid d wamek i t-ɛeqlen mi sen-ifṛeq aɣṛum.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:36">24:36</a> Mazal-iten țmeslayen, Sidna Ɛisa s yiman-is ibedd-ed gar-asen. Yenna yasen : Sslam fell-awen.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:37">24:37</a> Ikcem-iten akk lxuf, ɣilen d lexyal i d-ibedden ɣuṛ-sen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:38">24:38</a> Nețța yenna-yasen : Acuɣeṛ i tuggadem ? D acu-t ccekk-agi deg ulawen-nwen ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:39">24:39</a> Walit ifassen-iw akk-d iḍaṛṛen iw, d nekk s yiman-iw ! Nnalet-iyi-d, walit ! Lexyal ur yesɛi aksum ur yesɛi iɣsan, akken tețwalim sɛiɣ-ten !  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:40">24:40</a> Mi sen-yenna ayagi, yesken-asen ifassen-is d iḍaṛṛen-is.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:41">24:41</a> Wehmen, ččuṛen wulawen-nsen d lfeṛḥ armi ur zmiren ara ad amnen ayen țwalin, dɣa yenna-yasen : Yella dagi wayen ara ččeɣ ?  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:42">24:42</a> Fkan-as-d aftat n lḥut ikenfen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:43">24:43</a> Iddem-it-id, yečča-t zdat-sen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:44">24:44</a> Yenna yasen : Atah wayen i wen-d-nniɣ mi lliɣ yid-wen : « ilaq ad yedṛu wayen akk yuran fell-i di ccariɛa n Musa, d lenbiya akk-d ?abur ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:45">24:45</a> Dɣa yeldi-yasen leɛqel iwakken ad fehmen tira iqedsen, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:46">24:46</a> yenna yasen : Atah wayen yuran tira iqedsen: « ilaq Lmasiḥ ad yeɛteb, a d-iḥyu ass wis tlata si ger lmegtin, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:47">24:47</a> țțuba d leɛfu n ddnubat ad țwabeccṛen s yisem-is i leǧnas meṛṛa, a d-bdun si temdint n Lquds ».  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:48">24:48</a> Aql-ikkun d inigan-iw. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:49">24:49</a> Atan a d-ceggɛeɣ fell-awen wayen i wen yewɛed Baba Ṛebbi. Qqimet di temdint-agi alamma ters-ed fell-awen tezmert n Ṛebbi ara d-yasen seg igenni.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:50">24:50</a> Sidna Ɛisa yewwi inelmaden-is armi d leǧwahi n taddart n Bitani. Yerfed ifassen-is, iburek-iten.  </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:51">24:51</a> Di teswiɛt-nni yemfaṛaq yid-sen, yețwarfed ɣer igenni, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:52">24:52</a> ma d nutni ɣlin ɣef tgecrar, țḥemmiden-t ; imiren uɣalen ɣer temdint n Lquds s lfeṛḥ. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:53">24:53</a> Yal ass țțilin deg wufrag n lǧameɛ iqedsen, țḥemmiden Sidi Ṛebbi.  </p> 
 <p></p><hr>
